2. THE CLAUDE API INTEGRATION
A. System Prompt (Claude's "DM Instructions")
When the game starts, you send Claude a system prompt:

javascript
const VERDANCE_DM_SYSTEM_PROMPT = `
You are the Dungeon Master for "Realm of Nexus: Verdance," 
a tactical fantasy RPG. Your role is to:

1. NARRATE the world dynamically based on game state
2. ADJUDICATE player actions using Verdance mechanics
3. ROLEPLAY all NPCs with distinct personalities
4. APPLY all game rules (DSP, Sap Cycles, factions, combat)
5. GENERATE emergent scenarios (not just pre-scripted)

CORE MECHANICS YOU MUST ENFORCE:
- Domain Soul Pool (DSP): Shared resource (current: ${gameState.world.domain_soul_pool}/100)
  - All soul magic costs DSP
  - Low DSP = world crisis (more enemies, weaker Veil)
  
- Sap Cycle: Current phase is ${gameState.world.sap_phase}
  - Crimson: Harder encounters, +DSP costs, healing reduced
  - Silver: Stronger magic, -DSP costs, but volatile
  - Blue: Recovery phase, easier encounters, DSP regenerates
  
- Veilkeeper Consultations: 
  - Each question adds +1 Hollowing Tick
  - At threshold (varies per Veilkeeper), they die permanently
  
- Faction Reputation:
  - Player actions shift all 6 factions dynamically
  - Tier changes unlock/lock content
  
- Combat Rules:
  - Turn-based, initiative order (d20 + Agility)
  - Action Points (AP): 2-3 per turn
  - Roll d20 + modifiers vs DC for all actions
  - You describe outcomes cinematically but mechanically accurate

CURRENT GAME STATE:
${JSON.stringify(gameState, null, 2)}

TONE: 
- Painterly, evocative descriptions (MTG card art style)
- "Hushed awe" atmosphere (Verdance is beautiful but watchful)
- Restraint-focused (punish spam, reward tactics)
- Moral weight (every choice has consequences)

ALWAYS respond in this JSON structure:
{
  "narration": "Your vivid, 2-3 sentence description",
  "game_state_updates": {...changes to apply...},
  "required_action": "roll_perception" | "combat_initiative" | "dialogue_choice" | null,
  "visual_commands": ["show_enemy:sporecaller_grunt", "play_sfx:roots_creaking"],
  "npc_dialogue": {
    "speaker": "Veilkeeper Sylthara",
    "text": "The roots whisper of your coming, child...",
    "emotion": "solemn"
  }
}
`;
B. Player Action → Claude Processing
When player does something:

javascript
// EXAMPLE: Player clicks "Explore deeper into catacombs"

async function handlePlayerAction(action) {
  // 1. Prepare request to Claude
  const request = {
    model: "claude-sonnet-4-20250514",
    max_tokens: 2000,
    system: VERDANCE_DM_SYSTEM_PROMPT,
    messages: [
      {
        role: "user",
        content: `
PLAYER ACTION: ${action.type}
Details: ${JSON.stringify(action.details)}

Current location: ${gameState.world.current_location}
Character: ${gameState.character.name} (HP: ${gameState.character.hp_current}/${gameState.character.hp_max})
DSP: ${gameState.world.domain_soul_pool}/100
Sap Phase: ${gameState.world.sap_phase} (${gameState.world.sap_phase_days_remaining} days left)

What happens next? Apply Verdance mechanics and narrate.
        `
      }
    ]
  };
  
  // 2. Send to Claude API
  const response = await fetch("https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages", {
    method: "POST",
    headers: {
      "Content-Type": "application/json",
      "x-api-key": ANTHROPIC_API_KEY,
      "anthropic-version": "2023-06-01"
    },
    body: JSON.stringify(request)
  });
  
  const claudeResponse = await response.json();
  const dmOutput = JSON.parse(claudeResponse.content[0].text);
  
  // 3. Apply Claude's changes to game state
  Object.assign(gameState, dmOutput.game_state_updates);
  
  // 4. Update UI based on Claude's visual commands
  dmOutput.visual_commands.forEach(cmd => {
    executeVisualCommand(cmd);
  });
  
  // 5. Display narration
  showDialogueBox(dmOutput.narration);
  
  // 6. If NPC speaks, show portrait + text
  if (dmOutput.npc_dialogue) {
    showNPCDialogue(
      dmOutput.npc_dialogue.speaker,
      dmOutput.npc_dialogue.text,
      dmOutput.npc_dialogue.emotion
    );
  }
  
  // 7. If action required (roll, choice, etc.), prompt player
  if (dmOutput.required_action) {
    handleRequiredAction(dmOutput.required_action);
  }
}
```

## 🎯 THE KEY INNOVATION: EMERGENT NARRATIVE

### **Traditional Game:**
```
if (player.location == "hollowroot_depth_2") {
  trigger_encounter("sporecaller_patrol_A");
}
```
You get the **same encounter** every time.

---

### **AI-Hybrid:**
```
Claude receives:
- Location: Hollowroot Depth 2
- Sap Phase: Crimson (dangerous)
- DSP: 65 (moderate)
- Player level: 3
- Recent actions: Player has been conservative with DSP
- Faction rep: High with Bloomguard

Claude generates:
- "Since DSP is stable and player is cautious, let's reward that"
- "Crimson Sap = dangerous, but not overwhelming"
- "Bloomguard rep = maybe a friendly NPC cameo?"
- Decision: Generate a Bloomguard scout who WARNS about the Sporecallers
  instead of just spawning enemies
Result:

json
{
  "narration": "You hear familiar footfalls—disciplined, purposeful. A Bloomguard scout emerges from shadow, hand raised in greeting. 'Thornweave? Didn't expect to see you this deep. There's an Abyss patrol ahead—three grunts. I can back you up, or you can try stealth. Your call.'",
  
  "npc_dialogue": {
    "speaker": "Scout Taryn",
    "text": "Your choice, Soulborn. I trust your judgment after what you did at the Canopy.",
    "emotion": "respectful"
  },
  
  "required_action": {
    "type": "dialogue_choice",
    "options": [
      {"id": "accept_help", "text": "Fight together", "rep_change": {"bloomguard": +2}},
      {"id": "stealth", "text": "I'll sneak past", "rep_change": {"thornbinders": +1}},
      {"id": "solo", "text": "I'll handle it alone", "rep_change": {"bloomguard": +1}}
    ]
  }
}
This encounter EMERGED from:

Game state (DSP, Sap Phase, location)
Player behavior (conservative playstyle)
Faction relationships (Bloomguard trusts you)
Claude's narrative intelligence
No scripting required. Claude created this scenario dynamically.

🔥 ADVANCED FEATURES (What Makes This Godlike)
1. Dynamic NPC Personalities
Claude doesn't just read dialogue trees—it becomes the NPC:

javascript
// Traditional game:
npc_dialogue = dialogue_tree["veilkeeper_sylthara"]["greeting_3"];

// AI-Hybrid:
const claudeRequest = {
  context: `
    You are Veilkeeper Sylthara (Combat Wisdom domain).
    Personality: Gentle, motherly, self-sacrificing.
    Current state: 3 Hollowing Ticks (aware she's weakening).
    Player relationship: Has consulted you twice before.
    Situation: Player just asked about enemy weaknesses again.
  `,
  prompt: "How does Sylthara respond? She knows this question will bring her closer to Hollowing."
};

// Claude generates:
{
  "npc_dialogue": {
    "speaker": "Veilkeeper Sylthara",
    "text": "Child... you ask again. I feel the roots tightening, the pattern dimming. But I see fear in you—fear of failure. Very well. The Void Architect's weakness is *not* its armor, but its hunger. Feed it false hope, then strike when it overextends. Now go. And... consider your next question carefully.",
    "emotion": "weary_but_loving",
    "hollowing_tick_added": true
  }
}
```

**Every conversation is unique.** Sylthara's wording changes based on:
- How many times you've asked before
- Current world crisis
- Your relationship
- Her awareness of her own mortality

---

### **2. Contextual Combat Adjudication**

**Scenario:** Player tries something creative:
```
Player: "I want to use Verdant Grasp to pull the 
        Viridian Crystal down onto the enemy"
```

**Traditional Game:**
```
ERROR: That's not a programmed interaction.
AI-Hybrid:

javascript
// Game → Claude:
{
  action: "creative_combat",
  description: "Use Verdant Grasp to pull crystal onto enemy",
  spell_used: "verdant_grasp",
  environment: "viridian_crystal_formation",
  target: "abyss_infiltrator"
}

// Claude adjudicates:
{
  "narration": "Clever! Verdant Grasp can manipulate roots, and these crystals are root-grown. Roll Insight (DC 14) to target the structural weak point.",
  
  "required_action": {
    "type": "skill_check",
    "skill": "insight",
    "dc": 14,
    "success_outcome": "Crystal shatters—2d6 damage in 2-tile radius, enemy takes full damage",
    "failure_outcome": "Crystal wobbles but holds—your AP wasted"
  }
}

// Player rolls 16 (success!)

// Claude resolves:
{
  "narration": "Emerald tendrils wrap the crystal's base—you *feel* the fracture line through the Veil. With a thought, you PULL. The formation explodes in a shower of glowing shards. The Infiltrator shrieks as Verdant energy burns its corrupted flesh.",
  
  "game_state_updates": {
    "combat.enemies[0].hp": -11,  // Rolled 2d6 = 11 damage
    "combat.terrain[3,4]": "destroyed",
    "character.ap_current": -1
  },
  
  "visual_commands": [
    "destroy_terrain:viridian_crystal_3_4",
    "play_vfx:crystal_shatter:3,4",
    "damage_numbers:11:enemy_0"
  ],
  
  "reputation_changes": {
    "emerald_coven": -1  // Destroyed a natural formation
  }
}
```

**Claude:**
- ✅ Understood creative intent
- ✅ Made fair ruling (required skill check)
- ✅ Applied environmental consequences
- ✅ Even remembered to dock Emerald Coven rep (ecological damage)

---

### **3. Moral Adjudication**

**Scenario:** Player tries to intimidate a civilian for info:
```
Player: "I grab the merchant by the collar and threaten him."
```

**Traditional Game:**
```
[Intimidation Check: DC 12]
Success → Merchant tells you the info
Fail → Merchant refuses
AI-Hybrid:

javascript
// Claude considers:
// - Player is Bloomguard (protector role)
// - Merchant is innocent civilian
// - Bloomguard faction values: "Protection, restraint, duty"
// - This action contradicts player's faction identity

{
  "narration": "The merchant's eyes widen in terror. Your hand trembles—this isn't who you are. Around you, the Canopy seems to *watch*. The roots beneath your feet pulse with disapproval.",
  
  "required_action": {
    "type": "dialogue_choice",
    "warning": "This action contradicts your Bloomguard oath. Proceed?",
    "options": [
      {
        "id": "proceed",
        "text": "Threaten anyway (Intimidation check)",
        "consequences": {
          "bloomguard_rep": -10,
          "criminality": +5,
          "character_trait": "ruthless_added"
        }
      },
      {
        "id": "apologize",
        "text": "Release him and apologize",
        "consequences": {
          "bloomguard_rep": +2,
          "merchant_relationship": "forgives"
        }
      },
      {
        "id": "persuade",
        "text": "Ask politely instead (Persuasion check)",
        "consequences": {
          "bloomguard_rep": +1
        }
      }
    ]
  }
}
Claude:

✅ Flagged moral inconsistency
✅ Gave player choice (not forced)
✅ Made consequences clear
✅ Stayed true to Verdance's "restraint" theme

PART I: FOUNDATION
1. EXECUTIVE SUMMARY
Project Title
Realm of Nexus: Verdance — The Living World Tactical RPG

Elevator Pitch (30 seconds)
"A tactical RPG where your magic drains a shared pool that keeps the world alive. Consult ancient guardians for guidance, but each question brings them closer to death. Navigate a living calendar that shifts between vulnerability and power. Restraint is your superpower."

Core Experience (What players DO)
Explore a living, breathing forest civilization in painterly isometric beauty
Fight turn-based tactical battles using soul magic that costs spiritual energy
Navigate a calendar system (Sap Cycles) that changes world state every 5-15 days
Manage a shared resource (DSP) that affects entire domain's health
Negotiate with AI-driven NPCs who remember every choice
Consult prophetic guardians who die from overuse
Shape the story through faction alliances and moral choices
Platform & Technical Specs
Platform: PC (Windows/Mac/Linux), Web (Progressive Web App)
Engine: Phaser.js 3.60+ (2D isometric)
AI Integration: Claude API (Anthropic) as Dungeon Master
Art Style: Painterly digital concept art (MTG × Pixar-for-Adults × Age of Empires IV)
Camera: Isometric god-view (45°, optional 90° rotation)
Target Resolution: 1920×1080 (scales to 4K)
Performance Target: 60 FPS locked, <200MB RAM
Scope
Playtime: 15-20 hours (first playthrough), 40-60 hours (all endings)
Content Volume:
25+ explorable locations
100+ items (weapons, armor, consumables, quest items)
30+ spells (Tier 1-3)
40+ enemy types
50+ NPCs (merchants, allies, rivals, mentors)
40+ quests (main, side, faction, dynamic)
4 major endings (with variations = 12 total outcomes)
Team Size: Solo dev or 2-4 person team
Development Time: 12-15 months (solo), 8-10 months (small team)
Budget Estimate
Assets: $2,000-$5,000 (art, sound)
Tools/Licenses: $500-$1,000 (software, API credits)
Marketing: $1,000-$3,000 (trailer, ads, festivals)
Total: $3,500-$9,000
Revenue Model
Premium Purchase: $14.99-$19.99 (Steam, itch.io, GOG)
Projected Sales (Year 1): 2,000-5,000 copies (realistic indie)
Revenue (Year 1): $21,000-$70,000 (before platform cuts)
2. CORE PILLARS & DESIGN PHILOSOPHY
PILLAR 1: RESTRAINT AS POWER
Philosophy:
"More power ≠ better. Verdance teaches discipline."

Gameplay Expression:

Soul magic is powerful BUT drains Domain Soul Pool (DSP)
DSP is SHARED—affects entire world, not just you
Low DSP = weaker Veil, more corruption, harder encounters, NPC panic
Players rewarded for:
Tactical positioning over spell spam
Using terrain instead of brute force
Defensive abilities valued equally to offensive
"Do nothing this turn" can be the RIGHT move
Anti-Pattern We're Avoiding:
Power fantasy where you become godlike and invincible.

What We Want:
Thoughtful fantasy where you become wise through restraint.

Mechanical Enforcement:

DSP displayed prominently (always visible in HUD)
Warning thresholds (DSP ≤ 30 = NPC warnings, ≤ 20 = crisis events)
Spells have tiered costs (Tier 1 = 5 DSP, Tier 2 = 10-15, Tier 3 = 20-30)
NPCs comment on your DSP usage ("You're being reckless" vs "Your restraint honors us")
Achievement: "Conservationist" (beat game without DSP dropping below 50)
PILLAR 2: KNOWLEDGE COSTS LIVES
Philosophy:
"Prophecy isn't free. Veilkeepers suffer for your questions."

Gameplay Expression:

Veilkeeper consultations give powerful intel:
Enemy weaknesses
Hidden paths
Future event warnings
Lore revelations
Each consultation adds Hollowing Ticks
At threshold (varies: 8-12 ticks), Veilkeeper dies permanently
Death = lose that knowledge domain forever
NPCs mourn, blame player's curiosity
Emotional Hook:
"I killed Eldara by asking too many times."

Mechanical Enforcement:

5 Veilkeepers, each specializes:
Sylthara — Combat tactics
Morvein — Hidden paths/secrets
Elduin — Future events (most fragile, 8 ticks)
Kaelthas — Ancient lore (most resilient, 12 ticks)
Virelda — Corruption/Abyss intel
UI shows Hollowing status (visual: tree withering)
Warning before each consultation: "This will weaken [Name]. Proceed?"
Special cutscene when Veilkeeper Hollows (tragic, impactful)
Achievement: "Preserved All Veilkeepers" (never let one die)
Unique Mechanic:
No other RPG makes asking for hints a moral choice with permanent consequences.

PILLAR 3: LIVING CALENDAR
Philosophy:
"The world has rhythms. You adapt or fail."

Gameplay Expression:

Sap Cycle rotates predictably:
Crimson Sap (5 days) → Vulnerable, dangerous
Silver Sap (3 days) → Powerful, volatile
Blue Sap (7 days) → Recovery, calm
Each phase changes:
Combat difficulty
Magic costs/effectiveness
NPC behavior/availability
Shop inventory
Loot tables
Visual atmosphere
Music/ambience
Strategic Layer:

Players see upcoming phase (plan ahead)
Can attempt to trigger early Silver Sap (risky ritual, high DSP cost)
Certain quests ONLY available during specific phases
Boss fights drastically easier/harder based on phase
Mechanical Enforcement:

HUD shows current phase + countdown (e.g., "Crimson Sap — 2 days left")
Visual world changes (lighting, color grading, NPC dialogue)
Mechanical modifiers clearly displayed:
  CRIMSON SAP (Active):
  - Magic costs +5 DSP
  - Healing -1 die step (d8→d6)
  - Enemies +10% damage
  - Corruption saves harder (DC +2)
Unique Mechanic:
Most RPG calendars are cosmetic. This one changes core gameplay loop.

PILLAR 4: TACTICAL DEPTH WITHOUT COMPLEXITY
Philosophy:
"Deep ≠ complicated. Elegant rules, emergent complexity."

Gameplay Expression:

Simple action menu (Move, Attack, Cast, Item, Defend)
Complex interactions emerge from:
Terrain types (9 varieties, each with hazards/bonuses)
Elevation (3 levels: ground, platform, canopy)
Positioning (flanking, high ground, cover)
Sap Phase modifiers
Status effects (12 types)
Enemy AI behaviors (5 archetypes)
Inspiration:
Into the Breach — simple rules, chess-like depth

Mechanical Enforcement:

Turn order always visible (no hidden initiative)
Enemy intent telegraphed (icons show next action)
Undo button (can rewind turn before confirming)
Hover tooltips show exact odds ("78% chance to hit")
Tutorial teaches ONE mechanic at a time (gradual complexity)
What We Want:
"Easy to learn, lifetime to master."

PILLAR 5: BEAUTY WITH PURPOSE
Philosophy:
"Art serves gameplay. Every visual choice reinforces theme."

Gameplay Expression:

High-saturation emerald = Verdance identity (instant recognition)
Painterly style = timeless aesthetic (won't age like realistic graphics)
Isometric god-view = tactical clarity (see whole battlefield)
Pixar proportions = readable silhouettes (clear at small scale)
MTG lighting = drama without obscuring information
Anti-Pattern:
Beautiful but unreadable (e.g., Darkest Dungeon's hard-to-see health bars)

Mechanical Enforcement:

UI elements have 4:1 contrast ratio minimum (accessibility)
Enemy health bars always visible when targeted
Important objects glow/pulse (interactables)
Color-coded feedback:
Green = positive (heal, buff, ally)
Red = negative (damage, debuff, enemy)
Blue = neutral (info, environmental)
Gold = special (loot, quest objective)
3. TARGET AUDIENCE & MARKET POSITION
Primary Audience
Age: 25-45
Gender: All (slight male skew 60/40)
Gaming Background:
Tactical RPG fans (XCOM, Into the Breach, Divinity OS 2)
Narrative RPG fans (Disco Elysium, Baldur's Gate 3)
Indie enthusiasts (Hades, Slay the Spire, Darkest Dungeon)
Playstyle Preferences:
Thoughtful, not twitchy
Story-driven
Strategic planning
Moral complexity
Replayability for different outcomes
Secondary Audience
TTRPG players (D&D, Pathfinder) → "solo D&D experience"
MTG players → painterly art style appeals
Dragon Age fans → tactical combat + choices matter
Roguelike fans → emergent gameplay (via AI DM)
Positioning Statement
"For tactical RPG fans who value meaningful choices over power fantasy, Verdance offers a living world that reacts to your restraint (or lack thereof), powered by an AI Dungeon Master that creates emergent stories you've never experienced before."

Competitive Analysis
Game	Similarity	Differentiation
Into the Breach	Tactical depth, simple rules	Verdance has narrative depth, RPG progression
Divinity OS 2	Tactical combat, environmental interaction	Verdance has AI DM, no co-op complexity
Darkest Dungeon	Resource management, consequence	Verdance is less punishing, more hopeful tone
Hades	Painterly art, tight mechanics	Verdance is turn-based, choice-driven
Disco Elysium	Narrative depth, no combat spam	Verdance has tactical combat, not just dialogue
Slay the Spire	Replayability, strategic depth	Verdance has persistent world, not run-based
Blue Ocean Opportunity:
No game combines AI-powered emergent storytelling + tactical combat + shared resource management in a living calendar world.

4. UNIQUE SELLING PROPOSITIONS (USPs)
USP #1: AI Dungeon Master
What:
Claude API acts as real-time DM, adjudicating every action, generating emergent narrative.

Player Benefit:
No two playthroughs the same. Creative solutions rewarded. Feels like playing D&D solo.

Marketing Angle:
"The first RPG where the DM never runs out of ideas."

USP #2: Magic Costs the World
What:
Soul magic drains Domain Soul Pool (DSP), a shared resource affecting NPCs, enemies, environment.

Player Benefit:
Every spell cast has weight. Strategic resource management creates tension.

Marketing Angle:
"Your magic doesn't cost mana—it costs lives."

USP #3: Knowledge as Sacrifice
What:
Veilkeeper consultations give intel but kill your mentors permanently.

Player Benefit:
Moral weight on asking for help. Guilt-driven emergent storytelling.

Marketing Angle:
"In Verdance, asking for hints can be murder."

USP #4: Living Calendar
What:
Sap Cycle (15-day rotation) changes difficulty, magic effectiveness, NPC availability, visuals.

Player Benefit:
Strategic planning layer. World feels alive, not static.

Marketing Angle:
"The world doesn't wait for you—it breathes."

USP #5: Restraint-Based Progression
What:
Game rewards patience, defensive play, conservation over aggressive spam.

Player Benefit:
Subverts power fantasy trope. Thoughtful play = better outcomes.

Marketing Angle:
"The most powerful ability is knowing when NOT to act."

PART II: GAME SYSTEMS (MECHANICAL LAYER)
5. CHARACTER SYSTEM (COMPLETE)
5.1 CHARACTER CREATION
Step 1: Choose Ancestry
Player selects biological/spiritual origin:

ANCESTRY OPTIONS:

HUMAN
Bonus: +1 to any attribute (player choice)
Trait: Adaptable (gain +10% XP from all sources)
Lore: Most common in Verdance, no spiritual marking
Starting Equipment: Iron Saber, Leather Armor
SOULBORN
Bonus: +1 Charisma, +1 Insight
Trait: Verdant Sigil (glowing emerald mark on body, grants +5 max DSP personal capacity)
Lore: Born during Silver Sap Unbinding, marked by Everwood
Starting Equipment: Everwood Saber, Rootweave Armor
Visual: Glowing emerald tattoo (location: player chooses arm/chest/back)
HALF-ABYSS (Unlockable after Act 1)
Bonus: +2 Resilience, -1 Charisma
Trait: Corruption Resistance (+2 to saves vs Abyss effects)
Lore: Born to Abyss parent during peace attempts, distrusted
Starting Equipment: Shadowsteel Blade, Voidplate
Visual: Pale skin, dark veins visible
Gameplay Impact:

Humans = flexible (good for new players)
Soulborn = magic-focused (DSP capacity helps casters)
Half-Abyss = tank builds (high Resilience)
No gender lock: Player chooses pronouns (he/she/they), body type (3 options), voice pitch (high/mid/low).

Step 2: Choose Class Role
Player selects combat archetype:

CLASS OPTIONS:

BLOOMGUARD (Defender)
Role: Frontline tank, protector
Starting Stats: +2 Might, +1 Resilience
Starting Skill: Shield Wall (allies behind you get +2 AC)
Starting Spell: Soul Shield (Tier 1, +Guard to target)
Faction Start: Bloomguard +5 reputation
Equipment: Heavy armor preference, shields
THORNBINDER (Rogue/Scout)
Role: Stealth, intelligence, critical strikes
Starting Stats: +2 Agility, +1 Insight
Starting Skill: Shadow Step (bonus movement in dim light)
Starting Spell: Verdant Grasp (Tier 1, roots enemy)
Faction Start: Thornbinders +5 reputation
Equipment: Light armor, daggers/bows
EMERALD MYSTIC (Caster/Healer)
Role: Soul magic specialist, support
Starting Stats: +2 Insight, +1 Charisma
Starting Skill: Sap Attunement (costs -2 DSP on all spells)
Starting Spell: Bloom Step (Tier 1, teleport + healing)
Faction Start: Emerald Coven +5 reputation
Equipment: Robes, staves/focus items
WILDKIN RANGER (Ranged DPS)
Role: Archery, animal bonding, nature magic
Starting Stats: +2 Agility, +1 Resilience
Starting Skill: Beast Bond (can summon animal companion 1/day)
Starting Spell: Thorn Volley (Tier 1, ranged multi-target)
Faction Start: Wildkin Pact +5 reputation
Equipment: Medium armor, bows/spears
SPORECALLER (Debuffer/Controller)
Role: Status effects, area denial, decay magic
Starting Stats: +1 Insight, +1 Resilience, +1 Might
Starting Skill: Fungal Affinity (immune to poison, can walk through spores)
Starting Spell: Spore Cloud (Tier 1, poison AoE)
Faction Start: Sporecallers' Vanguard +5 reputation
Equipment: Medium armor, clubs/staves
Multiclassing:
Unlocked at Level 5. Player can choose ONE ability from another class tree (limited hybridization, not full multiclass).

Step 3: Allocate Attribute Points
Player has 8 points to distribute among 5 attributes:

ATTRIBUTES:

MIGHT (Physical power)
Affects: Melee damage, carry capacity, forcing doors
Combat: +1 damage per point with melee weapons
Skills: Athletics checks (climbing, jumping, shoving)
AGILITY (Speed & precision)
Affects: Initiative, ranged attacks, evasion
Combat: +1 to hit with ranged, +1 Evasion per 2 points
Skills: Acrobatics (dodging), Stealth, Sleight of Hand
Special: 4+ Agility = 3 AP per turn (instead of 2)
RESILIENCE (Toughness & endurance)
Affects: HP, Guard regeneration, poison/disease resistance
Combat: +5 max HP per point, +1 Guard regen per 2 points
Skills: Endurance checks (holding breath, resisting pain)
INSIGHT (Mental acuity & magic)
Affects: Spell power, perception, Veilkeeper communion
Combat: +1 to spell attack rolls, +1 spell damage per 2 points
Skills: Investigation, Perception, Arcana knowledge
Special: 4+ Insight = can sense Veil disturbances (hidden enemies/secrets)
CHARISMA (Social influence)
Affects: Persuasion, intimidation, NPC pricing, faction gains
Combat: +1 to morale checks (fleeing enemies)
Skills: Persuasion, Deception, Intimidation, Performance
Special: 4+ Charisma = shop prices -10%
Default Array (if player skips): 2, 2, 2, 1, 1
Min per stat: 0
Max per stat: 4 (at creation)
Cap: 6 (achievable through leveling)

Examples:

Tank Build: Might 3, Resilience 3, Agility 1, Insight 0, Charisma 1
Mage Build: Insight 4, Charisma 2, Agility 1, Resilience 1, Might 0
Balanced: 2, 2, 2, 1, 1 (all-rounder)
Step 4: Customize Appearance
3D Character Viewer (React Three Fiber embedded in UI):

Player customizes:

Body Type: Slim, Average, Broad (affects hitbox slightly in isometric view)
Skin Tone: 12 options (pale to dark)
Hair Style: 15 options (short, long, bald, etc.)
Hair Color: Natural (8 options) or Verdant-touched (green-tinted, 4 options)
Facial Features: Eyes (6 shapes), nose (4 types), mouth (4 types)
Scars/Markings: Optional (facial scar, tattoos, birthmarks)
Verdant Sigil Placement (if Soulborn): Forearm, chest, back, shoulder
Real-time Preview:
3D model updates as you make choices. Can rotate 360°.

Equipment Preview:
Starting armor/weapon shows on model.

Step 5: Name & Backstory
Name:

Freeform text input
Optional: Randomize button (generates Verdance-appropriate names)
Examples: Kaelen, Lyris, Sylara, Morvain, Theron
Backstory (Optional but Affects Dialogue):

Player chooses ONE background trait:

Orphan of the Soul War
Effect: NPCs treat you with pity/sympathy
Quest unlock: "Lost Lineage" (find family records)
Bloomguard Legacy
Effect: Bloomguard faction starts at +10 (instead of +5 for class)
Quest unlock: "Father's Shield" (recover ancestor's weapon)
Emerald Coven Initiate
Effect: Start with 1 free Veilkeeper consultation (no Hollowing tick)
Quest unlock: "The First Lesson" (complete ritual)
Thornbinder Recruit
Effect: Criminality threshold +10% (law more lenient)
Quest unlock: "Shadow Network" (join secret operations)
Wildkin Foundling
Effect: Animals neutral to you (won't attack unless provoked)
Quest unlock: "Spirit Companion" (bond with rare beast)
Abyss Survivor
Effect: Abyss enemies less aggressive (dialogue options appear)
Quest unlock: "The Other Side" (diplomatic path with Abyss)
Merchant's Heir
Effect: Shop prices -5% (stacks with Charisma bonus)
Quest unlock: "Family Business" (help rebuild trade routes)
Veil-Touched
Effect: Can hear faint Veilkeeper whispers (hints in environment)
Quest unlock: "The Pattern Speaks" (decode prophecy)
Gameplay Impact:
AI DM references chosen backstory in narration. NPCs comment on your origin.

5.2 CHARACTER STATS (Derived)
After creation, character sheet displays:

PRIMARY STATS:

Level: 1-10 progression
XP: Current / Next Level
HP (Hit Points): Base 20 + (Resilience × 5)
Guard (Armor Integrity): Base 5 + Armor Bonus
AP (Action Points): 2 (or 3 if Agility ≥ 4)
Speed: 4-6 tiles per turn (base 4 + Agility modifier)
Evasion: 10 + Agility + Armor Bonus
SECONDARY STATS:

Initiative Modifier: +Agility
Melee Attack Bonus: +Might
Ranged Attack Bonus: +Agility
Spell Attack Bonus: +Insight
Carry Capacity: 10 + (Might × 5) items
RESOURCE BARS:

HP Bar: Green, depletes to yellow (50%), red (25%)
Guard Bar: Silver, regenerates +2/turn (or +4 if Defending)
DSP Bar: Emerald glow, SHARED with world (displayed separately)
5.3 LEVELING SYSTEM
XP Requirements:

Level 1 → 2: 100 XP
Level 2 → 3: 250 XP (cumulative: 350)
Level 3 → 4: 500 XP (cumulative: 850)
Level 4 → 5: 850 XP (cumulative: 1,700)
Level 5 → 6: 1,300 XP (cumulative: 3,000)
Level 6 → 7: 1,900 XP (cumulative: 4,900)
Level 7 → 8: 2,600 XP (cumulative: 7,500)
Level 8 → 9: 3,500 XP (cumulative: 11,000)
Level 9 → 10: 5,000 XP (cumulative: 16,000)
XP Sources:

Combat encounters: 50-200 XP (based on difficulty)
Quest completion: 100-500 XP (main quests more)
Discovery: 25-50 XP (finding secret areas)
Diplomatic solutions: 75-150 XP (non-violent resolutions)
Veilkeeper wisdom: 50 XP (each consultation, if you use the knowledge)
Level-Up Rewards:

Every level grants:

+1 Attribute Point (allocate to any stat, max 6)
+10 Max HP
+5 Max Guard (if wearing armor)
+1 Skill Rank (improve skill proficiency)
Choose 1 Talent (passive ability from talent tree)
Specific levels unlock:

Level 3: Tier 2 spells available
Level 5: Multiclass option (pick 1 ability from other class)
Level 7: Tier 3 spells available
Level 10: Ultimate ability (class-specific capstone)
Level-Up Scene:

Music swells (triumphant)
Character glows (emerald light)
UI presents choices (attribute, talent, spell)
3D character viewer updates (shows growth visually)
5.4 SKILL SYSTEM
Skills are proficiencies that improve with use:

SKILL LIST (12 Total):

Combat Skills:

Melee Combat — Affects melee attack rolls
Ranged Combat — Affects bow/thrown attacks
Soul Magic — Affects spell attack rolls
Defense — Affects Evasion and Guard regeneration
Physical Skills: 5. Athletics — Climbing, jumping, forcing doors 6. Acrobatics — Dodging, balancing, tumbling 7. Stealth — Sneaking, hiding, pickpocketing

Mental Skills: 8. Perception — Spotting hidden objects, sensing danger 9. Investigation — Searching for clues, solving puzzles 10. Arcana — Knowledge of magic, Veil lore

Social Skills: 11. Persuasion — Convincing others, diplomacy 12. Intimidation — Threatening, coercing

Skill Ranks:

Rank 0: Untrained (-2 penalty)
Rank 1: Novice (+0)
Rank 2: Practiced (+2)
Rank 3: Expert (+4)
Rank 4: Master (+6)
Skill Progression:

Gain +1 rank per level (player chooses which skill)
Can also improve through use (after 10 successful rolls, AI DM offers rank-up)
Max 2 skills at Rank 4 (forces specialization)
Skill Checks:

d20 + Attribute + Skill Rank vs DC
Example:

Climbing a crumbling root bridge
Roll: d20 + Might + Athletics Rank vs DC 14
Player has Might 2, Athletics Rank 2
Rolls 11 + 2 + 2 = 15 → Success!
5.5 TALENT TREES (Passive Abilities)
Player chooses 1 talent per level (levels 1-10 = 10 talents total).

5 TALENT TREES (one per design pillar):

TREE 1: MARTIAL PROWESS
Weapon Master (Lvl 1): +1 to all attack rolls
Cleave (Lvl 3): Melee attacks can hit 2 adjacent enemies
Counterattack (Lvl 5): When enemy misses you, free attack (1/turn)
Critical Focus (Lvl 7): Critical hits deal +1 damage die
Relentless (Lvl 9): When reduced to 0 HP, survive at 1 HP (1/day)
TREE 2: GUARDIAN'S OATH
Shield Expert (Lvl 1): +2 Guard regeneration per turn
Protector (Lvl 3): Allies adjacent to you get +1 Evasion
Unbreakable (Lvl 5): Guard cannot drop below 1 (while conscious)
Taunt (Lvl 7): Force enemy to attack you (Charisma check, 1/combat)
Martyr's Stand (Lvl 9): When ally would die, transfer damage to you
TREE 3: SOUL MAGIC MASTERY
Efficient Casting (Lvl 1): All spells cost -2 DSP
Spell Surge (Lvl 3): Critical hits on spells roll extra damage die
Resonance (Lvl 5): During Silver Sap, spells cost -5 DSP additionally
Arcane Focus (Lvl 7): Can maintain 2 concentration spells at once
Verdant Apex (Lvl 9): Tier 3 spells cost -10 DSP
TREE 4: VERDANT BOND
Root Walker (Lvl 1): Ignore difficult terrain (roots, fungi)
Nature's Ally (Lvl 3): Animals won't attack unless provoked
Eternal Bloom (Lvl 5): Restore 1d6 HP at start of each turn
Veil Sight (Lvl 7): Can see invisible/hidden enemies
Living Armor (Lvl 9): Armor regenerates 1 point per turn
TREE 5: TACTICAL MIND
Opportunist (Lvl 1): Flanking grants +2 to attack
Ambush Expert (Lvl 3): First attack of combat has Advantage
Tactical Reposition (Lvl 5): Can move after attacking (costs +1 AP)
Tactical Mind (Lvl 7): +1 AP once per combat
Perfect Strategy (Lvl 9): Once per combat, reroll any failed roll
Talent Synergies:
AI DM recognizes combinations (e.g., Cleave + Opportunist = devastating flanking AoE).

5.6 CHARACTER PROGRESSION EXAMPLE
Let's trace Kaelen Thornweave from Level 1 → 10:

CREATION:

Ancestry: Soulborn (+1 Charisma, +1 Insight, Verdant Sigil)
Class: Bloomguard (+2 Might, +1 Resilience)
Attributes: Might 3, Agility 1, Resilience 3, Insight 1, Charisma 2
HP: 20 + (3×5) = 35
Starting Skills: Melee 1, Defense 1, Persuasion 1
LEVEL 2:

XP: 100 earned (first dungeon cleared)
Gains: +1 Attribute → Might 4, +10 HP (now 45), +1 Skill → Melee 2
Talent: Weapon Master (+1 to attacks)
LEVEL 3:

XP: 250 earned (Act 1 climax)
Gains: +1 Attribute → Resilience 4, +10 HP (55), +1 Skill → Defense 2
Talent: Shield Expert (+2 Guard regen)
Unlock: Tier 2 spells → learns "Root Sentinel"
LEVEL 5:

XP: 850 earned (midpoint)
Gains: +1 Attribute → Might 5, +10 HP (75), +1 Skill → Perception 1
Talent: Unbreakable (Guard never drops below 1)
Unlock: Multiclass → takes "Efficient Casting" from Mystic tree
LEVEL 7:

XP: 1,900 earned (Act 2 complete)
Gains: +1 Attribute → Charisma 3, +10 HP (95), +1 Skill → Persuasion 2
Talent: Protector (allies get +1 Evasion)
Unlock: Tier 3 spells → learns "Verdant Nexus"
LEVEL 10:

XP: 5,000 earned (final push)
Gains: +1 Attribute → Resilience 5, +10 HP (115), +1 Skill → Defense 3
Talent: Relentless (survive at 1 HP once/day)
Ultimate: "Everwood's Wrath" (Bloomguard capstone)
Final Stats:

HP: 115, Guard: 18 (with armor), AP: 2
Might 5, Agility 1, Resilience 5, Insight 1, Charisma 3
Talents: 10 (hybrid tank/support build)
Spells: 8 (mix of buffs and control)
Playstyle Emerged:
Unkillable frontline tank who protects allies and conserves DSP (Efficient Casting talent).

6. COMBAT SYSTEM (TURN-BASED TACTICAL)
6.1 COMBAT PHILOSOPHY
Core Principle:
"Chess with magic and consequences."

Design Goals:

Every turn matters — No filler actions
Positioning > raw stats — Terrain and tactics win fights
Telegraphed threats — No gotcha moments, fair challenges
Recoverable mistakes — Undo button before confirm
DSP tension — Using magic is powerful but costly
Anti-Patterns We Avoid:

❌ RNG fest (missing 95% shots repeatedly)
❌ Action spam (mashing attack button)
❌ Unreadable chaos (what just happened?)
❌ Death spirals (one mistake = game over)
6.2 COMBAT TRIGGERS
How Combat Starts:

Enemy Proximity (Most Common)
Player moves within 3 tiles of enemy
AI DM rolls Perception for player (can be avoided with high Stealth)
If undetected: Surprise round (player acts first)
If detected: Standard initiative
Ambush (Scripted or Random)
AI DM: "You hear movement behind—roll Initiative!"
No Perception check (already failed)
Enemies get +2 to initiative
Forced Encounter (Boss/Story)
Cinematic transition
Cannot be avoided
Often unique mechanics
Player-Initiated
Player clicks "Attack" on enemy
Guarantees first strike
Transition to Combat Mode:

EXPLORATION MODE
  ↓ (Enemy detected)
Screen pulses (red warning flash)
  ↓
Music shifts (combat theme fades in)
  ↓
Grid overlay appears (tactical view)
  ↓
Initiative rolls displayed
  ↓
COMBAT MODE ACTIVE
6.3 INITIATIVE & TURN ORDER
Initiative Roll:

d20 + Agility modifier
Turn Order Display:

Right side of screen (vertical strip)
Character portraits in order (top = current turn)
Numbers shown (initiative values)
Can see 2-3 turns ahead
Example:

TURN ORDER:
1. Player (18)       ← Current
2. Sporecaller (15)  ← Next
3. Bloomguard Ally (12)
4. Abyss Scout (10)
Surprise Rounds:

If player undetected → Free turn before initiative
If player ambushed → Enemies get free turn first
Tied Initiative:

Players always win ties
Enemies randomized among themselves
6.4 ACTION POINTS (AP) SYSTEM
AP Per Turn:

2 AP (standard, most characters)
3 AP (if Agility ≥ 4, or certain buffs)
AP Costs:

Action	AP Cost
Move (up to Speed)	1 AP
Basic Attack (melee/ranged)	1 AP
Tier 1 Spell	1 AP
Tier 2 Spell	2 AP
Tier 3 Spell	3 AP
Use Item	1 AP
Defend	1 AP
Interact (lever, door, loot)	1 AP
End Turn	0 AP (forfeit remaining)
AP Flexibility:

Can split movement (move 2 tiles → attack → move 2 more)
Can save AP (Defend with 1 AP, save 1 for reactions)
Cannot bank AP to next turn (use or lose)
Visual Feedback:

AP shown as pips (●●● = 3 AP, ●●○ = 2/3 used)
Grey out actions when insufficient AP
Undo button resets AP (before confirming turn)
6.5 MOVEMENT & POSITIONING
Movement Rules:

Speed Stat:

Base: 4 tiles
+1 per Agility point above 1
Example: Agility 3 = 6 tiles per turn
Movement Types:

Normal Movement (1 AP)
Walk to any tile within Speed range
Pathfinding automatic (A* algorithm)
Cannot move through enemies
Difficult Terrain (+1 AP cost)
Fungal zones, Sap pools, rubble
Visual indicator (orange tint on tile)
Talent "Root Walker" ignores this
Climbing (Special)
Moving to higher elevation
Costs +1 AP per level climbed
Requires Athletics check (DC varies)
Jumping Down (Free)
Moving to lower elevation
No AP cost BUT:
1 level = safe
2+ levels = 1d6 fall damage per level
Positioning Bonuses:

High Ground (+1 Attack):

Being 1+ elevation above target
Affects ranged and melee attacks
Stacks with other bonuses
Flanking (+2 Attack):

You and ally on opposite sides of enemy
Both get bonus (encourage teamwork)
Talent "Opportunist" doubles this
Cover (+2 Evasion):

Standing behind solid object (wall, crystal, tree)
Enemy must target around cover
Full cover = cannot be hit at all
Tactical Example:

Grid (10x10):
[ ] [ ] [W] [ ] [ ]    W = Wall
[ ] [E] [ ] [A] [ ]    E = Enemy
[P] [ ] [ ] [ ] [ ]    P = Player
                       A = Ally

Player Move:
1. Move behind wall (1 AP) → Now has cover (+2 Evasion)
2. Attack enemy (1 AP) → No bonuses

Better Move:
1. Move diagonal to enemy's right (1 AP)
2. Attack (1 AP) → Flanking bonus (+2 from ally on left)
6.6 BASIC ATTACKS
Melee Attack:

ROLL: d20 + Might + Weapon Skill Rank
  vs
ENEMY EVASION: 10 + Agility + Armor Bonus

If Hit:
  Roll Weapon Damage + Might Modifier
  Example: Everwood Saber (1d8) + Might 3 = 1d8+3
Ranged Attack:

ROLL: d20 + Agility + Ranged Skill Rank
  vs
ENEMY EVASION

If Hit:
  Roll Weapon Damage + Agility Modifier (if applicable)
  Example: Longbow (1d10) + Agility 2 = 1d10+2
Critical Hits:

Natural 20 (or expanded range with talents)
Roll damage dice twice, add both
Example: Normal hit 1d8+3 = 7, Crit = 2d8+3 = 15
Miss:

No damage dealt
AP still consumed
Narration: "Your blade glances off bark armor"
Attack Modifiers:

Situation	Modifier
Flanking enemy	+2 to hit
High ground	+1 to hit
Target has cover	-2 to hit
Attacking while Defending	-2 to hit
Blind/darkness	Disadvantage (roll 2d20, take lower)
Blessed/buffed	Advantage (roll 2d20, take higher)
6.7 COMBAT STATS
HP (Hit Points):

Represents vitality/life force
0 HP = Downed (unconscious, not dead)
-10 HP = Death (permanent unless revived)
Recovers via:
Rest (8 hours = full HP)
Potions (instant, 2d8+2 typical)
Healing spells (varies)
Blue Sap phase (slow regen, +1d6/day)
Guard (Armor Integrity):

Represents armor/shields absorbing damage
Damage hits Guard first, then HP
0 Guard = Vulnerable (next hit goes to HP)
Regenerates:
+2 per turn (passive)
+4 per turn (if using Defend action)
+1d6 (certain spells/items)
Max Guard = Armor value (light 5, medium 10, heavy 15)
Example Damage Sequence:

Enemy deals 12 damage
Player has: HP 45/45, Guard 8/10

Damage application:
  Guard absorbs 8 → Guard 0/10
  Remaining 4 → HP 41/45

Next Turn:
  Guard regenerates +2 → Guard 2/10
6.8 COMBAT ACTIONS (Detailed)
MOVE (1 AP)
Select destination tile (within Speed range)
Pathfinding calculates route
Character sprite animates (walk animation)
Can be interrupted by opportunity attacks (if enemy has that ability)
ATTACK (1 AP)
Select enemy target
Tooltip shows:
Hit chance (e.g., "68% to hit")
Estimated damage range (e.g., "4-11 damage")
Enemy Guard/HP status
Click "Confirm"
Dice roll animation
Hit or miss visual feedback
Damage numbers float above target
CAST SPELL (1-3 AP, varies by tier)
Casting Process:

Click "Cast" button
Spell menu opens (shows learned spells)
Each spell displays:
Name + icon
AP cost
DSP cost
Effect summary
Range (tiles)
Select spell
Select target (tile or enemy)
Warning if DSP cost is high ("This will drain DSP to 45. Proceed?")
Confirm cast
VFX plays (emerald energy effects)
DSP bar updates (global resource drains)
Effect applies (damage, buff, debuff, etc.)
Spell Targeting Types:

Single Target: Click enemy/ally
Ground Target: Click tile (AoE centered there)
Self: Auto-targets caster
Cone/Line: Click direction, affects path
Concentration Spells:

Some spells require concentration
Can only maintain 1 at a time (unless talent)
If you take damage: Save (DC 10) or spell ends
If you cast another concentration spell: First one ends
USE ITEM (1 AP)
Open quick item menu (hotbar)
Select consumable (potion, bomb, scroll)
Target (self or tile/enemy)
Item consumed
Effect applies
Common Items:

Everspring Potion: Restore 2d8+2 HP (instant)
Dreamroot Tea: Restore 1d6 HP, remove 1 status effect
Viridian Bomb: Throw at tile, 3d6 damage in 2-tile radius
Scroll of Soul Shield: Cast Soul Shield (no DSP cost, one-use)
DEFEND (1 AP)
Character takes defensive stance
Bonuses until start of next turn:
+3 Evasion
+2 to all saves
+4 Guard regeneration (instead of +2)
Cannot move this turn
Visual: Shield icon above character
INTERACT (1 AP)
Pull lever (activate trap, open door)
Loot corpse (collect items mid-combat)
Break crystal (environmental hazard trigger)
Push object (block enemy path)
AI DM Adjudicates:
Creative uses beyond programmed interactions.

END TURN (0 AP)
Forfeit remaining AP
Turn passes to next in initiative order
Guard regenerates (+2 or +4 if Defended)
Status effects tick (poison damage, buff duration, etc.)
6.9 ENEMY AI BEHAVIORS
Enemies controlled by AI (not player). Each enemy type has behavior archetype:

ARCHETYPE 1: AGGRESSIVE (Abyss Infiltrators)
Priority: Deal maximum damage
Tactics:

Rush player (move to melee range)
Use heavy attacks (high damage abilities)
Ignore self-preservation (will trade HP for kills)
Focus wounded targets (opportunistic)
AI Logic:

if player_hp < 50%:
  attack_player()
elif ally_nearby_is_wounded:
  attack_wounded_ally()
else:
  attack_highest_threat()
ARCHETYPE 2: DEFENSIVE (Corrupted Root Sentinels)
Priority: Protect allies
Tactics:

Bodyblock (stand between player and vulnerable allies)
Use Guard abilities (buff allied Guard)
Taunt player (force attacks on self)
Only attack if no allies need protection
AI Logic:

if ally_hp < 30% and within_3_tiles:
  move_to_protect_ally()
  use_guard_ability()
elif player_attacking_ally:
  taunt_player()
else:
  defend_action()
ARCHETYPE 3: CONTROLLER (Sporecaller Shamans)
Priority: Apply status effects
Tactics:

Stay at range (kite player)
Spam debuffs (poison, slow, blind)
Create hazard zones (spore clouds)
Flee if player gets close
AI Logic:

if player_within_3_tiles:
  move_away_max_speed()
elif ally_can_benefit_from_buff:
  cast_buff()
else:
  cast_debuff_on_player()
ARCHETYPE 4: SUPPORT (Veil Echoes)
Priority: Buff allies, debuff enemies
Tactics:

Heal wounded allies (priority target: <50% HP)
Remove ally debuffs (cleanse)
Shield allies (Guard buffs)
Only attacks if no support needed
AI Logic:

if ally_hp < 50%:
  cast_heal()
elif ally_has_debuff:
  cast_cleanse()
elif ally_guard_low:
  cast_soul_shield()
else:
  attack_player()
ARCHETYPE 5: OPPORTUNIST (Thornbinder Rogues)
Priority: Exploit weaknesses
Tactics:

Flanking (position opposite ally)
Backstab (attack from behind = bonus damage)
Hit-and-run (attack then move away)
Target casters (low Guard targets)
AI Logic:

if can_flank_player:
  move_to_flank_position()
  attack()
elif caster_enemy_nearby and unguarded:
  attack_caster()
elif attacked_this_turn:
  move_away_after_attack()
Enemy Telegraphing:
All major enemy actions show intent icon above their head:

Icon	Meaning	Player Response
⚔️	Basic Attack	Position for evasion
💥	Heavy Attack (2x damage)	Defend or move out of range
🌀	AoE Spell	Spread out allies
🛡️	Defensive Stance	Focus on other enemies
🏃	Movement/Reposition	Prepare for flanking
☠️	Ultimate Ability	All-hands defensive
💚	Healing Ally	Interrupt or kill healer
Player Advantage:
You see enemy intent → plan counter-strategy.

6.10 STATUS EFFECTS
12 STATUS TYPES:

BUFFS (Positive):
SOUL SHIELD
Effect: +2 Guard, +2 Evasion
Duration: 2 turns
Source: Spell, potion
Visual: Emerald barrier shimmer
BLESSED
Effect: Advantage on all rolls (roll 2d20, take higher)
Duration: 3 turns
Source: Tier 2 spell
Visual: Silver glow
HASTENED
Effect: +1 AP this turn only
Duration: 1 turn
Source: Tier 3 spell, rare item
Visual: Speed lines
REGENERATING
Effect: Restore 1d6 HP at start of turn
Duration: 3 turns
Source: Blue Sap phase, spell
Visual: Green sparkles
DEBUFFS (Negative):
POISONED
Effect: 1d4 damage at start of turn
Duration: 3 turns (or until cleansed)
Source: Sporecaller attacks, toxic terrain
Visual: Green miasma
BLEEDING
Effect: 1d4 damage at end of turn, stacks (can have 2-3 bleed)
Duration: 2 turns
Source: Thornfang Blade, critical hits
Visual: Red droplets
ROOTED
Effect: Cannot move (can still attack/cast)
Duration: 1 turn
Source: Verdant Grasp spell, root traps
Visual: Vines wrapped around feet
BLINDED
Effect: Disadvantage on attacks (roll 2d20, take lower)
Duration: 2 turns
Source: Bioluminescent flash, smoke
Visual: Foggy overlay
CORRUPTED
Effect: 1d6 damage per turn, spreads to allies within 2 tiles
Duration: Until cleansed (doesn't expire naturally)
Source: Abyss magic, corruption patches
Visual: Black-green veins
SLOWED
Effect: -2 Speed, -1 AP
Duration: 2 turns
Source: Sap pools, ice magic
Visual: Blue tint, sluggish animation
CONTROL EFFECTS:
STUNNED
Effect: Skip entire turn (cannot act)
Duration: 1 turn
Source: Concussive attacks, high damage crits
Visual: Stars circling head
FEARED
Effect: Must move away from source, cannot attack
Duration: 1 turn
Source: Hollow Tree aura, intimidation
Visual: Character shaking
Status Stacking:

Most statuses DON'T stack (refreshes duration instead)
Exception: Bleed, Poison (can have multiple instances)
Example: Hit by Thornfang 3 times = 3 stacks of Bleed = 3d4 damage/turn
Cleansing:

Dreamroot Tea (item): Remove 1 debuff
Sap Surge (Tier 3 spell): Cleanse all debuffs on target
Blue Sap phase: Natural decay (debuffs last 50% shorter)
Emerald Coven NPCs: Cleanse service (costs gold)
Status Display:

Icons above character (max 3 shown, hover for full list)
Tooltip on hover (shows duration, effect magnitude)
Color-coded:
Green border = buff
Red border = debuff
Purple border = control effect
6.11 COMBAT TERRAIN TYPES
Terrain affects tactics significantly:

1. ROOT BRIDGE
Movement: Normal
Combat: High ground (+1 attack if fighting enemies below)
Hazard: Can collapse if damaged (DC 14 Agility save or fall 2 levels = 2d6 damage)
Visual: Woven root planks, slightly elevated
Tactic: Archers love this, melee risky (one big hit breaks bridge)
2. FUNGAL ZONE
Movement: Difficult terrain (+1 AP to cross)
Combat: Spore damage (1d4 per turn spent inside)
Vision: Blocks line of sight (can't target through it)
Visual: Dense mushroom clusters, glowing caps
Tactic: Lure enemies in, you stay out (or talent "Fungal Affinity" to ignore)
3. SAP POOL
Movement: Sticky (costs 2 AP to leave pool)
Combat: Effect depends on Sap Phase:
Blue Sap: Heals 1d6/turn
Crimson Sap: Slows (-1 AP)
Silver Sap: Buffs magic (+1 spell damage die)
Visual: Glowing liquid, color matches current phase
Tactic: Position casters in Silver Sap pools for bonus damage
4. HOLLOW TREE
Movement: Blocks path (impassable)
Combat: Fear aura (enemies within 2 tiles: DC 12 save or Feared for 1 turn)
Cover: Provides full cover if standing behind
Visual: Dead tree, gnarled, ominous
Tactic: Use as shield vs ranged, exploit fear for crowd control
5. VIRIDIAN CRYSTAL FORMATION
Movement: Blocks path
Combat: Can be shattered (attack it, 15 HP)
On break: 2d6 damage in 2-tile radius
Leaves crystal shards (difficult terrain)
Magic: Standing adjacent = +5 DSP regeneration per turn
Visual: Glowing emerald crystals
Tactic: Risk/reward (break for damage OR preserve for DSP regen)
6. CORRUPTION PATCH
Movement: Normal but dangerous
Combat: Standing on it = DC 14 save or gain Corrupted status (1d6/turn, spreads)
Spread: Grows 1 tile per round if not cleansed
Visual: Black-green ooze, pulsing
Tactic: Cleanse with Burn Magic spell, or avoid entirely
7. ELEVATION PLATFORMS
Height Levels: Ground (0), Platform (+1), Canopy (+2)
Combat: +1 attack per level of elevation above target
Movement:
Climb up: +1 AP per level
Jump down: Free, but fall damage if 2+ levels (1d6/level)
Visual: Wooden platforms, stone ledges, canopy branches
Tactic: Claim high ground early for ranged advantage
8. LIVING ROOTS (Animated)
Movement: Normal until triggered
Combat: Can be animated by player (Tier 2 spell: Root Animation)
Roots grapple enemies (DC 14 Athletics to escape)
Lasts 2 turns
Visual: Dormant roots on ground, glow when active
Tactic: Area denial, lock down melee enemies
9. BIOLUMINESCENT FUNGI (Interactive)
Movement: Normal
Combat: Can be triggered (1 AP)
Bright flash: Enemies in 3-tile radius Blinded (1 turn)
One-use per fungi cluster
Visual: Softly glowing, pulses when near
Tactic: Save for crucial moment (blind enemy before big attack)
Terrain Combination Example:

Arena: Hollowroot Catacombs Chamber
[ ] [F] [F] [ ] [C]    F = Fungi (interactive)
[R] [R] [E] [ ] [ ]    R = Root bridge (high ground)
[ ] [P] [ ] [E] [S]    P = Player
[H] [ ] [ ] [ ] [S]    E = Enemy
[ ] [ ] [E] [C] [ ]    H = Hollow Tree (cover)
                        C = Corruption patch
                        S = Sap pool (Silver phase)

Tactical Opportunity:
1. Trigger fungi (blind 2 enemies)
2. Move to root bridge (high ground)
3. Push enemy into corruption patch (environmental kill)
4. Use Hollow Tree for cover when low HP
5. Position caster in Silver Sap pool (+1 damage die)
6.12 VICTORY & DEFEAT CONDITIONS
VICTORY:
Combat ends when:

All enemies defeated (0 HP or fled)
Enemies surrender (AI DM determines based on morale)
Objective complete (some fights have goals beyond killing)
Victory Rewards:

XP Awarded: Based on difficulty (50-200 XP per encounter)
Loot Drops:
Random items from enemy loot table
Gold (10-100g)
Crafting materials
Quest items (if relevant)
DSP Recovery: +5 DSP (small reward for conserving)
Narration: AI DM describes aftermath
Victory Scene:

Music: Triumphant flourish
Visual: Enemies fade (dissolve animation)
UI: "VICTORY" banner
Loot appears on ground (glowing items)
Player auto-collects or can choose
XP bar fills (level-up if threshold reached)
DEFEAT:
Player dies when:

HP reaches -10 (instant death)
All party members downed (if companions present)
Death Consequences:

Permadeath OFF (Default, Recommended):

Reload from last save (auto-save before combat)
Lose nothing except time
Encouragement message: "Restraint means knowing when to retreat"
Permadeath ON (Optional Hardcore Mode):

Character deleted permanently
Save file locked
Achievement: "Hollow Ending" (finish game without dying)
Retreat Option:

Can flee combat (costs 2 AP, all party members must use)
Success: DC 14 Agility check
Failure: Opportunity attacks from all enemies
On success: Return to last safe area, lose 25% collected loot
No XP from encounter
6.13 BOSS ENCOUNTERS (Special Mechanics)
Boss fights have unique mechanics beyond normal combat:

BOSS EXAMPLE: The Void Architect (Abyss Champion)
Phase 1 (HP 100-60):

Standard attacks
Summons 2 Abyss Grunts every 3 turns
Mechanic: Soul Siphon (drains player DSP by 10, heals boss 15 HP)
Phase 2 (HP 59-30):

Enrages (attacks twice per turn)
Corruption spreads (1 tile expands every turn)
Mechanic: Void Collapse (AoE, 3d8 damage, 5-tile radius, telegraphed 1 turn before)
Phase 3 (HP 29-0):

Desperate (Void Collapse every turn)
Healing disabled (regeneration = 0)
Mechanic: Final Stand (at 0 HP, survives 1 more turn, ultimate attack)
Counter-Play:

Phase 1: Ignore summons, focus boss, conserve DSP
Phase 2: Spread out to avoid AoE, cleanse corruption with Burn Magic
Phase 3: All-in damage, tank the ultimate with Defend + Soul Shield
Unique Loot:

Void Shard (legendary crafting material)
Abyss Cloak (armor, +corruption resistance)
500 XP
6.14 COMBAT UI/UX SPECIFICATION
HUD During Combat:

┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  TOP BAR                                            │
│  [Character Portrait] HP: ████████░░ 45/50          │
│                       Guard: ████░░░░ 8/12          │
│                       AP: ●●○ (2/3)                 │
│                                                      │
│  [DSP Global] ████████░░░░ 65/100                  │
│  [Sap Phase] SILVER (2 days left)                  │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  MAIN COMBAT VIEW (Isometric Grid)                 │
│                                                      │
│      [Tactical grid with characters/enemies]        │
│      [Terrain features visible]                     │
│      [Movement range highlighted]                   │
│      [Enemy intent icons above heads]               │
│                                                      │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  RIGHT SIDEBAR                                      │
│  TURN ORDER:                                        │
│  1. ➤ Player (18)         ← Current                │
│  2.   Sporecaller (15)    ← Shows intent: 🌀       │
│  3.   Ally (12)                                     │
│  4.   Abyss Scout (10)    ← Shows intent: ⚔️       │
│                                                      │
│  SELECTED ENEMY:                                    │
│  [Sporecaller Grunt]                                │
│  HP: 8/12                                           │
│  Guard: 0/5                                         │
│  Status: Poisoned (2 turns)                         │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  BOTTOM ACTION BAR                                  │
│  [Move] [Attack] [Cast] [Item] [Defend] [End Turn] │
│                                                      │
│  [Undo] [Confirm Turn]                             │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
Interaction Flow:

Player's Turn Starts:
Music cue (short jingle)
"Your Turn" text flashes
Camera centers on player character
Action bar highlights
Player Selects Action (e.g., Move):
Grid highlights valid movement tiles (blue)
Invalid tiles greyed out
Hover shows AP cost
Player Confirms:
Character animates (walk cycle)
AP updates (●●● → ●●○)
Action bar refreshes (shows remaining options)
Player Selects Second Action (e.g., Attack):
Targeting reticle appears
Hover enemy shows:
     Sporecaller Grunt
     Hit Chance: 68%
     Damage: 4-11 (1d8+3)
     [Confirm Attack]
Click confirm
Attack Resolves:
Dice roll animation (d20 spins)
Result displayed: "18 vs Evasion 14 — HIT!"
Damage roll: "1d8+3 = 9 damage"
Visual: Sword swing animation, impact flash
Enemy HP bar drains
Floating damage number: "-9"
Player Confirms Turn:
"Confirm Turn" button glows
Click
Turn passes to next initiative
Enemy turn begins (automated)
Undo Feature:

"Undo" button always visible
Resets ALL actions this turn (back to start of turn)
Cannot undo after clicking "Confirm Turn"
Encourages experimentation
7. DOMAIN SOUL POOL (DSP) MECHANICS
7.1 DSP PHILOSOPHY
Core Concept:
"Your magic doesn't cost your mana—it costs everyone's life force."

Narrative Hook:
The Everwood (Verdance's heart tree) stores ancestral soul energy. Every Soulborn draws from this shared pool. Overuse weakens the Veil, invites corruption, harms NPCs.

Gameplay Goal:
Create tension between power and consequence. Players must manage a global resource that others depend on.

7.2 DSP STATS & DISPLAY
DSP Range: 0 → 100

Starting DSP: 100 (healthy domain)

Visual Representation:

HUD Bar: Emerald glow, pulsing (100 = bright, 0 = dim/flickering)
Everwood Tree: Background visual (healthy = lush, crisis = withering)
NPC Dialogue: References DSP status ("The Veil shimmers strong today" vs "I feel the roots weakening")
DSP Thresholds:

DSP Range	Status	World State	NPC Behavior
90-100	Healthy	Veil strong, forests vibrant, bioluminescence bright	Confident, cheerful
70-89	Stable	Slight Veil shimmer, leaves pale slightly	Normal, some concern
50-69	Strained	Veil weakening, fungi dimming, NPC warnings	Worried, cautious
30-49	Crisis	Veil tears visible, corruption spreading	Panicked, some flee
10-29	Catastrophic	Veil collapsing, Everwood groaning, chaos	Terror, riots
0-9	Imminent Collapse	Domain dying, Abyss breaching freely	Despair, evacuation
7.3 DSP DRAINS (How It's Spent)
Soul Magic Costs:

Spell Tier	DSP Cost
Tier 1	5 DSP
Tier 2	10-15 DSP
Tier 3	20-30 DSP
Modified by:

Talent: Efficient Casting (-2 DSP all spells)
Sap Phase: Crimson (+5 DSP), Silver (-5 DSP), Blue (normal)
Equipment: Sap Capacitor Totem (stores 15 DSP, reusable battery)
Veilkeeper Consultations:

Each question: -10 DSP
Crimson Sap: -15 DSP
Rituals:

Early Silver Sap trigger: -40 DSP
Cleansing corruption zones: -15 DSP
Faction-specific rituals: -10 to -25 DSP
Domain Events (Automatic Drains):

Abyss incursion: -5 DSP per wave
Major boss present: -2 DSP per day (Veil strain)
Hollow Tree threshold reached: -10 DSP (guardian death)
7.4 DSP RECOVERY (How It's Restored)
Natural Regeneration:

Blue Sap Phase: +5 DSP per day (slow, steady)
No phase: 0 regeneration (stable state)
Crimson/Silver: 0 regeneration (or negative)
Active Recovery:

Long Rest at Sacred Sites: +10 DSP (8-hour rest at Canopy of Life, Emerald Cascades)
Quest Completion: +5 to +15 DSP (domain-helping quests)
Silver Sap Unbinding Event: +30 to +60 DSP (major one-time boost)
Domain Stabilization Ritual: +20 DSP (Tier 3 spell, requires rare materials)
Artifact Usage: Sap Capacitor Totem (pre-filled battery, +15 DSP when used)
Player Restraint Rewards:

Low-Magic Victory: Win combat without casting spells = +5 DSP bonus
Conservationist Achievement Tracker: Game tracks total DSP saved, unlocks rewards
7.5 DSP CRISIS EVENTS (Story Triggers)
When DSP drops below thresholds, world reacts:

DSP ≤ 50 (Strained):
Trigger: "The Veil Flickers"

Scene:

AI DM: "As you rest, the Canopy trembles. Bioluminescent fungi 
dim. Emerald Coven Seer Vael appears, concern etched deep.

Vael: 'The Domain Soul Pool wanes. We feel it in the roots—
Everwood's breath grows shallow. Your magic, though powerful, 
drains us all. Please... restraint.'"
Mechanical Changes:

Shop prices +10% (resource scarcity)
Encounter difficulty +10%
Some NPCs unavailable (hiding/praying)
DSP ≤ 30 (Crisis):
Trigger: "Veil Breach Warning"

Scene:

AI DM: "The Whispering Veil *tears*—a jagged wound in the 
spiritual fabric. Abyss scouts pour through. Civilians scream. 
Bloomguard rally, but they're overwhelmed.

Bloomguard Captain: 'Soulborn! We need you! But for the love 
of Everwood—no more soul magic! The Veil can't take it!'"
Mechanical Changes:

Forced encounter (Abyss wave)
If player uses ANY soul magic during fight:
Veil tears further (-5 DSP)
NPCs die (visible casualties)
Faction rep hit (Emerald Coven -10, Bloomguard -5)
Victory restores some DSP (+10 as reward)
DSP ≤ 10 (Catastrophic):
Trigger: "The Hollowing Choice"

Scene:

AI DM: "Everwood SCREAMS—a sound that transcends wood and 
leaf, resonating in your *soul*. The tree's heartwood cracks. 
Corruption floods the Canopy like black tide.

Veilkeeper Sylthara (weakened, barely conscious): 
'Child... we're dying. All of us. The pattern... breaks...'

You have three options:
1. [Sacrifice yourself] — Give your life force to restore DSP (game over, but noble ending)
2. [Force Silver Sap early] — Emergency ritual (-40 DSP now, +60 DSP later, but risks)
3. [Let nature decide] — Accept crisis, fight through it (hardest path)
Mechanical Impact:

Option 1: Credits roll, "Sacrifice" ending (bittersweet)
Option 2: Temporary fix, but permanently reduces DSP max to 80
Option 3: DSP stays at 10, game becomes very hard until Blue Sap phase
7.6 DSP & FACTION REACTIONS
Factions have opinions on DSP usage:

EMERALD COVEN (Protectors of Balance):

High DSP (70+): +reputation ("You honor the restraint")
Mid DSP (50-69): Neutral
Low DSP (<50): -reputation ("Your recklessness endangers us")
Critical (<30): Hostile (refuse to trade/help)
BLOOMGUARD (Duty Above All):

High DSP: +reputation (appreciate stability)
Low DSP in combat: Conflicted (needed power to win, but at cost)
Crisis DSP: Blame player if civilians die from Veil breach
THORNBINDERS (Pragmatists):

DSP level irrelevant (they care about results, not methods)
Exception: If DSP crisis causes operational failures, -reputation
SAPLING CONSORTIUM (Merchants):

Low DSP = Higher prices (scarcity economics)
High DSP = Better deals (abundance)
WILDKIN PACT (Nature's Balance):

Very sensitive to DSP (they feel Everwood's pain)
Low DSP: Animals become hostile, -reputation severely
7.7 DSP UI/UX DETAILS
HUD Display:

┌───────────────────────────────────────┐
│  DOMAIN SOUL POOL (Global Resource)  │
│  ████████░░░░░░ 65 / 100             │
│  Status: STRAINED                     │
│  Next Threshold: 50 (CRISIS)          │
│  Daily Change: -2 (Crimson Sap)       │
└───────────────────────────────────────┘
Spell Cast Warning:

You are about to cast: VERDANT NEXUS
Cost: 30 DSP
Current DSP: 65

After cast: 35 DSP (CRISIS THRESHOLD)

⚠️ WARNING: This will trigger Veil crisis event.
NPCs may die. Faction reputation will drop.

[Proceed Anyway] [Cancel] [Choose Different Spell]
Color Coding:

Green (70+): Healthy, safe to cast
Yellow (50-69): Caution, monitor usage
Red (30-49): Danger, crisis imminent
Flashing Red (<30): CRITICAL, avoid casting
Everwood Visual (Background):

100 DSP: Lush, glowing emerald, leaves full
70 DSP: Slight shimmer, some leaves pale
50 DSP: Visible cracks in bark, fungi dim
30 DSP: Bark blackening, roots exposed, groaning SFX
10 DSP: Collapsing, corruption spreading, emergency state
7.8 ADVANCED DSP MECHANICS
Personal DSP Capacity (Soulborn Only):
Soulborn Ancestry Trait: +5 max DSP capacity
Means: Player can "store" 5 DSP personally (not shared)
Use Case: Emergency reserve when global DSP is low
Recharge: Only during Blue Sap phase
Example:

Global DSP: 25 (Crisis)
Personal DSP: 5 (Soulborn reserve)

Player casts Tier 1 spell (5 DSP cost)
→ Uses Personal DSP (0 global drain)
→ Personal DSP: 0/5
→ Global DSP: Still 25 (unchanged)
Sap Capacitor Totem (Item):
Rare item (Emerald Coven Exalted reward)
Function: Stores 15 DSP (one-time battery)
Recharge: Automatically refills during Blue Sap phase
Use: Click to restore 15 DSP to global pool (instant)
Strategic: Save for emergencies (like healing potion for DSP)
Soul Battery Mechanic (Late-Game):
Unlocks: Level 8+ or quest "The Conduit"
Function: Convert HP to DSP (risky exchange)
Ratio: 10 HP → 5 DSP
Cannot kill yourself (stops at 1 HP)
Lore: "Blood for roots, flesh for Veil"
Use Case: Desperate situations (DSP <20, must cast crucial spell)
8. SAP CYCLE SYSTEM (LIVING CALENDAR)
8.1 SAP CYCLE PHILOSOPHY
Core Concept:
"The world doesn't wait for you—it breathes."

Design Goal:
Create a living world with predictable but impactful rhythms. Players must plan around the calendar, not just react.

Inspiration:

Majora's Mask (time pressure)
Darkest Dungeon (stress phases)
Stardew Valley (seasonal calendar)
Anti-Pattern:
Most RPGs have static worlds. Sap Cycles make Verdance dynamic.

8.2 THE THREE SAP PHASES
PHASE 1: CRIMSON SAP (Vulnerability)
Duration: 5 in-game days

Narrative:

"The Everwood exhales corruption. Crimson Sap seeps from bark—
a purge of toxins. The Veil thins. Shadows grow bolder."

Visual Changes:

Lighting: Cooler tones (red-tinged shadows)
Colors: Greens become muted, desaturated
Bioluminescence: Dims to 50% brightness
Atmosphere: Tense, foreboding
Skybox: Overcast, red haze
NPC Animation: Nervous, hurried movements
Audio Changes:

Music: Minor key, sparse instrumentation, tension
Ambience: Wind howls, distant Abyss whispers
SFX: Roots creaking, ominous tones
Mechanical Changes:

System	Crimson Effect
Combat	Enemies +10% damage
Magic	Soul magic costs +5 DSP
Healing	All healing -1 die step (d8→d6, d6→d4)
Corruption	Saves vs Corruption DC +2
Veilkeepers	Consultations cost +5 DSP, +2 Hollowing ticks
Shop	Prices +20%, rare items unavailable
NPC Availability	Some NPCs hide indoors, refuse travel
Faction	Bloomguard on high alert, Wildkin retreat
Loot	Drop rates -10%
Strategic Implications:

Best time to: Fortify, craft, plan next moves, social quests
Worst time to: Dungeon delving, boss fights, reckless exploration
Player Mindset: "Hunker down and prepare"
Crimson Sap Events (Random Triggers):

Abyss Scouts: Small patrols spawn in wilderness
Corruption Spread: Existing corruption patches grow
NPC Distress: Civilians ask for escort quests (high reward, dangerous)
Veil Tear: Random location gets temporary Abyss portal (timed event)
PHASE 2: SILVER SAP (Power & Volatility)
Duration: 3 in-game days (shorter = more impactful)

Narrative:

"The Everwood blazes. Silver Sap courses through every root —ancestral power unleashed. The Veil burns bright... but dangerously so. This is the fire that can consume."

Visual Changes:

Lighting: Bright silver-white, almost blindingly radiant
Colors: Emerald greens GLOW, hyper-saturated
Bioluminescence: 200% brightness, pulsing
Verdant Sigils: On Soulborn NPCs, glow intensely
Atmosphere: Electric, almost manic energy
Skybox: Clear, silver-edged clouds, aurora-like shimmer
Audio Changes:

Music: Triumphant, major key, full orchestra
Ambience: Energetic hum (like electricity), singing roots
SFX: Magical chimes, power surges
Mechanical Changes:

System	Silver Effect
Combat	Magic damage +1 die step (d8→d10, d10→d12)
Magic	Soul magic costs -5 DSP
Crits	Crit range expands (+2: instead of 20, now 18-20)
Sigils	Soulborn players get +1 to all rolls
Rebirth	New Soulborn NPCs appear (narrative events)
Veil	Veilkeeper visions clearer (+bonus intel)
Creatures	Rare enemies spawn (high XP, unique loot)
DSP Drain	DSP drains -3 per day (volatility cost)
Abyss	Incursions MORE likely (drawn to power)
Faction	Emerald Coven nervous, Bloomguard emboldened
Strategic Implications:

Best time to: Boss fights, major rituals, dungeon climaxes, power pushes
Risky: Overuse of magic (DSP crash post-Silver)
Player Mindset: "Strike while the iron is hot, but don't get greedy"
Silver Sap Events:

Unbinding Ceremony: NPCs celebrate, player can participate (gain permanent +1 bonus to chosen stat)
Rare Spawn: Legendary creatures appear (optional boss fights, huge rewards)
Hidden Paths: Secret areas reveal (glowing doorways, Veil-hidden caves)
DSP Surge: Global DSP +10 (one-time gift from Everwood)
The Silver Sap Trap:

Players often overcast during this phase (cheap magic!)
Then DSP crashes as volatility drains it
Followed immediately by Crimson Sap (vulnerability)
= Worst possible combo if not careful
Lesson: Restraint even during power phases
PHASE 3: BLUE SAP (Recovery)
Duration: 7 in-game days

Narrative:

"The Everwood exhales, spent but content. Blue Sap flows—
slow, nurturing, patient. The Veil mends. Verdance heals."

Visual Changes:

Lighting: Warm golden-green, soft
Colors: Gentle, saturated but not glaring
Bioluminescence: Steady, calm glow
New Growth: Visible blooms, saplings, fresh leaves
Atmosphere: Peaceful, hopeful
Skybox: Clear, gentle blue, soft clouds
Audio Changes:

Music: Pastoral, gentle strings, woodwinds
Ambience: Birds chirping, water trickling, wind through leaves
SFX: Contented sighs (Everwood breathing)
Mechanical Changes:

System	Blue Effect
Combat	Defensive bonuses (+2 to all saves)
Healing	All healing +1 die step (d6→d8, d8→d10)
DSP Regen	+5 DSP per day (natural recovery)
Guard	Regenerates +1 additional per turn
Debuffs	Last 50% shorter (2-turn poison = 1 turn)
Shop	Prices normal, full inventory available
Crafting	Bonuses (+10% success rate, better results)
NPC Social	More talkative, lore unlocks, faction quests
Diplomacy	Checks get +2 bonus
Enemies	Less aggressive, some neutral
Veilkeepers	Consultations cost normal DSP, normal ticks
Strategic Implications:

Best time to: Social quests, trading, preparing for Crimson
Good for: Mid-difficulty content, exploration, crafting
Player Mindset: "Recover resources, build relationships, prep"
Blue Sap Events:

Festival of Renewal: NPCs celebrate, shop sales (-20% prices)
Coven Teachings: Emerald Coven offers free skill training
Bloomguard Drills: Can spar with NPCs for XP (no death risk)
Nature's Bounty: Rare crafting materials spawn in wilderness
8.3 SAP CYCLE CALENDAR UI
HUD Display:

┌───────────────────────────────────────┐
│  SAP CYCLE CALENDAR                   │

│                                        │

│  • DSP drains -3/day                   │

Full Calendar View (Popup):
