Quest Planning Integration:

Quest: "Cleanse the Corruption at Hollowroot Depths"
Recommended Phase: SILVER SAP (magic bonus helps)

Current Phase: Crimson Sap (Day 3 of 5)

Options:
[Wait 3 days for Silver Sap] (optimal)
[Attempt now] (harder, but immediate)
[Delay until Blue Sap] (safer, but corruption spreads)

AI DM: "Waiting for Silver Sap would give you the 
magical edge needed. However, corruption grows 1 tile 
per day. By day 8 (Silver Sap day 2), it will have 
spread 5 additional tiles. Your call."
8.4 SAP PHASE TRANSITIONS (Cutscenes)
Each phase transition is marked by event:

Crimson → Silver Transition:
SCENE: Canopy of Life, Dawn

AI DM: "The sun breaks crimson clouds—no, *pierces* them. 
Light floods the Canopy in silver torrents. Everwood 
*shudders*—not in pain, but in *release*.

Bioluminescent fungi erupt in brilliance. Your Verdant 
Sigil burns (but doesn't hurt)—warm, electric. NPCs gasp, 
pointing at the sky.

Emerald Coven Seer: 'The Unbinding! Silver Sap flows! 
For three days, we are mighty—but guard against hubris.'"

[SILVER SAP BEGINS]
[Global DSP +10]
[All players/NPCs gain temporary +1 to rolls]
Mechanical Trigger: Automatic on Day 6

Silver → Blue Transition:
SCENE: Emerald Cascades, Sunset

AI DM: "The silver fire fades—not extinguished, but 
*gentled*. Everwood exhales, and Blue Sap wells from 
its roots like tears of relief.

The Cascades run cerulean. Flowers bloom overnight. 
A Soulborn child laughs—first time in days.

Wildkin Elder: 'The world remembers balance. Rest now.'"

[BLUE SAP BEGINS]
[DSP regeneration +5/day activated]
[Healing bonuses apply]
Blue → Crimson Transition:
SCENE: Whispering Veil, Midnight

AI DM: "The Veil... *shivers*. You feel it before you 
see it—a chill in the roots, a dimming of hope.

Crimson Sap begins to seep. The Veil thins. In the 
distance, an Abyss whisper: 'We hunger...'

Bloomguard Captain: 'Here we go again. Steel yourselves.'"

[CRIMSON SAP BEGINS]
[Combat difficulty increases]
[Warning: Abyss activity expected]
8.5 MANIPULATING SAP CYCLES (Advanced)
Players can force early phase transitions:

RITUAL: EARLY SILVER SAP
Trigger: Player initiates at Emerald Coven Sanctum
Requirements:

Must be during Blue Sap (cannot skip Crimson entirely)
Costs 40 DSP (massive drain)
Requires rare materials:
1× Viridian Crystal (pure)
5× Blooming Sap
10× Dreamroot
Ritual Process:

AI DM narrates ritual (interactive scene, player makes choices)
Skill checks required (Arcana DC 16, Insight DC 14)
On success: Silver Sap triggers immediately
On failure: DSP lost, no phase change, materials consumed
Consequences:

Immediate: Silver Sap for 3 days (as normal)
Long-term: Next Blue Sap phase is -2 days shorter (5 days instead of 7)
Risk: If DSP drops below 20 during ritual, permanent DSP max reduction to 90
Use Case: Emergency boss fight prep (nee

Continue

Feb 4
power NOW)

RITUAL: EXTEND BLUE SAP
Trigger: Player initiates during Blue Sap (Day 5-7)
Requirements:

20 DSP cost (moderate)
High Emerald Coven reputation (Trusted+)
Meditation skill check (DC 12)
Effect:

Blue Sap phase extended +2 days (7 → 9 days total)
Trade-off: Next Silver Sap phase is -1 day shorter (3 → 2 days)
Use Case: Need more recovery time, willing to sacrifice power phase

8.6 SAP CYCLE & STORY INTEGRATION
Main Story Beats Tied to Phases:

Act 1 Climax (Forced Crimson):

AI DM forces Crimson Sap phase for difficulty spike
"The Abyss has learned to time their strikes"
Player must fight boss during vulnerability phase (harder)
Act 2 Midpoint (Silver Sap Revelation):

During Silver Sap, Veilkeeper reveals true history
"The first Unbinding was a mistake—we broke the balance"
Moral complexity introduced during power phase
Act 3 Final Choice (Phase Selection):

Player chooses which phase to face final boss in:
Crimson: Hardest combat, but best "restraint" ending
Silver: Easier combat, but risks catastrophic DSP crash
Blue: Moderate combat, peaceful resolution possible
8.7 SAP CYCLE REPLAYABILITY
New Game+ Feature:

Can start campaign in ANY phase (choose at beginning)
Different dialogue opens (NPCs react to starting conditions)
Speedrun potential (Silver Sap start = fast power spike)
Challenge Modes:

Endless Crimson: Only Crimson Sap, no recovery
Volatile Silver: Only Silver Sap, constant DSP drain
Tranquil Blue: Only Blue Sap, enemies much weaker (pacifist run)
9. VEILKEEPER CONSULTATION MECHANICS
9.1 VEILKEEPER PHILOSOPHY
Core Concept:
"Knowledge costs lives. Every question you ask shortens a guardian's existence."

Design Goal:
Turn asking for help into a moral choice with permanent consequences.

Emotional Hook:
"I killed Eldara by asking too many times."

Unique in Gaming:
No other RPG makes hint/help systems a resource you can deplete permanently.

9.2 THE FIVE VEILKEEPERS
Each Veilkeeper specializes in a knowledge domain:

VEILKEEPER 1: SYLTHARA (Combat Wisdom)
Appearance: Ancient oak-like being, bark skin, glowing emerald eyes
Personality: Gentle, motherly, self-sacrificing
Voice: Warm but fading, like wind through leaves

Knowledge Domain:

Enemy weaknesses (vulnerabilities, resistances)
Combat tactics ("Flank from the east, high ground advantage")
Boss mechanics ("The Void Architect cannot be harmed while shields are active")
Optimal spell rotations
Hollowing Threshold: 10 ticks
Hollowing Visual: Bark cracking, leaves falling, voice weakening

Example Questions:

"What is the Void Architect's weakness?"
"How do I defeat the Sporecaller swarm?"
"Where should I position my party for this encounter?"
Example Answer:

"Child of roots... whispers The Void Architect's hunger is its downfall. It cannot resist Soul energy— bait it with false hope, let it overextend, then strike the exposed core. But beware... corruption spreads from its wounds."

Death Scene (If Hollowed):

AI DM: "Sylthara's bark splits completely. She doesn't 
scream—just... sighs. A final whisper: 'I gave what I 
could. Use it wisely.'

Her form crumbles to ash. The other Veilkeepers dim in 
mourning. You feel the weight of her absence—no more 
combat wisdom. Ever."

[Achievement Unlocked: "The Cost of Certainty"]
[Sylthara's knowledge domain LOCKED permanently]
VEILKEEPER 2: MORVEIN (Hidden Paths)
Appearance: Willowy, translucent, like mist given form
Personality: Cryptic, playful, riddler
Voice: Echoing, layered (multiple tones)

Knowledge Domain:

Secret areas (hidden caves, Veil-obscured doors)
Treasure locations ("Beneath the third root from Canopy's heart")
Shortcut passages
Puzzle solutions
Hollowing Threshold: 10 ticks
Hollowing Visual: Fading transparency, voice becoming single-tone

Example Questions:

"Where is the legendary Bloomwarden Bracelet?"
"How do I access the Veil-locked chamber?"
"Is there a faster route to Hollowroot Depths?"
Example Answer:

"Seek the third root from the heart-tree's embrace.
Where moonlight never touches, where Glintsilk webs
shimmer silver... there lies what you seek. But riddle
me this: What grows in darkness yet fears the Veil?"

[Player must solve riddle: Answer = Corruption]

VEILKEEPER 3: ELDUIN (Future Events)
Appearance: Eyes like shifting constellations, robes of starlight
Personality: Melancholic, burdened by foresight
Voice: Haunted, quiet, like distant thunder

Knowledge Domain:

Future consequences of player choices
Upcoming story events (warnings)
Faction outcomes ("If you ally with Thornbinders, Bloomguard will fracture")
Disaster prevention
Hollowing Threshold: 8 ticks (MOST FRAGILE)
Why Fragile: Seeing futures drains him faster

Hollowing Visual: Stars in eyes dim, robes turn to shadow

Example Questions:

"What happens if I kill the Abyss emissary?"
"Will this choice lead to disaster?"
"What does the future hold for Verdance?"
Example Answer (Cryptic):

"I see... three paths. In one, steel clashes and the
Canopy burns. In another, words forge uneasy peace,
but shadows linger. In the third... you are not there
to see the outcome."

[Player must interpret: War, Diplomacy, or Death]

Warning on Overuse:

"Elduin trembles. 'Stop... the futures... too many...
I cannot hold them all...' (Hollowing Ticks: 7/8)"

Death Scene:

AI DM: "Elduin's constellation eyes collapse—stars 
falling inward. His final words: 'The pattern breaks. 
I see... nothing. At last... peace.'

No more future sight. You're blind to consequences now."
VEILKEEPER 4: KAELTHAS (Ancient Lore)
Appearance: Stone-like, covered in runes, ageless
Personality: Stoic, patient, teacher
Voice: Deep, resonant, like earth shifting

Knowledge Domain:

Historical events (Soul War details, Verdance origins)
Artifact identification ("This relic is the Key of Unbinding")
Magic theory
Lore revelations
Hollowing Threshold: 12 ticks (MOST RESILIENT)
Why Resilient: Thousands of years old, strong pattern

Hollowing Visual: Runes fading, stone cracking

Example Questions:

"What is this artifact I found?"
"What really happened during the first Silver Sap Unbinding?"
"How does the Veil actually work?"
Example Answer:

"The first Unbinding was desperation, not wisdom. Your
ancestors, starving for soul energy, ripped the Veil
wider than nature intended. The Abyss responded—not
with malice, but with hunger. Both sides victims of
imbalance."

VEILKEEPER 5: VIRELDA (Corruption Expert)
Appearance: Half-tree, half-shadow, corruption visible but contained
Personality: Grim, pragmatic, survivor
Voice: Raspy, like burning wood

Knowledge Domain:

Corruption mechanics (how it spreads, how to cleanse)
Abyss enemy intel ("Soul Siphon drains 10 DSP per hit")
Hollowing process (ironically, she knows her own death)
Anti-corruption rituals
Hollowing Threshold: 10 ticks
Hollowing Visual: Corruption overtakes containment, shadow spreads

Example Questions:

"How do I cleanse this corruption zone?"
"What are the Abyss truly?"
"Can Hollowing be reversed?"
Example Answer:

"Corruption is not evil—it's hunger. The Abyss starves. Your Everwood hoards. Both extremes breed suffering. To cleanse corruption, feed it controlled energy—Burn Magic works, but sparingly. Starve it, it festers. Overfeed it, it explodes."

Death Scene:

AI DM: "Virelda's containment fails. Shadow consumes her 
tree-form. But she smiles: 'Ironic. Spent my existence 
studying death, yet surprised by my own. Goodbye, child.'

Corruption knowledge lost. You're on your own now."
9.3 CONSULTATION PROCESS (Step-by-Step)
Step 1: Approach Veilkeeper Grove

Located in sacred area (Whispering Veil, Emerald Cascades)
Atmospheric shift (quieter, ethereal)
Music changes (spiritual, haunting)
Step 2: Emerald Coven Seer Warning

AI DM: "Seer Vael intercepts you at the grove's edge.

Vael: 'You seek the Veilkeepers again. I must warn you—
Sylthara has answered 3 times already. Each question 
drains her. At 10, she Hollows... and we lose her forever. 
Are you certain?'"

[Yes, I need answers] [No, I'll manage without]
Step 3: Select Veilkeeper

UI presents 5 portraits:

┌─────────────────────────────────────────┐
│  CHOOSE VEILKEEPER TO CONSULT           │
├─────────────────────────────────────────┤
│  SYLTHARA (Combat Wisdom)               │
│  Hollowing: ███░░░░░░░ (3/10)          │
│  Cost: 10 DSP (+5 Crimson Sap)          │
│                                          │
│  MORVEIN (Hidden Paths)                 │
│  Hollowing: █░░░░░░░░░░ (1/10)         │
│  Cost: 10 DSP                            │
│                                          │
│  ELDUIN (Future Events)                 │
│  Hollowing: █████░░░ (5/8) ⚠️ FRAGILE  │
│  Cost: 10 DSP                            │
│                                          │
│  [Continue] [Cancel]                     │
└─────────────────────────────────────────┘
Step 4: Ask Question

Two modes:

A) Freeform Text Input:

Player types: "What is the Void Architect's weakness?"

AI DM processes question, determines relevance to 
Sylthara's domain, generates answer using Veilkeeper's 
personality and lore knowledge.
B) Multiple Choice Menu:

SYLTHARA (Combat Wisdom):
1. "What are the Void Architect's weaknesses?"
2. "How do I defeat Sporecaller swarms?"
3. "Is there a tactical advantage I'm missing?"
4. [Ask something else] (freeform)
Step 5: Veilkeeper Responds

AI DM: "Sylthara's bark glows faintly. Her voice enters 
your mind—not words, but *patterns*. You see the Void 
Architect's core exposed, feel its hunger for Soul energy.

Sylthara: 'It cannot resist... feed false hope... then 
strike core... beware corruption spread...'

She dims slightly. You feel the weight of what was given."

[COST APPLIED: DSP -10, Hollowing Tick +1]
[Sylthara: 4/10 ticks]
Step 6: Knowledge Gained (Mechanical)

Player gets tangible benefit:

Enemy weakness revealed (UI update: "Void Architect: WEAK to Soul magic")
Map marker added (for hidden location questions)
Dialogue option unlocked (for future event questions)
Recipe/ritual instructions (for lore questions)
AND

Hollowing tick recorded (permanent damage)

9.4 HOLLOWING MECHANIC (Death Clock)
Hollowing Ticks:

Each consultation: +1 tick (or +2 during Crimson Sap)
Threshold varies: Elduin (8), Sylthara/Morvein/Virelda (10), Kaelthas (12)
Permanent and irreversible (no resurrection)
Hollowing Visual Progression:

0-3 Ticks (Healthy):

Veilkeeper vibrant, full voice, eager to help
4-6 Ticks (Strained):

Slight dimming, voice weaker
NPCs comment: "Sylthara seems tired"
Warning tooltip: "⚠️ Approaching midpoint"
7-9 Ticks (Critical):

Severe visual decay (bark cracking, light fading)
Voice barely audible
Warning popup every consultation:
  ⚠️⚠️ CRITICAL WARNING ⚠️⚠️
  
  Sylthara is near Hollowing (9/10 ticks).
  ONE more question will kill her permanently.
  
  Are you ABSOLUTELY CERTAIN?
  
  [Yes, I need this answer] [No, I'll find another way]
10+ Ticks (Death):

Trigger death scene (unique per Veilkeeper)
Permanent lockout of that knowledge domain
Achievement unlocked (bittersweet)
NPC mourning (Emerald Coven holds funeral)
World state change (one less voice in the Veil)
9.5 STRATEGIC LAYER (Player Decisions)
Three Playstyles Emerge:

1. The Hoarder (Preservation)
Strategy: Never or rarely consult Veilkeepers
Difficulty: Much harder (no hints, trial-and-error)
Reward:
All Veilkeepers survive
Achievement: "Preserved Wisdom"
Special ending dialogue (Veilkeepers thank you)
Moral high ground
Quote from player:

"I refused to ask for help. It made the game brutally
hard, but when I beat the final boss without killing
a single Veilkeeper, I felt like I truly honored the
theme of restraint."

2. The Spender (Tactical Use)
Strategy: Consult only when truly stuck
Sweet Spot: ~15-20 total consultations across all Veilkeepers
Result:
1-2 Veilkeepers might Hollow (usually Elduin, most fragile)
Balanced difficulty
Guilt but manageable
Quote from player:

"I lost Elduin halfway through. It hurt. But his
sacrifice got me through the Abyss ambush. I made
his death count."

3. The Glutton (Power Gamer)
Strategy: Spam consultations, abuse for every advantage
Result:
3-4 Veilkeepers dead by endgame
Easy combat (full intel)
Heavy narrative punishment (NPCs hate you, bad ending)
Achievement: "Hollow Victory" (beat game but killed all Veilkeepers)
Quote from player:

"I asked every question I could. The game became trivial.
But the ending... god. Seer Vael looked at me with such
disappointment. 'They gave everything for you, and you
took without thought.' That hit harder than any death."

9.6 VEILKEEPER DEATH CONSEQUENCES
Immediate:

Knowledge domain locked (can't get that type of intel anymore)
DSP -10 (grief drains Everwood)
All other Veilkeepers gain +1 Hollowing tick (shared trauma)
Faction Reactions:

Emerald Coven: -15 reputation ("You were reckless")
Bloomguard: -5 reputation ("We needed their wisdom")
Thornbinders: 0 (they don't care, pragmatic)
NPC Dialogue Changes:

Before Sylthara's Death:
NPC: "Sylthara's wisdom guides us all."

After:
NPC: "You... you killed her. With your questions. 
      I know you didn't mean to, but... she's gone."
World State:

Whispering Veil dims permanently (fewer Veilkeepers = weaker Veil)
Abyss incursions +5% frequency (sensing weakness)
Ending Impact:

0 deaths: "Wisdom Preserved" ending (best moral outcome)
1-2 deaths: "Sacrifice Necessary" ending (bittersweet)
3+ deaths: "Hollow Victory" ending (won, but at what cost?)
5 deaths: "Silence" ending (all Veilkeepers gone, Veil collapses)
9.7 ADVANCED VEILKEEPER MECHANICS
FREE CONSULTATION (One-Time)
Trigger: Backstory choice "Emerald Coven Initiate"

Benefit:

First consultation to ANY Veilkeeper costs 0 DSP, 0 Hollowing ticks
Represents: "Your bond with the Coven grants you one question as gift"
Strategic Use: Save for crucial moment (boss fight intel, endgame question)

VEILKEEPER COMMUNION RITUAL
Unlocks: Emerald Coven Exalted reputation

Function:

Can ask ONE question to a dead Veilkeeper
Costs 50 DSP (massive)
Requires rare materials (Dreamroot ×20, Viridian Crystal ×3)
One-time only per Veilkeeper
Limitations:

Answer is cryptic (ghosts speak in riddles)
No Hollowing tick (already dead)
Only works if you genuinely regret their death (AI DM checks player behavior)
Use Case:

Resurrect Elduin's foresight for final boss
OR get one last answer from Sylthara after you realized you needed her
VEILKEEPER MEMORIAL SYSTEM
Function:

When Veilkeeper dies, a memorial tree appears in grove
Player can leave offerings (flowers, Dreamroot, DSP infusions)
Offerings give small buffs:
Sylthara's Memorial: +5% combat XP gain
Morvein's Memorial: +10% treasure find rate
Elduin's Memorial: Occasional vague future hints (dreams)
Emotional Impact:

Visiting memorial triggers sad music
NPCs leave offerings too (world mourns with you)
Late-game quest: "Restore the Grove" (revive Veilkeeper spirits as echoes, not full power)
10. FACTION REPUTATION SYSTEM
10.1 FACTION PHILOSOPHY
Core Concept:
"Your actions ripple across all of Verdance. Every choice shifts alliances."

Design Goal:
Multi-axis reputation (not simple good/evil). Pleasing one faction often angers another.

Inspiration:

New Vegas (faction conflict)
Dragon Age (companion approval)
Skyrim (hold allegiances)
Anti-Pattern:
Single karma meter. We want complex webs of loyalty.

10.2 THE SIX FACTIONS
FACTION 1: BLOOMGUARD (Defenders of Verdance)
Core Values:

Protection above all
Restraint (don't overuse DSP)
Duty to civilians
Transparency
Likes:

Defending civilians
Completing patrol quests
Using defensive abilities in combat
Refusing to overcast (low DSP usage)
Honesty in dialogue
Hates:

Civilian casualties
Recklessness with DSP
Cowardice (fleeing combat)
Lying to authority
Key NPCs:

Captain Taryn Ironroot: Gruff leader, values discipline
Sentinel Lyris Ashenblade: Player's early mentor, compassionate
Faction Headquarters: Canopy Barracks

Reputation Tiers:

Tier	Rep Range	Benefits
Exalted	+35 to +50	Unique armor set, safe house, Bloomguard ally summon (1/day)
Trusted	+20 to +34	10% shop discount, Root Sentinel Halberd blueprint, priority quests
Known	+10 to +19	Standard prices, normal interactions
Wary	-9 to +9	Neutral (default starting)
Hostile	-29 to -10	Refused entry to barracks, harassment, higher prices
Hunted	≤ -30	Kill-on-sight, bounties placed
Exalted Quest: "The Last Stand"

Defend Canopy of Life from massive Abyss assault
Success: Promoted to Honorary Captain, unique dialogue options
FACTION 2: EMERALD COVEN (Spiritual Guardians)
Core Values:

Balance (DSP conservation)
Ritual respect
Veilkeeper protection
Knowledge over violence
Likes:

Conserving DSP (winning fights without magic)
Consulting Veilkeepers wisely (not excessively)
Completing Coven rituals
Respecting sacred sites
Diplomatic solutions
Hates:

DSP abuse (letting it drop below 30)
Killing Veilkeepers through overuse
Desecrating sacred sites
Soul crimes (extracting souls from living beings)
Key NPCs:

Seer Vael: High priestess, patient teacher, warns of consequences
Initiate Kaelen: Young coven member, idealistic
Faction Headquarters: Emerald Sanctum (in Cascades)

Exalted Reward:

Ritual of Clarity: Free Veilkeeper consultation (1/week, no Hollowing)
Sap Capacitor Totem: Stores 15 DSP, recharges in Blue Sap
Hostile Consequence:

Coven refuses to cleanse corruption (you're on your own)
Veilkeepers won't speak to you
FACTION 3: THORNBINDERS (Intelligence Network)
Core Values:

Secrecy
Prevention (stop threats before they manifest)
Control information
Pragmatism (ends justify means)
Likes:

Stealth gameplay
Gathering intel (interrogations, eavesdropping)
Preemptive strikes
Completing shadow ops
Lying convincingly
Hates:

Public spectacles (drawing attention)
Loose talk (revealing secrets)
Naivety (trusting enemies)
Bloomguard transparency
Key NPCs:

Spymaster Kael Thornweave: Cynical, effective, morally grey
Agent Morvain: Silent operative, deadliest fighter in Verdance
Faction Headquarters: Hidden (revealed at Trusted tier)

Exalted Reward:

Shadow Step Spell: Tier 2 teleport (short range, leaves no trace)
Stealth Cloak: +5 to Stealth rolls, invisible in dim light
Criminality Reduction Service: -20% criminality for gold
Conflict with Bloomguard:

Siding with Thornbinders for preemptive strike → Bloomguard -10 rep
They want transparency; Thornbinders need secrecy
FACTION 4: WILDKIN PACT (Nature Protectors)
Core Values:

Wilderness preservation
Animal welfare
Freedom (oppose cages, restrictions)
Ecological balance
Likes:

Avoiding Sacred Fire zones (don't burn forests)
Freeing caged animals
Plant-based diet choices (optional dialogue)
Completing nature quests (regrow flora, cleanse pollution)
Hates:

Burn Magic abuse (scorched earth tactics)
Hunting endangered species
Over-harvesting resources
Caging beasts
Key NPCs:

Elder Sylvara Rootsong: Druid-like leader, speaks for trees
Ranger Thalos: Gruff hunter, teaches survival
Faction Headquarters: Wildkin Grove (deep forest)

Exalted Reward:

Beast Bond Companion: Permanent animal ally (wolf, owl, or stag)
Beast Form Transformation: Temporary (1/day, +5 Might, +10 Speed)
Nature's Bounty: Rare crafting materials spawn near you
Conflict with Sporecallers:

Wildkin wants living forests
Sporecallers use controlled decay
Using decay magic → Wildkin -5 rep
FACTION 5: SPORECALLERS' VANGUARD (Renewal Through Decay)
Core Values:

Death is natural
Decay feeds rebirth
Fungal network (collective intelligence)
Pragmatic cleanup
Likes:

Using decay/poison magic
Accepting death (don't resurrect unnecessarily)
Cleaning corruption with fungal methods
Completing rot quests (clear infected areas)
Hates:

Necromancy (unnatural preservation)
Wasting corpses (not harvesting materials)
Fire (destroys spores, prevents decay)
Key NPCs:

Mycologist Varl: Creepy but wise, understands spores
Sporecaller Shaman: Fungal-covered NPC, speaks in spore patterns
Faction Headquarters: Mycelium Nexus (underground fungal network)

Exalted Reward:

Decay Mastery Spell: Tier 3, cleanses corruption + heals (paradoxical)
Mycelium Fast Travel: Use fungal nodes to teleport between locations
Spore Immunity: Cannot be poisoned
Conflict with Wildkin:

Sporecallers use controlled burns → Wildkin angry
Wildkin preserves life → Sporecallers see as stagnation
FACTION 6: SAPLING CONSORTIUM (Trade Guild)
Core Values:

Commerce
Prosperity
Fair trade
Resource stability
Likes:

Buying goods (spending gold)
Completing trade quests (escort caravans, open routes)
Economic stability (high DSP = stable trade)
Hates:

Theft
Boycotts (refusing to trade)
Destabilizing markets (flooding with loot)
Key NPCs:

Merchant-Prince Aldric: Wealthy, shrewd, politically neutral
Trader Mira: Common merchant, always has side quests
Faction Headquarters: Verdant Exchange (marketplace)

Exalted Reward:

25% Discount: All shops in Verdance
Exclusive Legendary Items: Only available at Exalted tier
Investment System: Invest gold, earn passive income
Conflict with Emerald Coven:

Consortium wants profitable resource extraction
Coven wants conservation
Over-harvesting quests → Coven -5 rep
10.3 REPUTATION MECHANICS
Reputation Range: -50 to +50 (per faction)

Starting Reputation:

All factions: 0 (Wary/Neutral)
Except: Faction matching your class gets +5 (Known tier)
Example: Bloomguard class → Bloomguard faction starts at +5
Reputation Gains/Losses:

Action Type	Rep Change
Complete faction quest (minor)	+5
Complete faction quest (major)	+10 to +15
Side with faction in conflict	+10
Betray faction trust	-20
Kill faction member	-30 (instant Hunted)
Donate gold/materials	+1 per 50g
Multi-Faction Events:

Example: Thornbinder Preemptive Strike Quest

Thornbinders want to assassinate Abyss scouts before attack.
Bloomguard want to capture them for interrogation.

Player Choice:
1. [Side with Thornbinders] → Assassinate scouts
   Result: Thornbinders +10, Bloomguard -10
   
2. [Side with Bloomguard] → Capture for interrogation
   Result: Bloomguard +10, Thornbinders -5
   
3. [Compromise] → Persuasion check (DC 16)
   Success: Both get +5 (difficult but possible)
   Failure: Both get -5 (failed mediation)
   
4. [Ignore both] → Do nothing
   Result: Both -3 (disappointed)
Reputation Decay:

Rep does NOT decay over time (permanent)
Can only change through actions
10.4 FACTION CONFLICT MATRIX
Some factions oppose each other:

Faction	Opposes	Reason
Bloomguard	Thornbinders	Transparency vs Secrecy
Wildkin Pact	Sporecallers	Preservation vs Decay
Emerald Coven	Sapling Consortium	Conservation vs Profit
Mechanical Enforcement:

If you reach Exalted with one faction, opposing faction caps at Known (max +19)
Can't be Exalted with BOTH sides of conflict
Forces player to choose political alignment
Example:

Player reaches Exalted with Bloomguard (+40 rep).

Thornbinders reputation capped at +19 (Known tier).
Cannot access Thornbinder Exalted rewards.

AI DM: "Spymaster Kael eyes you coldly. 'You're too 
close to the Bloomguard. We cannot trust you with our 
deepest secrets.'"
10.5 FACTION QUESTS (Examples)
BLOOMGUARD QUEST CHAIN:
Quest 1: "Patrol the Borderlands" (Level 2)

Simple escort quest (guard caravan from Abyss scouts)
Reward: +5 rep, 100g, Bloomguard Tabard (cosmetic)
Quest 2: "The Missing Sentinel" (Level 4)

Investigate disappearance of Bloomguard patrol
Discover they were captured by Abyss
Choice: Rescue (combat) OR Negotiate (diplomacy)
Reward: +10 rep, Sentinel's Blade (uncommon weapon)
Quest 3: "Trial by Honor" (Level 7)

Bloomguard officer accused of corruption
Investigate evidence (find truth)
Choice: Exonerate (if innocent) OR Condemn (if guilty)
Moral complexity: Truth isn't clear-cut (AI DM presents ambiguity)
Reward: +15 rep, unlock Exalted tier
EMERALD COVEN QUEST CHAIN:
Quest 1: "Ritual of Awakening" (Level 3)

Assist with Silver Sap ceremony
Gather materials (Blooming Sap, Dreamroot)
Reward: +5 rep, learn Tier 2 spell
Quest 2: "The Hollowing Grove" (Level 5)

Investigate why Hollow Trees are spreading
Discover corruption source (mini-dungeon)
Cleanse with Burn Magic (costs DSP)
Reward: +10 rep, DSP +15 (domain healed)
Quest 3: "Vael's Burden" (Level 8)

Seer Vael reveals she's considering Hollowing herself (mercy for Everwood)
Player must convince her life matters OR accept her sacrifice
Moral weight: Her death restores +30 DSP permanently
Reward: Variable (depends on choice)
THORNBINDER QUEST CHAIN:
Quest 1: "Eyes in the Dark" (Level 3)

Plant surveillance devices in Abyss-controlled zone
Stealth gameplay (avoid detection)
Reward: +5 rep, Stealth Cloak
Quest 2: "The Double Agent" (Level 6)

Thornbinder suspects mole in Bloomguard
Gather evidence (eavesdrop, search quarters)
Present findings to Spymaster Kael
Twist: Evidence is fabricated (test of loyalty)
Choice: Expose innocent OR stay silent
Reward: +10 rep IF you call out the test (Kael respects intelligence)
Quest 3: "Shadow War" (Level 9)

Assassinate Abyss leadership (point of no return)
OR sabotage mission and warn Abyss (if doing diplomacy ending)
Massive rep swing based on choice
10.6 FACTION ENDINGS (Epilogue Impact)
In Epilogue, factions' fates depend on player's reputation:

BLOOMGUARD:

Exalted: Named Honorary Captain, Canopy defenses strongest, peace maintained
Hostile: Disbanded after player's betrayal, Canopy vulnerable
EMERALD COVEN:

Exalted: Veilkeepers survive (if player didn't Hollow them), Veil strong
Hostile: Coven exiled, Veil weakens permanently
THORNBINDERS:

Exalted: Intelligence network prevents future Abyss attacks
Hostile: Faction goes rogue, becomes new threat
WILDKIN PACT:

Exalted: Forests thrive, beast populations recover
Hostile: Wilderness becomes hostile to all Verdance
SPORECALLERS:

Exalted: Controlled decay prevents corruption spread
Hostile: Mycelium network turns parasitic
SAPLING CONSORTIUM:

Exalted: Economic boom, Verdance prospers
Hostile: Trade collapse, poverty spreads
Balanced Approach:

If player stays neutral (all factions Wary/Known), world remains stable but unremarkable
"You changed nothing, for better or worse"
11. CRIMINALITY & LAW ENFORCEMENT SYSTEM
11.1 CRIMINALITY PHILOSOPHY
Core Concept:
"Verdance has laws. Breaking them has consequences beyond faction reputation."

Design Goal:
Separate legal standing from faction politics. You can be Exalted with Bloomguard but still a wanted criminal.

Inspiration:

Skyrim (bounty system)
Red Dead Redemption 2 (honor vs law)
Disco Elysium (detective consequences)
11.2 CRIMINALITY MECHANICS
Criminality Percentage: 0% → 100%

How It Increases:

Crime	Criminality Gain	Notes
Theft (witnessed)	+3%	Stealing from shops, homes
Assault (unprovoked)	+5%	Attacking civilians
Murder (civilian)	+20%	Killing innocent NPC
Soul Extraction	+30%	Using forbidden magic
Necromancy	+50%	Raising dead (ultimate taboo)
Veilkeeper Tampering	+40%	Attempting to harm Veilkeepers
"Witnessed" Mechanic:

If crime has no witnesses → +0% criminality
Thornbinder skill: "Shadow" (can hide bodies, erase evidence)
Stealth kills don't count IF no one sees
How It Decreases:

Method	Criminality Loss	Cost
Time passing	-1% per day	Free (slow)
Faction quests (redemption)	-5%	Complete assigned quest
Bribe Thornbinders	-10%	500g
Sacred Ritual (Emerald Coven)	-20%	One-time only
Turn self in	-50%	Serve jail time (7 days)
11.3 ENFORCEMENT TIERS
Criminality Thresholds:

% Range	Status	Enforcement
0-10%	Clean	No issues, normal gameplay
11-25%	Watched	Guards alert, occasional stops for questioning
26-45%	Suspect	Patrols follow you, searches, restricted area access
46-65%	Wanted	Bounty hunters spawn (3-4 per day)
66-85%	Hunted	Kill-on-sight in cities, Bloomguard actively pursue
86-100%	Enemy of Verdance	Entire domain hostile, flee or fight everyone
Bounty Hunters:

Scale with player level (challenging fights)
Drop good loot (incentive to fight rather than flee)
Can be bribed (Charisma check, DC 16, costs 200g)
11.4 ARREST SYSTEM
If caught (low-medium criminality):

AI DM: "Bloomguard Sentinel corners you in alley.

Sentinel: 'You're under suspicion for theft. Come quietly 
or face judgment.'"

Options:
1. [Surrender] → Arrested, taken to holding
2. [Bribe] (200g) → Charisma check (DC 14)
   Success: Sentinel looks away
   Failure: Arrested + Bloomguard -10 rep
3. [Fight] → Combat, but killing guard = +20% criminality
4. [Flee] → Agility check (DC 15)
   Success: Escape, +5% criminality
   Failure: Arrested
Arrest Consequences:

Jail Time: 1-7 days (based on severity)
Confiscation: Lose 25% of carried gold
Criminality: -10% (served time)
Faction: Bloomguard +5 rep (respected law)
Jail Gameplay:

Can attempt escape (lockpicking, bribe guard)
OR serve time (skip ahead, world continues)
NPCs visit (dialogue scenes, lore)
11.5 CRIMINALITY & FACTION INTERACTIONS
Faction Stances on Criminality:

BLOOMGUARD: Strictly enforce law

High criminality → auto-hostile (regardless of reputation)
Will arrest you even if Trusted tier
THORNBINDERS: Tolerate crime IF discreet

High criminality from PUBLIC crimes → negative
High criminality from unseen crimes → neutral (they respect competence)
EMERALD COVEN: Context matters

Petty theft → mild disapproval
Soul crimes → extreme hostility (values-based)
WILDKIN / SPORECALLERS / CONSORTIUM: Mostly indifferent

Only care if crimes affect them directly
11.6 CRIMINAL PLAYSTYLES
Three Approaches:

THE SAINT (0-10% Criminality):
Never steal, kill, or break laws
Hardest economically (can't loot freely)
Best faction standings
Achievement: "Exemplar of Restraint"
THE PRAGMATIST (11-45% Criminality):
Steals when needed, but avoids murder
Balanced risk/reward
Most common playthrough
THE OUTLAW (46-100% Criminality):
Steal, kill, chaos
Hunted constantly (very hard)
Unique dialogue (NPCs fear you)
Achievement: "Enemy of the State"
12. PROGRESSION & LEVELING (CONTINUED)
(See Section 5.3 for core leveling. This expands.)

12.1 ALTERNATIVE PROGRESSION (Non-Combat XP)
Discovery XP:

Finding secret areas: +25 XP
Discovering lore collectibles: +15 XP
First visit to new location: +10 XP
Social XP:

Winning debate/persuasion checks: +20 XP
Resolving conflicts peacefully: +50 XP
Befriending key NPCs: +30 XP
Crafting XP:

Creating new item for first time: +10 XP
Mastering recipe (perfect quality): +25 XP
Goal: Reward non-violent playstyles equally.

12.2 SKILL MASTERY SYSTEM
At Rank 4 (Master) in any skill, unlock Mastery Perk:

Melee Combat Mastery:

"Blade Dancer": Can attack twice with 1 AP (once per combat)
Soul Magic Mastery:

"Arcane Ascendance": Tier 3 spells cost -10 DSP additionally
Stealth Mastery:

"Shadow Form": Become invisible for 2 turns (1/day)
Persuasion Mastery:

"Silver Tongue": Auto-succeed on one persuasion check per day
13. EQUIPMENT & INVENTORY
13.1 EQUIPMENT SLOTS
7 Equipment Slots:

Main Hand (weapon)
Off Hand (shield, weapon, focus)
Armor (chest piece)
Trinket (magical accessory)
Quick Slot 1 (potion/bomb)
Quick Slot 2 (potion/bomb)
Ammo (arrows, if using bow)
13.2 WEAPON TYPES & STATS
Melee Weapons:

Type	Damage Die	Special	Weight
Sword	1d8	Balanced	Medium
Axe	1d10	-1 to hit, +2 damage	Heavy
Dagger	1d6	+2 to hit, can throw	Light
Spear	1d10	Reach (attack from 2 tiles away)	Medium
Club	1d8	Can stun (10% chance)	Medium
Ranged Weapons:

Type	Damage Die	Range	Special
Bow	1d10	8 tiles	Uses arrows (ammo)
Crossbow	1d12	6 tiles	Slow (can't attack + move same turn)
Thrown	1d6	4 tiles	Consumable (daggers, axes)
13.3 ARMOR TYPES
Type	Guard Bonus	Evasion Penalty	Speed Penalty
Light (Leather, Glintsilk)	+5 Guard	0	0
Medium (Barkplate, Rootweave)	+10 Guard	-1 Evasion	0
Heavy (Viridian Plate, Blooming Sap)	+15 Guard	-2 Evasion	-1 Speed
Trade-off: More armor = harder to dodge, slower movement

13.4 RARITY TIERS
5 Rarity Levels:

Common (White)
Basic stats, no special effects
Example: Iron Sword (1d8 damage)
Uncommon (Green)
+1 bonus or minor effect
Example: Thornfang Blade (1d8, inflicts Bleed)
Rare (Blue)
+2 bonus or strong effect
Example: Viridian Spear (1d10+2, crit bursts for +1d6)
Legendary (Purple)
+3 bonus, multiple effects, unique
Example: Warden's Everwood Blade (1d12+2, heals on crit, soulbound)
Mythic (Gold)
Artifact-tier, gamechanging
Example: Eldara's Memorial Armor (+3 AC, +20 Guard, auto-casts Soul Shield at 10 HP)
Only 3-5 Mythic items in entire game
Loot Distribution:

Common: 60% of drops
Uncommon: 25%
Rare: 10%
Legendary: 4%
Mythic: 1% (boss-only)
13.5 INVENTORY SYSTEM
Carry Capacity:

10 + (Might × 5) items
Example:

Might 2 → 20 item limit
Might 5 → 35 item limit
Inventory UI:

Overflow:

If over capacity: Cannot pick up new items
Must drop or sell existing items
Stash:

Can store unlimited items at Canopy of Life (home base)
Access anytime in town
14. CRAFTING & ECONOMY
14.1 CRAFTING SYSTEM
Three Crafting Stations:

Bloomguard Forge (Canopy Barracks)
Weapons & Armor
NPC: Blacksmith Garren
Emerald Coven Sanctum (Cascades)
Magic Items & Potions
NPC: Alchemist Seris
Sapling Workshop (Verdant Exchange)
Utility Items & Upgrades
NPC: Tinker Mira
14.2 CRAFTING PROCESS
Step 1: Acquire Blueprint

Find in world (loot, quest reward)
Purchase from merchants
Unlock via Veilkeeper consultation
Step 2: Gather Materials

Harvested from environment (Everwood shards from trees)
Dropped from enemies (Corrupted Essence from Abyss)
Purchased from merchants
Step 3: Craft at Station

Requires gold fee (10-500g based on item tier)
Optional: Skill check (Crafting skill, better results on success)
Time cost (immediate in-game, but counts as action)
Step 4: Receive Item

Quality depends on skill check:
Failure: Item created but -1 to stats
Success: Normal item
Critical Success (nat 20): +1 bonus ("Masterwork" quality)
14.3 EXAMPLE CRAFTING RECIPES
WEAPON: Thornfang Blade (Uncommon)

Materials:
Everwood Shards ×5
Thorn Vines ×3
Viridian Crystal Fragment ×1
Gold Cost: 100g
Crafting Skill DC: 12
Result: 1d8 damage, inflicts Bleed (d4, 2 turns)
ARMOR: Barkplate Harness (Uncommon)

Materials:
Everwood Bark ×10
Rootweave Fibers ×5
Gold Cost: 150g
Crafting Skill DC: 14
Result: +10 Guard, +1 AC
POTION: Everspring Potion (Common)

Materials:
Blue Sap ×1
Dreamroot ×2
Gold Cost: 25g
Crafting Skill DC: 10
Result: Restore 2d8+2 HP
MAGIC ITEM: Sap Capacitor Totem (Rare)

Materials:
Viridian Crystal (pure) ×1
Blooming Sap ×10
Ancient Runestone ×1
Gold Cost: 500g
Crafting Skill DC: 18
Result: Stores 15 DSP, recharges in Blue Sap
14.4 UPGRADE SYSTEM
Can upgrade existing weapons/armor:

Process:

Take item + materials to forge
Costs gold + rare materials
Adds +1 to damage/AC (max +3)
Example:

Everwood Saber (base: 1d8)
  ↓ (Upgrade +1: 100g, 5 Viridian Fragments)
Everwood Saber +1 (1d8+1)
  ↓ (Upgrade +2: 300g, 10 Viridian Fragments)
Everwood Saber +2 (1d8+2)
  ↓ (Upgrade +3: 500g, Viridian Crystal ×1)
Everwood Saber +3 (1d8+3, CAPPED)
Prevents infinite scaling (cap at +3).

14.5 ECONOMY (GOLD & PRICES)
Gold Sources:

Enemy drops: 5-50g per fight
Quest rewards: 50-500g
Selling loot: 50% of item value
Treasure chests: 20-200g
Gold Sinks:

Shop purchases (potions, equipment)
Crafting fees
Bribes (guards, NPCs)
Faction donations
Ritual costs (early Silver Sap, etc.)
Shop Prices (Base):

Item Type	Price Range
Consumables (potions)	25-100g
Common weapons	50-150g
Uncommon equipment	200-500g
Rare equipment	1,000-3,000g
Legendary (if available)	5,000-10,000g
Price Modifiers:

Charisma 4+: -10%
Sapling Consortium Exalted: -25%
Low DSP (crisis): +20%
Crimson Sap phase: +20%
15. MAGIC SYSTEM (SOUL MAGIC)
(See Section 6.8 for spell list. This expands lore/mechanics.)

15.1 SOUL MAGIC PHILOSOPHY
What It Is:

Not "mana" — it's channeling ancestral soul energy from Everwood
Soulborn have Verdant Sigils (physical conduits)
Non-Soulborn can learn magic but it's harder (costs +2 DSP)
How It Looks:

Emerald-green energy (primary)
Silver wisps (during Silver Sap)
Black-green corruption (Abyss magic, forbidden)
Casting Animation:

Verdant Sigil glows
Energy flows from ground (roots) up through body
Hands/staff emit emerald light
VFX projectile/aura appears
15.2 SPELL TIERS
TIER 1 (1 AP, 5 DSP):

Basic utility
Examples: Soul Shield, Verdant Grasp, Bloom Step
TIER 2 (2 AP, 10-15 DSP):

Combat-focused
Examples: Burn Magic, Root Sentinel, Ancestor's Whisper
TIER 3 (3 AP, 20-30 DSP):

Gamechangers, ultimate abilities
Examples: Sap Surge, Hollow Strike, Verdant Nexus
15.3 SPELL LEARNING SYSTEM
How to Learn Spells:

Level-Up: Choose 1 new spell at levels 3, 5, 7, 9
Spell Scrolls: Find in world, consume to learn (one-use)
NPC Teachers: Emerald Coven offers lessons (gold cost)
Veilkeeper: Consult Kaelthas for ancient spells
Spell Limit:

Can know up to 10 spells total
Forces specialization (can't learn everything)
Can "forget" spell to make room (at Coven, costs 50g)
15.4 FORBIDDEN MAGIC
Three Forbidden Spells (unlockable but costly):

1. NECROMANCY: Raise Dead
Cost: 40 DSP
Effect: Resurrect enemy corpse as undead ally (5 turns)
Consequence:
+50% Criminality (instant Wanted status)
Emerald Coven -30 rep (soul crime)
Sporecallers -20 rep (perverts decay)
Veil tears (permanent -5 max DSP)
Use Case: Desperate situation, worth the cost

2. SOUL EXTRACTION: Harvest Soul
Cost: 30 DSP
Effect: Kill target, gain +20 DSP from their essence
Consequence:
+30% Criminality
Emerald Coven -40 rep (ultimate taboo)
NPCs fear you (dialogue changes)
Nightmares (debuff: -1 to all rolls for 1 day)
Temptation: When DSP is dangerously low, this "solves" the problem... but at moral cost.

3. ABYSS PACT: Void Hunger
Cost: 0 DSP (draws from Abyss instead)
Effect: Deal 4d10 damage (massive), but...
Consequence:
Corruption spreads 2 tiles around caster
Gain Corrupted status (1d6/turn until cleansed)
Abyss "marks" you (future encounters harder)
Path to "bad ending" (repeated use)
Lore: "When Verdance fails you, the Abyss whispers: 'We can give you power...'"

15.5 SPELL SYNERGIES (Combos)
AI DM recognizes spell combinations:

Example 1: Root + Fire Combo

Turn 1: Cast Verdant Grasp (roots enemy in place)
Turn 2: Cast Burn Magic (fire damages rooted enemy)

AI DM: "The roots ignite—trapped prey burns. 
Bonus damage: +1d6 (combo bonus)."
Example 2: Shield + Teleport

Turn 1: Cast Soul Shield on ally
Turn 2: Cast Bloom Step to teleport ally out of danger

AI DM: "You pull your ally through the Veil—shield 
intact, threat evaded. Tactical!"
Encourages experimentation without hard-coding every combo.

16. SKILL SYSTEM (EXPANDED)
(See Section 5.4 for basics. This adds complexity.)

16.1 SKILL CHECKS (Detailed)
When Do Skill Checks Happen?

Dialogue (Persuasion, Intimidation)
Exploration (Perception to spot traps, Athletics to climb)
Social (Deception to lie, Insight to detect lies)
Crafting (better results)
Check Difficulty Classes (DC):

DC	Difficulty	Success Rate (Average PC)
8	Very Easy	95%
10	Easy	85%
12	Moderate	70%
14	Hard	55%
16	Very Hard	40%
18	Extremely Hard	25%
20	Nearly Impossible	10%
Contextual Modifiers:

Base DC: 14 (convince guard to let you pass)

Modifiers:
+ You're known to guards: -2 DC (now 12)
+ Crimson Sap (everyone tense): +2 DC (now 16)
+ High Bloomguard rep: -2 DC (now 14)
+ You're visibly armed: +1 DC (now 15)

Final DC: 15
16.2 OPPOSED CHECKS
When two characters compete:

Example: Stealth vs Perception

You're sneaking past guard.

You roll: d20 + Stealth Rank (3) = 18
Guard rolls: d20 + Perception Rank (2) = 14

18 vs 14 → You win, remain hidden
Example: Deception vs Insight

You're lying to NPC.

You roll: d20 + Deception (2) + Charisma (2) = 19
NPC rolls: d20 + Insight (3) + Wisdom (1) = 16

19 vs 16 → NPC believes your lie
16.3 GROUP CHECKS
When multiple party members attempt:

Example: Sneaking past patrol (player + 2 allies)

Everyone rolls Stealth:
- Player: 18 (success)
- Ally 1: 14 (success)
- Ally 2: 8 (failure)

Rule: Majority succeeds = group succeeds
Result: 2/3 passed → You sneak past, but it was close
17. STATUS EFFECTS & CONDITIONS (EXPANDED)
(See Section 6.10 for basics. This adds mechanics.)

17.1 BUFF STACKING RULES
General Rule: Buffs of the same type DON'T stack (take highest).

Example:

Soul Shield: +2 Evasion (2 turns)
Blessed: +1 to all rolls (3 turns)

Result: +2 Evasion, +1 to all rolls (separate buffs, both apply)

BUT

Soul Shield from Player: +2 Evasion
Soul Shield from Ally: +2 Evasion

Result: +2 Evasion (not +4, doesn't stack with itself)
Exception: "Stacking" statuses explicitly say so (Bleed, Poison).

17.2 CONDITION IMMUNITIES
Some enemies/items grant immunities:

Example Immunities:

Fungal Affinity Talent: Immune to Poison
Corrupted Enemies: Immune to Fear
Viridian Plate Armor: Resist Bleed (reduce by half)
Soulborn Ancestry: Resist Corruption (+2 to saves)
Displayed in Enemy Tooltip:

Sporecaller Shaman
HP: 20/20
Guard: 5/8

Immunities:
- IMMUNE: Poison
- RESIST: Fire (half damage)
17.3 CONDITION REMOVAL
How to Remove Debuffs:

Condition	Removal Method
Poisoned	Dreamroot Tea, wait 3 turns, cleanse spell
Bleeding	Bandage (item), healing spell, rest
Rooted	Ally frees you (1 AP), Athletics check (DC 14)
Blinded	Wait 2 turns, cleanse spell
Corrupted	Burn Magic (risky), Decay Mastery spell, Coven ritual
Stunned	Automatically ends next turn
Feared	Kill source, Courage spell, wait 1 turn
18. ENVIRONMENTAL INTERACTION SYSTEM
18.1 INTERACTIVE OBJECTS
Common Objects:

Levers
Pull to activate (1 AP)
Opens doors, triggers traps, changes terrain
Crates/Barrels
Break for loot (1 AP)
Can be pushed to block paths (2 AP, Athletics check)
Bioluminescent Fungi
Trigger for flash (blinds enemies, one-use)
Viridian Crystals
Shatter for AoE damage (attacks destroy)
Stand near for +5 DSP regen/turn
Corruption Patches
Cleanse with Burn Magic (costs DSP)
Spreads if ignored (1 tile/round)
Root Bridges
Collapse if damaged (DC 14 Agility save or fall)
Sap Pools
Effects depend on Sap Phase (heal, slow, or buff)
18.2 DESTRUCTIBLE ENVIRONMENT
What Can Be Destroyed:

Wooden structures (doors, crates, bridges)
Crystal formations
Fungal growths
What Can't:

Stone walls
Everwood (too sacred)
NPCs' homes (protected by law)
Destruction Mechanics:

Each object has HP (usually 10-20)
Takes damage from attacks/spells
When HP = 0, breaks
Example:

Wooden Door (HP: 15)

Player attacks with axe (1d10+3 = 9 damage)
Door HP: 15 → 6

Ally casts Burn Magic (2d8 = 10 damage)
Door HP: 6 → 0

Door DESTROYED (new path opens)
18.3 ENVIRONMENTAL PUZZLES
Example Puzzle: The Veil-Locked Chamber

Setup:

You find a door covered in emerald runes.

AI DM: "The door pulses faintly—Veil magic. Three 
pedestals surround it, each with a crystal slot. The 
runes read: 'Only the balanced may enter.'"

Nearby: 5 Viridian Crystals (3 needed)
Solution:

Player must choose 3 crystals that sum to specific weight
Arcana skill check (DC 14) reveals hint
Correct combination opens door
Wrong combination: 2d6 damage (magical backlash)
AI DM Handles:

If player asks creative questions ("Can I use Insight to sense which crystals?"), AI adjudicates
Not hard-coded solution, flexible

19. WORLD STRUCTURE (VERDANCE GEOGRAPHY - COMPLETE)
19.1 WORLD DESIGN PHILOSOPHY
Core Principles:

Verticality: Verdance is 3D (ground level, canopy platforms, underground)
Interconnection: Locations loop back (Metroidvania-style unlocks)
Living World: Locations change based on Sap Phase, DSP level, player choices
Density over Size: 25 small, rich areas > 100 empty fields
Design Inspiration:

Dark Souls (interconnected world, shortcuts unlock)
Hollow Knight (layered map, secrets everywhere)
Divinity OS 2 (reactive environments)
Anti-Pattern: Open-world bloat (empty spaces, fetch quests)

19.2 LOCATION TIER SYSTEM
Locations organized by accessibility + danger:

TIER 1 — SAFE ZONES (No Combat)

Canopy of Life (hub)
Verdant Exchange (market)
Bloomguard Barracks
Emerald Sanctum

Patrolled roads
Farms and outposts
Minor dungeons

Deep forests
Abandoned ruins
Corruption zones
TIER 4 — HOSTILE TERRITORY (Heavy Combat)

Abyss-controlled zones
Major dungeons
Boss lairs
TIER 5 — ENDGAME AREAS (Extreme)

The Scar (Abyss breach)
Everwood Heart
Final boss locations
19.3 THE 25 LOCATIONS (COMPLETE SPECIFICATION)
LOCATION 1: CANOPY OF LIFE (Hub City)
Type: Safe Zone (Tier 1)
Size: Large (10 districts, 30+ NPCs)
Verticality: 3 levels (ground, mid-canopy, high canopy)

Description:

"A city woven from living Everwood branches. Platforms
spiral upward around massive trunks. Root bridges connect
districts. Bioluminescent fungi provide soft emerald light.
The air smells of sap and blooming flowers."

Visual Style:

Architecture: Living wood (grows naturally, no nails/boards)
Lighting: Bioluminescent fungi (emerald glow at night)
Color Palette: Rich greens, natural browns, silver accents
Atmosphere: Peaceful but watchful (guards patrol)
Districts:

The Heart Plaza (Central Square)
Everwood's main trunk visible (glowing emerald)
Public gathering space
NPCs: Street performers, merchants, civilians
Services: Quest board, town crier (announcements)
Bloomguard Barracks (Military Quarter)
Training grounds (can spar with NPCs for XP)
Armory (weapon/armor shop, high-quality)
Captain's Office (faction quests)
Jail (if arrested, you're held here)

5 shops:
General Goods (potions, food, supplies)
Blacksmith (weapons, armor, repairs)

Animal sanctuary (can befriend beasts)
Ranger training (archery, survival skills)
Herbalist (plant-based potions, cheaper than alchemist)
Sporecaller Descent (Underground Access)
Staircase leading to Mycelium Nexus
Fungal growths on walls (glowing, ambient)
NPCs: Sporecallers, fungi researchers
Decay magic training available
Residential District (Housing)
NPCs live here (can visit homes for quests)
Player's room (if purchased, 500g)
Storage chest (unlimited stash)
Bed (rest for free, full heal)
The Whispering Gardens (Park)
Peaceful green space
NPCs: Couples, children playing, elderly
Benches (sit to trigger contemplation scenes)
Hidden: Secret quest item under specific bench
Overlook Platform (Scenic Viewpoint)
Highest point in Canopy
Panoramic vista (see all of Verdance biome)
Romantic spot (NPC dates happen here)
Fast travel hub (unlock after Act 1)

Canopy of Life — Sap Phase Changes:

Crimson Sap (Vulnerability):

Lighting: Darker, red-tinged shadows
NPCs: Indoors, nervous dialogue, shops close early
Patrols: Doubled Bloomguard presence
Music: Tense, minor key
Silver Sap (Power):

Lighting: Bright silver-white, everything glows
NPCs: Celebrating, Unbinding festivals
Special Event: Festival of Silver (minigames, bonuses)
Music: Triumphant, major key
Blue Sap (Recovery):

Lighting: Warm golden-green
NPCs: Relaxed, talkative, shops offer sales
Special: Free healing at Sanctum, crafting bonuses
Music: Pastoral, peaceful
Canopy of Life — DSP Impact:

High DSP (70+):

Bioluminescence bright
NPCs cheerful
Children playing in streets
Low DSP (30-50):

Lights dimming
NPCs worried, whispering
Some shops closed (fear)
Critical DSP (<30):

Lights flickering, some out
NPCs panicked, some fleeing
Bloomguard martial law
Music: Ominous, crisis tones

LOCATION 5: WHISPERING VEIL (Veilkeeper Grove)
Type: Sacred Zone (Tier 1)

Description:

"Not a physical place, but a pocket within the Veil itself.

Visual Style:

Surreal, dreamlike (not realistic)
Colors: Silver mist, emerald glows, faint stars
No shadows (ambient light from everywhere)
Trees: Massive, ancient, glowing runes on bark
Sound: Layered whispers (not words, but feeling)
The Five Trees:

1. SYLTHARA'S OAK (Combat Wisdom)

Appearance: Broad, sturdy, battle-scarred bark
Hollowing Visual: Cracks spreading, leaves falling
Aura: Protective, motherly
2. MORVEIN'S WILLOW (Hidden Paths)

Appearance: Willowy, translucent, shifting
Hollowing Visual: Fading to invisibility
Aura: Playful, mysterious
3. ELDUIN'S STARWOOD (Future Events)

Appearance: Trunk like night sky, constellations in bark
Hollowing Visual: Stars dimming, going dark
Aura: Melancholic, burdened
4. KAELTHAS'S STONE-TREE (Ancient Lore)

Appearance: Petrified, covered in runes
Hollowing Visual: Runes cracking, eroding
Aura: Timeless, patient
5. VIRELDA'S SHADOW-TREE (Corruption)

Appearance: Half-tree, half-shadow, contained corruption
Hollowing Visual: Shadow consuming light
Aura: Grim, pragmatic
Mechanics:

Cannot explore freely (instanced consultation only)
No combat (sacred, protected by Veil)
Time doesn't pass (entering/exiting is instant)
NPCs cannot enter (player-only space)
Special Event: "The Silence"

If all 5 Veilkeepers die (Hollowed):
Grove becomes empty, desolate
Just dead trees, no whispers
Emerald Coven mourns
Veil weakens permanently (-10 max DSP)
Achievement: "The Silence" (grim)
LOCATION 6: HOLLOWROOT CATACOMBS (First Dungeon)
Type: Dungeon (Tier 2)
Size: Medium (10 rooms, 2 floors)
Enemies: Sporecaller Grunts, Abyss Scouts, Corrupted Roots
Boss: Void Tendril (Abyss mini-boss)

Description:

"Beneath Verdance's roots, a network of tunnels carved
by ancient decay. Fungal growths pulse with sickly light.
Corruption patches spread like infection. The air is
thick with spores—breathe shallow. Distant dripping
echoes. Something moves in the dark."

Visual Style:

Dark, claustrophobic
Bioluminescent fungi (sickly green/yellow, not healthy cyan)
Corruption: Black-green ooze on walls
Atmosphere: Oppressive, damp, dangerous
Layout:

FLOOR 1:
[Entrance]
    ↓
[Fungal Tunnel] — [Spore Chamber] — [Corruption Pool]
    ↓                                       ↓
[Root Bridge]                         [Hidden Cache]
    ↓
[Descent to Floor 2]

FLOOR 2:
[Underground Lake] — [Corruption Source] — [Boss Arena]
         ↓
    [Secret Exit]
Rooms (Detailed):

ROOM 1: Entrance Hall

Enemies: None (safe entry)
Features:
Save point (campfire, can rest)
Warning sign: "Turn back. Corruption spreads."
Loot: Minor healing potion
ROOM 2: Fungal Tunnel

Enemies: 2× Sporecaller Grunt (easy fight)
Features:
Difficult terrain (fungal zone)
Bioluminescent flash fungi (can trigger to blind enemies)
Loot: Dreamroot ×3
ROOM 3: Spore Chamber

Enemies: 3× Sporecaller Grunt, 1× Spore Shaman
Features:
Spore clouds (poison damage if you enter)
Vent levers (can clear spores, 1 AP)
Loot: Uncommon armor (Rootweave Harness)
ROOM 4: Corruption Pool

Enemies: None (environmental hazard)
Features:
Large corruption patch (spreading, 1 tile/turn)
Must cleanse with Burn Magic (15 DSP) OR path around
If cleansed: +15 DSP reward (domain healed)
Loot: Corrupted Essence ×2 (crafting material)
ROOM 5: Root Bridge

Enemies: 2× Abyss Scout (ambush)
Features:
Narrow root bridge (high ground bonus)
Can collapse if damaged (DC 14 Agility save)
Loot: Abyss Shard (quest item)
ROOM 6: Hidden Cache (Optional)

Enemies: None
Features:
Secret wall (Perception DC 14 to find)
Contains: Rare weapon (Thornfang Blade), 200g
Trapped chest (Disarm DC 12 or 2d6 damage)
ROOM 7: Descent to Floor 2

Enemies: None (transition)
Features:
Spiral staircase (carved roots)
Warning growl from below (boss hint)
ROOM 8: Underground Lake

Enemies: 3× Abyss Scout
Features:
Sap pool (Blue Sap, healing if you stand in it)
Deep water (drowning hazard if pushed in)
Loot: Viridian Crystal Fragment
ROOM 9: Corruption Source

Enemies: 4× Corrupted Root (animated plants)
Features:
Corruption spreading from central node
Can destroy node (boss fight becomes easier)
OR leave it (boss harder, but node is rare crafting material)
Loot: Corruption Node (if harvested, not destroyed)
ROOM 10: Boss Arena

Enemy: Void Tendril (mini-boss)
HP: 80
Abilities:
Soul Siphon (drains 10 DSP, heals 15 HP)
Corruption Spread (1 tile/turn)
Tendril Slam (2d10 damage, knockback)
Weakness: Fire (Burn Magic +50% damage)
Strategy: Destroy corruption source first (easier) OR conserve DSP and use terrain
Features:
Large arena (10×10 grid)
Corruption patches everywhere
Viridian crystals (can shatter for damage)
Loot on Victory:
Void Shard (quest item, proof of victory)
Rare weapon: Void-touched Blade (1d10, corruption on hit)
300 XP
+10 DSP (domain cleansed)
ROOM 11: Secret Exit (Optional)

Unlocks after boss defeat
Shortcut back to surface
Contains: Legendary crafting blueprint (if found)
Dungeon Completion:

Quest: "Shadows in the Roots" (main quest, Act 1)
Return Void Shard to Bloomguard
Reward: +15 Bloomguard rep, 500g, level up
