25. ENDING SYSTEM (COMPLETE)
(Already covered in Section 20.4-20.5, but expanded here)

25.1 ENDING MATRIX (Complete)
4 Major Endings × 3 Reputation States × 2 Veilkeeper States = 24 Possible Variations

ENDING 1: DOMINATION (War Victory)
Requirements:

Defeated Void Architect
Sealed The Scar properly (50 DSP ritual)
VARIATION A: High Rep, All Veilkeepers Alive

Title: "Glorious Victory - The Eternal Guardians"

Epilogue:
- Verdance celebrates (festival)
- All factions unified (temporary)
- Veilkeepers honored as heroes
- Player statue in Canopy
- DSP stabilizes at 60/100
- Abyss sealed for 1000 years

Final Scene: Player at Overlook with companions, hopeful
VARIATION B: High Rep, Some Veilkeepers Dead

Title: "Victory with Sacrifice"

Epilogue:
- Verdance victorious but mourning
- Veilkeeper memorials (player attends, guilt)
- Veil weaker permanently (-10 max DSP)
- Some factions blame player for Veilkeeper deaths
- DSP at 55/90

Final Scene: Player alone at memorial, reflective
VARIATION C: Low Rep, Veilkeepers Alive

Title: "Hollow Triumph"

Epilogue:
- Victory, but player exiled (too many crimes)
- Verdance safe, but player not welcome
- Veilkeepers sad to see you go
- DSP at 60, but you don't benefit
- Wander as outcast

Final Scene: Player leaving Verdance, looking back sadly
ENDING 2: HARMONY (Diplomacy Victory)
Requirements:

Negotiated treaty with Void Architect
Persuasion checks passed
Shared DSP (65/35 split)
VARIATION A: Perfect Treaty, High Reps

Title: "The Balance Restored"

Epilogue:
- Abyss integration begins
- Cultural exchange (awkward but hopeful)
- Children of both sides play together
- DSP max increases to 120 (shared pool stronger)
- Occasional extremist attacks (some resist)
- Player as mediator, respected by both

Final Scene: Player watching mixed Verdance/Abyss festival
VARIATION B: Fragile Peace, Mixed Reps

Title: "Uneasy Truce"

Epilogue:
- Treaty holds, barely
- Frequent skirmishes (extremists)
- Player must constantly mediate
- DSP at 100, but volatile
- Some NPCs never accept Abyss
- Hope exists, but uncertain

Final Scene: Player between two groups, keeping peace
VARIATION C: Treaty Rejected, Return to War

Title: "Failed Diplomacy"

Epilogue:
- Negotiations collapse
- War resumes (worse than before)
- Player blamed by both sides
- Kaelen dies (executed as traitor)
- Returns to Domination ending, but darker

Final Scene: Player watching war from distance, regretful
ENDING 3: SACRIFICE (Player Dies)
Requirements:

Choose to merge soul with Everwood
Restore DSP +100 permanently
VARIATION A: Remembered Hero

Title: "The Eternal Guardian"

Epilogue:
- Verdance thrives for 1000 years
- Your statue at Everwood's roots
- NPCs tell children your story
- Veil strongest it's ever been
- Abyss retreats (balanced naturally)
- Your consciousness lives in trees (narration implies)

Final Scene: Camera pans to statue, children playing, peaceful
VARIATION B: Forgotten Martyr

Title: "What Remains"

Epilogue:
- Verdance saved, but few remember why
- Your name fades over time
- Effectiveness same (DSP restored)
- No statue (low rep = not honored)
- Verdance survives, you're a footnote

Final Scene: Overgrown grave marker, your name weathered
ENDING 4: COLLAPSE (DSP = 0)
Requirements:

Let DSP hit 0
Did not recover in time
VARIATION A: The Last Hope

Title: "Embers of Verdance"

Epilogue:
- Everwood dies
- Verdance falls in 3 days
- Survivors flee to other domains (Radiance, Sanctuary)
- Player survives, carries guilt
- Becomes legend of warning ("The Soulborn who failed")
- Years later, saplings grow (hope)

Final Scene: Player planting Everwood seed, elderly, alone
VARIATION B: The Survivors

Title: "Diaspora"

Epilogue:
- Verdance destroyed
- Refugees scatter across Nexus
- Player leads group to Radiance
- Becomes advocate for caution
- Teaches next generation about restraint
- Verdance becomes cautionary tale

Final Scene: Player teaching children in Radiance, showing them dead Everwood wood
VARIATION C: What Remains (Total Collapse)

Title: "The Hollow Ending"

Epilogue:
- Everwood dead, Verdance uninhabitable
- All NPCs dead or fled
- Player wanders ruins
- Becomes hermit
- 100 years later, legends speak of Lost Grove
- "Where restraint failed, where wisdom died"

Final Scene: Player, old, dying at Everwood's corpse, alone
25.2 EPILOGUE STRUCTURE (All Endings)
EPILOGUE FORMAT:

1. TIME SKIP

"Six months later..." (standard)
OR "Five years later..." (Collapse ending)
2. WORLD STATE MONTAGE

3-5 scenes showing consequences
Location states (Canopy, Spindlewood, etc.)
Faction conditions
DSP level shown
3. NPC FATES

Show what happened to each companion
Show faction leaders
Show Veilkeepers (if alive)
4. PLAYER'S LEGACY

How you're remembered
Statue, memorial, OR exile
Relationships (romance, friendships)
5. FINAL SHOT

Thematic conclusion
Usually at Overlook Platform
Music swells
Fade to credits
25.3 EPILOGUE EXAMPLE (Harmony Ending, High Rep)
[EPILOGUE: THE BALANCE RESTORED]

[SCENE 1: Canopy of Life, 6 Months Later]

AI DM: "The Canopy has changed. Abyss guards patrol 
alongside Bloomguard—awkward, but learning. Emerald 
Coven teaches Abyss initiates about the Veil. Verdant 
Exchange bustles with trade from both sides.

Not everyone is happy. You see suspicious glances. 
Whispered complaints. But children—Verdance and Abyss 
both—play together in the gardens. Hope."

[SCENE 2: Veilkeeper Grove]

AI DM: "Five trees stand tall. All survived—you preserved 
wisdom. They whisper gratitude. The pattern is balanced."

[SCENE 3: Faction Leaders]

AI DM: "Captain Taryn shakes hands with an Abyss general. 
Uncomfortable, but sincere. Seer Vael smiles—proud of you.

Kael watches from shadows. He doesn't approve... but he 
doesn't interfere. 'Your path, not mine,' he mutters."

[SCENE 4: Memorial Plaza]

AI DM: "A new statue stands beside Everwood. Not you—
both sides together. Verdance and Abyss, hands clasped. 
The inscription reads:

'Where hunger met hoarding, restraint found balance.'"

[SCENE 5: Personal Resolution]

AI DM: "You find Lyris at Overlook. She's watching the 
sunset—emerald and silver, blending.

Lyris: 'You did it. Real peace. I never thought... Thank 
you.'

She takes your hand. You stand together, silent."

[SCREEN FADES]

[TEXT APPEARS]
"The Balance Restored"
"Verdance and Abyss share the DSP (65/35)"
"Max DSP increased to 120"
"Integration ongoing (fragile but hopeful)"
"Your restraint changed history"

[CREDITS ROLL]

[POST-CREDITS SCENE]

AI DM: "Years later. A Soulborn child—half Verdance, half 
Abyss—is born during Silver Sap. The first of a new era.

The Veil hums, content."

[END]
25.4 NEW GAME+ (Post-Ending Feature)
Unlocked After Any Ending

What Carries Over:

Player knowledge (you remember lore)
Achievements
Codex entries
What Resets:

Character level (start at 1)
Inventory
World state
New Game+ Features:

1. Starting Phase Choice

Choose Crimson, Silver, or Blue Sap start
Changes opening difficulty
2. Alternate Start

Different ancestry (unlock Half-Abyss without restriction)
Different class
3. Veilkeeper Knowledge

Can access one "free" Veilkeeper consultation early
Choose your specialization
4. Hard Mode (Optional)

Enemies +50% HP/damage
DSP drains faster
Permadeath for companions
5. Speed Run Mode

Timer on screen
Leaderboards (if online)
Optimized quest chains

26.1 Advanced AI Features:

Dynamic Quest Generation:

javascript
function generateDynamicQuest(worldState) {
  const prompt = `
    World State:
    - DSP: ${worldState.dsp}/100
    - Sap Phase: ${worldState.sapPhase}
    - Player Level: ${player.level}
    - Recent Actions: ${player.recentActions}
    
    Generate a contextually appropriate side quest.
    Include: NPC, objective, reward, moral choice.
  `;
  
  const quest = await claudeAPI.complete(prompt);
  return parseQuest(quest);
}
NPC Personality Simulation:

javascript
const npcPersonality = {
  name: "Captain Taryn",
  traits: ["disciplined", "protective", "weary"],
  values: ["duty", "restraint", "honesty"],
  history: "Lost daughter in Soul War",
  currentMood: worldState.dsp < 50 ? "worried" : "confident"
};

const response = await claudeAPI.roleplay(npcPersonality, playerInput);
Consequences Tracking:

javascript
const consequenceEngine = {
  track: (choice) => {
    database.choices.push({
      timestamp: gameTime,
      choice: choice.id,
      context: worldState.snapshot()
    });
  },
  
  trigger: (condition) => {
    const relevantChoices = database.choices.filter(c => 
      condition.test(c)
    );
    return generateConsequence(relevantChoices);
  }
};

28. SAVE/LOAD SYSTEM (EXPANDED)
Save Features:

Auto-save: Every combat victory, quest completion, Sap Phase change
Manual save: Any time outside combat (3 slots)
Cloud save: Optional (Steam Cloud, account-based)
Save File Management:

javascript
class SaveManager {
  async save(slotNumber) {
    const gameState = this.captureFullState();
    const compressed = this.compress(gameState);
    
    await localStorage.setItem(
      `verdance_save_${slotNumber}`,
      JSON.stringify({
        version: "1.0.0",
        timestamp: Date.now(),
        playtime: gameState.playtime_seconds,
        thumbnail: this.generateThumbnail(),
        data: compressed
      })
    );
    
    this.showNotification("Game Saved");
  }
  
  async load(slotNumber) {
    const saveData = JSON.parse(
      localStorage.getItem(`verdance_save_${slotNumber}`)
    );
    
    if (!saveData) {
      throw new Error("No save in this slot");
    }
    
    if (saveData.version !== "1.0.0") {
      await this.migrateSave(saveData);
    }
    
    const gameState = this.decompress(saveData.data);
    this.restoreState(gameState);
  }
}

## 35-38. ENEMY, LOCATION, NPC, QUEST DATABASES (SUMMARY)

*(Due to extreme length, providing condensed specifications)*

**35. ENEMY DATABASE (40+ Enemies):**
- **Common (15):** Abyss Scout, Sporecaller Grunt, Corrupted Root, Fungal Shambler, Wild Boar
- **Uncommon (12):** Abyss Infiltrator, Spore Shaman, Corrupted Dryad, Hollow Tree Warden
- **Rare (8):** Void Tendril, Abyss Champion, Thornmaw Dryad, Corruption Elemental
- **Bosses (7):** Void Architect, Siege Worm, Corrupted Veilkeeper Echo, Mycelium Overmind, Ancient Hollow Tree, Silver Sap Aberration, The Hungering Void (secret boss)

**36. LOCATION DATABASE (25 Locations):**
*(See Section 19 for complete details)*

**37. NPC DATABASE (50+ Characters):**
- **Companions (5):** Lyris, Kael, Thalen, Virid, Kaelen
- **Faction Leaders (6):** Taryn, Vael, Kael, Sylvara, Varl, Aldric
- **Veilkeepers (5):** Sylthara, Morvein, Elduin, Kaelthas, Virelda
- **Merchants (8):** Garren, Seris, Lysa, Mira, etc.
- **Quest NPCs (26+):** Various civilians, soldiers, refugees

**38. QUEST DATABASE (40+ Quests):**
- **Main (15):** See Section 20
- **Side (20):** See Section 21
- **Faction (30):** See Section 21
- **Dynamic (Infinite):** AI-generated

## 39-44. PRODUCTION & DELIVERY (EXPANDED)

### **39. DEVELOPMENT ROADMAP (Week-by-Week, 49 Weeks)**

---

#### **PHASE 1: PRE-PRODUCTION (Weeks 1-6)**

**WEEK 1: Setup & Prototyping**
- **Tasks:**
  - Install Phaser.js 3.60, Vite, Node.js
  - Set up GitHub repository
  - Create basic isometric renderer (display test map)
  - Implement grid system (10×10 test grid)
  - Basic character sprite (placeholder, movement only)
- **Deliverables:** Playable prototype (move character on grid)
- **Hours:** 30-40 hours
- **Milestone:** "Grid Movement Works"

**WEEK 2: Core Systems I**
- **Tasks:**
  - Implement turn-based combat skeleton
  - Initiative system (d20 rolls, turn order display)
  - Basic attack mechanics (roll to hit, damage calculation)
  - HP/Guard tracking
  - UI wireframes (HUD, combat menu)
- **Deliverables:** 1v1 combat works (player vs dummy enemy)
- **Hours:** 35-45 hours
- **Milestone:** "Combat Loop Functional"

**WEEK 3: Core Systems II**
- **Tasks:**
  - DSP tracking system (global resource)
  - Spell implementation (Soul Shield, Verdant Grasp)
  - Spell UI (selection, targeting, DSP cost display)
  - Visual feedback (damage numbers, status icons)
  - Save/load basic framework
- **Deliverables:** Can cast spells, DSP drains visibly
- **Hours:** 35-45 hours
- **Milestone:** "Magic System Online"

**WEEK 4: Art Pipeline Setup**
- **Tasks:**
  - Finalize art style (create 1 reference character)
  - Design Pixar proportions template (Blender or 2D)
  - Create 10 tileset tiles (floor, walls, decorations)
  - Design 3 VFX (Soul Shield, Verdant Grasp, hit effect)
  - UI mockups (HUD, menus, dialogue box)
- **Deliverables:** Style guide PDF, 1 character sprite sheet, tilesets
- **Hours:** 30-40 hours (if commissioning, add 1-2 weeks lead time)
- **Milestone:** "Visual Identity Locked"

**WEEK 5: Sap Cycle Implementation**
- **Tasks:**
  - Calendar system (15-day cycle tracking)
  - Phase transitions (Crimson→Silver→Blue)
  - Visual phase changes (lighting, color grading)
  - Mechanical modifiers (DSP costs, damage bonuses)
  - Phase indicator UI
- **Deliverables:** Sap Cycle fully functional
- **Hours:** 30-40 hours
- **Milestone:** "Living Calendar Works"

**WEEK 6: Vertical Slice**
- **Tasks:**
  - Build 1 complete playable level (Hollowroot entrance)
  - Implement 1 main quest ("Shadows in the Roots" intro)
  - 3 enemy types (Sporecaller Grunt, Abyss Scout, Corrupted Root)
  - Basic AI (aggressive behavior)
  - 5 items (2 potions, 1 weapon, 1 armor, 1 quest item)
  - Dialogue system prototype (text box, NPC portrait)
- **Deliverables:** 15-minute vertical slice (playable demo)
- **Hours:** 40-50 hours
- **Milestone:** "Vertical Slice Complete"

**PHASE 1 TOTAL:** 6 weeks, 200-260 hours

---

#### **PHASE 2: PRODUCTION — ACT 1 (Weeks 7-24, 18 Weeks)**

**WEEKS 7-9: World Building**
- **Tasks:**
  - Build Canopy of Life hub (10 districts, 30+ NPCs)
  - Verdant Exchange (5 shops fully functional)
  - Bloomguard Barracks (training, quests)
  - Hollowroot Catacombs dungeon (10 rooms, boss)
  - Implement fast travel system
- **Deliverables:** Act 1 locations playable
- **Hours:** 100-120 hours
- **Milestone:** "Act 1 World Complete"

**WEEKS 10-12: Core Systems III**
- **Tasks:**
  - Implement all 12 Tier 1 spells
  - 10 Tier 2 spells
  - 15 weapons (common, uncommon)
  - 10 armor pieces
  - 30 consumables
  - Crafting system (3 stations)
  - Equipment UI (inventory, character sheet)
- **Deliverables:** Complete item/magic systems
- **Hours:** 90-110 hours
- **Milestone:** "Systems Depth Achieved"

**WEEKS 13-15: Act 1 Content**
- **Tasks:**
  - Main quest chain (5 quests: Tutorial → Hollowroot → Defense)
  - 3 side quests ("Lost Heirloom", "Hollow Memories", "Soulborn Child")
  - Veilkeeper system (consultation mechanics, Hollowing)
  - 10 NPCs (Taryn, Vael, Lyris, merchants, civilians)
  - Faction reputation tracking (UI + mechanics)
  - DSP crisis event (first narrative trigger)
- **Deliverables:** Act 1 story complete
- **Hours:** 90-110 hours
- **Milestone:** "Act 1 Narrative Done"

**WEEKS 16-18: Polish & QA I**
- **Tasks:**
  - UI implementation (all HUD elements, menus)
  - Sound integration (10 SFX, 2 music tracks)
  - Balance pass (DSP costs, enemy HP, damage)
  - Bug fixing (combat, UI, progression)
  - Playtesting (internal, 5-10 testers)

TASK 2.1: Create Grid Utility Class (2 hours)
Step 1: Create utils folder

touch src/utils/IsoGrid.js
Step 2: Write IsoGrid.js

src/utils/IsoGrid.js:

javascript
/**
 * Isometric Grid Utility
 * Converts between grid coordinates (x, y) and screen coordinates
 */
export default class IsoGrid {
  /**
   * @param {number} tileWidth - Width of isometric tile (in pixels)
   * @param {number} tileHeight - Height of isometric tile (in pixels)
   * @param {number} gridWidth - Number of tiles wide
   * @param {number} gridHeight - Number of tiles tall
   */
  constructor(tileWidth = 64, tileHeight = 32, gridWidth = 10, gridHeight = 10) {
    this.tileWidth = tileWidth;
    this.tileHeight = tileHeight;
    this.gridWidth = gridWidth;
    this.gridHeight = gridHeight;
  }

  /**
   * Convert grid coordinates to screen coordinates (isometric)
   * @param {number} gridX - Grid X position
   * @param {number} gridY - Grid Y position
   * @returns {object} {x, y} screen coordinates
   */
  gridToScreen(gridX, gridY) {
    const screenX = (gridX - gridY) * (this.tileWidth / 2);
    const screenY = (gridX + gridY) * (this.tileHeight / 2);
    return { x: screenX, y: screenY };
  }

  /**
   * Convert screen coordinates to grid coordinates
   * @param {number} screenX - Screen X position
   * @param {number} screenY - Screen Y position
   * @returns {object} {x, y} grid coordinates
   */
  screenToGrid(screenX, screenY) {
    const gridX = Math.floor((screenX / (this.tileWidth / 2) + screenY / (this.tileHeight / 2)) / 2);
    const gridY = Math.floor((screenY / (this.tileHeight / 2) - screenX / (this.tileWidth / 2)) / 2);
    return { x: gridX, y: gridY };
  }

  /**
   * Check if grid coordinates are valid (within bounds)
   */
  isValidTile(gridX, gridY) {
    return gridX >= 0 && gridX < this.gridWidth && gridY >= 0 && gridY < this.gridHeight;
  }

  /**
   * Get center screen position of a tile
   */
  getTileCenter(gridX, gridY) {
    const pos = this.gridToScreen(gridX, gridY);
    return {
      x: pos.x,
      y: pos.y
    };
  }
}
✅ Success Check:

TASK 2.2: Render Grid in Scene (3 hours)
Step 1: Update BootScene to render grid

src/scenes/BootScene.js:

javascript
import Phaser from 'phaser';
import IsoGrid from '../utils/IsoGrid.js';

export default class BootScene extends Phaser.Scene {
  constructor() {
    super({ key: 'BootScene' });
  }

  preload() {
    console.log('BootScene: preload()');
  }

  create() {
    console.log('BootScene: create()');
    
    // Initialize grid system
    this.grid = new IsoGrid(64, 32, 10, 10);
    
    // Offset to center grid on screen
    this.gridOffsetX = 640; // Center of 1280px width
    this.gridOffsetY = 200; // Top padding
    
    // Render the grid
    this.renderGrid();
    
    // Add instructions
    this.add.text(
      640, 50,
      'Isometric Grid Test - 10x10',
      {
        fontSize: '24px',
        color: '#E0F7FA',
        align: 'center',
        fontFamily: 'Arial'
      }
    ).setOrigin(0.5);
  }

  renderGrid() {
    const graphics = this.add.graphics();
    graphics.lineStyle(1, 0x00C853, 0.5); // Emerald green, semi-transparent

    // Draw all grid tiles
    for (let y = 0; y < this.grid.gridHeight; y++) {
      for (let x = 0; x < this.grid.gridWidth; x++) {
        this.drawIsometricTile(graphics, x, y);
      }
    }
  }

  drawIsometricTile(graphics, gridX, gridY) {
    const pos = this.grid.gridToScreen(gridX, gridY);
    const screenX = pos.x + this.gridOffsetX;
    const screenY = pos.y + this.gridOffsetY;

    const tileW = this.grid.tileWidth;
    const tileH = this.grid.tileHeight;

    // Draw diamond shape (isometric tile)
    graphics.beginPath();
    graphics.moveTo(screenX, screenY); // Top
    graphics.lineTo(screenX + tileW / 2, screenY + tileH / 2); // Right
    graphics.lineTo(screenX, screenY + tileH); // Bottom
    graphics.lineTo(screenX - tileW / 2, screenY + tileH / 2); // Left
    graphics.closePath();
    graphics.strokePath();

    // Draw grid coordinates (for debugging)
    this.add.text(
      screenX,
      screenY + tileH / 2,
      `${gridX},${gridY}`,
      {
        fontSize: '10px',
        color: '#00E5FF',
        align: 'center'
      }
    ).setOrigin(0.5);
  }

  update() {
    // Game loop
  }
}

TASK 2.3: Add Mouse Hover Highlight (2 hours)
Step 1: Add hover detection

Update src/scenes/BootScene.js:

javascript
// Add after renderGrid() in create():

// Mouse tracking
this.input.on('pointermove', (pointer) => {
  this.highlightTileAtMouse(pointer.x, pointer.y);
});

// Store highlighted tile
this.highlightedTile = null;
this.highlightGraphics = this.add.graphics();
Step 2: Add highlight function

Add to BootScene class:

javascript
highlightTileAtMouse(mouseX, mouseY) {
  // Convert mouse screen position to grid position
  const adjustedX = mouseX - this.gridOffsetX;
  const adjustedY = mouseY - this.gridOffsetY;
  
  const gridPos = this.grid.screenToGrid(adjustedX, adjustedY);
  
  // Check if valid tile
  if (!this.grid.isValidTile(gridPos.x, gridPos.y)) {
    this.highlightGraphics.clear();
    this.highlightedTile = null;
    return;
  }
  
  // Only redraw if different tile
  if (
    this.highlightedTile &&
    this.highlightedTile.x === gridPos.x &&
    this.highlightedTile.y === gridPos.y
  ) {
    return;
  }
  
  this.highlightedTile = gridPos;
  
  // Draw highlight
  this.highlightGraphics.clear();
  this.highlightGraphics.lineStyle(2, 0x00E5FF, 1); // Cyan, bright
  this.highlightGraphics.fillStyle(0x00E5FF, 0.2); // Cyan, semi-transparent
  
  const pos = this.grid.gridToScreen(gridPos.x, gridPos.y);
  const screenX = pos.x + this.gridOffsetX;
  const screenY = pos.y + this.gridOffsetY;
  
  const tileW = this.grid.tileWidth;
  const tileH = this.grid.tileHeight;
  
  // Draw filled diamond
  this.highlightGraphics.beginPath();
  this.highlightGraphics.moveTo(screenX, screenY);
  this.highlightGraphics.lineTo(screenX + tileW / 2, screenY + tileH / 2);
  this.highlightGraphics.lineTo(screenX, screenY + tileH);
  this.highlightGraphics.lineTo(screenX - tileW / 2, screenY + tileH / 2);
  this.highlightGraphics.closePath();
  this.highlightGraphics.fillPath();
  this.highlightGraphics.strokePath();
}

javascript
// Keyboard input

  w: Phaser.Input.Keyboard.KeyCodes.W,
  a: Phaser.Input.Keyboard.KeyCodes.A,
  s: Phaser.Input.Keyboard.KeyCodes.S,
  d: Phaser.Input.Keyboard.KeyCodes.D
});

// Movement cooldown (prevent spam)
this.canMove = true;
this.moveCooldown = 200; // milliseconds
Step 2: Create movement function

Add method to BootScene:

javascript
movePlayer(dx, dy) {
  if (!this.canMove) return;
  
  // Calculate new position
  const newX = this.player.gridX + dx;
  const newY = this.player.gridY + dy;
  
  // Check if valid tile
  if (!this.grid.isValidTile(newX, newY)) {
    console.log('Cannot move there - out of bounds');
    return;
  }
  
  // Update grid position
  this.player.gridX = newX;
  this.player.gridY = newY;
  
  // Convert to screen position
  const screenPos = this.grid.gridToScreen(newX, newY);
  
  // Move sprite with tween (smooth animation)
  this.tweens.add({
    targets: this.player.sprite,
    x: screenPos.x + this.gridOffsetX,
    y: screenPos.y + this.gridOffsetY,
    duration: 150,
    ease: 'Power2'
  });
  
  // Cooldown
  this.canMove = false;
  this.time.delayedCall(this.moveCooldown, () => {
    this.canMove = true;
  });
  
  console.log(`Player moved to: (${newX}, ${newY})`);
}
Step 3: Add input handling to update()

javascript
update() {
  // Check keyboard input
  if (Phaser.Input.Keyboard.JustDown(this.cursors.up) || 
      Phaser.Input.Keyboard.JustDown(this.keys.w)) {
    this.movePlayer(0, -1); // Up on grid
  } else if (Phaser.Input.Keyboard.JustDown(this.cursors.down) || 
             Phaser.Input.Keyboard.JustDown(this.keys.s)) {
    this.movePlayer(0, 1); // Down on grid
  } else if (Phaser.Input.Keyboard.JustDown(this.cursors.left) || 
             Phaser.Input.Keyboard.JustDown(this.keys.a)) {
    this.movePlayer(-1, 0); // Left on grid
  } else if (Phaser.Input.Keyboard.JustDown(this.cursors.right) || 
             Phaser.Input.Keyboard.JustDown(this.keys.d)) {
    this.movePlayer(1, 0); // Right on grid
  }
}

Step 2: Create click-to-move function

javascript
movePlayerToClick(mouseX, mouseY) {
  // Convert mouse to grid coordinates
  const adjustedX = mouseX - this.gridOffsetX;
  const adjustedY = mouseY - this.gridOffsetY;
  
  const gridPos = this.grid.screenToGrid(adjustedX, adjustedY);
  
  // Check if valid tile
  if (!this.grid.isValidTile(gridPos.x, gridPos.y)) {
    console.log('Cannot move there - invalid tile');
    return;
  }
  
  // Check if adjacent to player (only 1 tile movement for now)
  const dx = Math.abs(gridPos.x - this.player.gridX);
  const dy = Math.abs(gridPos.y - this.player.gridY);
  
  if ((dx === 1 && dy === 0) || (dx === 0 && dy === 1)) {
    // Valid adjacent move
    const moveX = gridPos.x - this.player.gridX;
    const moveY = gridPos.y - this.player.gridY;
    this.movePlayer(moveX, moveY);
  } else if (dx === 0 && dy === 0) {
    console.log('Already at that tile');
  } else {
    console.log('Too far - can only move to adjacent tiles');
  }
}

 Can click adjacent tile to move

markdown
# 🌿 Verdance RPG

**Tactical RPG with AI Dungeon Master Integration**

## 🎮 About

Verdance is a turn-based tactical RPG where magic drains a shared resource (Domain Soul Pool) that keeps the world alive. Features:

- Isometric tactical combat
- Living calendar system (Sap Cycles)
- AI-powered Dungeon Master (Claude API)
- Moral choices with permanent consequences
- Restraint-based progression

## 🛠️ Tech Stack

- **Engine:** Phaser.js 3.60
- **Build Tool:** Vite
- **Language:** JavaScript (ES6+)
- **AI Integration:** Claude API (Anthropic)

## 📦 Setup

### Prerequisites
- Node.js v18+
- npm v9+

### Installation

\`\`\`bash
# Clone repository
git clone https://github.com/YOUR_USERNAME/verdance-rpg.git
cd verdance-rpg

# Install dependencies
npm install

# Run development server
npm run dev
\`\`\`

Open http://localhost:3000

## 🗓️ Development Status

**Week 1 (Completed):**
- ✅ Phaser.js setup
- ✅ Isometric grid system
- ✅ Character movement (WASD/click)
- ✅ Basic UI

**Current Week:** Week 1 Day 4 - Code organization

**Next Up:** Combat prototype

Step 1: Create entities folder

Step 2: Write Enemy.js

src/entities/Enemy.js:

javascript
/**
 * Enemy Entity
 * Represents an enemy on the grid with AI behavior
 */
export default class Enemy {
  /**
   * @param {Phaser.Scene} scene - Parent scene
   * @param {number} gridX - Starting grid X
   * @param {number} gridY - Starting grid Y
   * @param {string} type - Enemy type identifier
   */
  constructor(scene, gridX, gridY, type = 'sporecaller_grunt') {
    this.scene = scene;
    this.gridX = gridX;
    this.gridY = gridY;
    this.type = type;
    
    // Stats (basic for now)
    this.hp = 12;
    this.maxHp = 12;
    this.damage = 4;
    this.alive = true;
    
    // AI behavior
    this.aiType = 'aggressive'; // Moves toward player
    
    // Create sprite
    this.createSprite();
  }

  createSprite() {
    // Create placeholder enemy graphic (red rectangle)
    const graphics = this.scene.add.graphics();
    graphics.fillStyle(0xFF0000, 1); // Red
    graphics.fillRect(-16, -32, 32, 48);
    graphics.generateTexture('enemy_placeholder', 32, 48);
    graphics.destroy();
    
    // Get screen position
    const screenPos = this.scene.grid.gridToScreen(this.gridX, this.gridY);
    
    // Create sprite
    this.sprite = this.scene.add.sprite(
      screenPos.x + this.scene.gridOffsetX,
      screenPos.y + this.scene.gridOffsetY,
      'enemy_placeholder'
    ).setOrigin(0.5, 1).setDepth(90); // Slightly behind player (depth 100)
    
    // Add HP bar
    this.createHealthBar();
  }

  createHealthBar() {
    // Background (red)
    this.hpBarBg = this.scene.add.rectangle(
      this.sprite.x,
      this.sprite.y - 60,
      32,
      4,
      0x8B0000
    ).setDepth(91);
    
    // Foreground (green, shows current HP)
    this.hpBarFg = this.scene.add.rectangle(
      this.sprite.x - 16,
      this.sprite.y - 60,
      32,
      4,
      0x00C853
    ).setOrigin(0, 0.5).setDepth(92);
  }

  updateHealthBar() {
    const hpPercent = this.hp / this.maxHp;
    this.hpBarFg.width = 32 * hpPercent;
  }

  /**
   * AI decision-making
   * @param {object} player - Player object with gridX, gridY
   * @returns {object} {dx, dy} movement delta
   */
  decideMove(player) {
    if (this.aiType === 'aggressive') {
      // Move toward player (simple pathfinding)
      const dx = player.gridX - this.gridX;
      const dy = player.gridY - this.gridY;
      
      // Move one step closer
      if (Math.abs(dx) > Math.abs(dy)) {
        return { dx: Math.sign(dx), dy: 0 };
      } else {
        return { dx: 0, dy: Math.sign(dy) };
      }
    }
    
    // Default: don't move
    return { dx: 0, dy: 0 };
  }

  /**
   * Execute AI turn
   */
  takeTurn(player, grid) {
    if (!this.alive) return;
    
    const move = this.decideMove(player);
    const newX = this.gridX + move.dx;
    const newY = this.gridY + move.dy;
    
    // Check if valid move
    if (!grid.isValidTile(newX, newY)) return;
    
    // Check if player is there (attack instead of move)
    if (newX === player.gridX && newY === player.gridY) {
      this.attackPlayer(player);
      return;
    }
    
    // Move
    this.moveTo(newX, newY);
  }

  moveTo(newX, newY) {
    this.gridX = newX;
    this.gridY = newY;
    
    const screenPos = this.scene.grid.gridToScreen(newX, newY);
    
    // Animate movement
    this.scene.tweens.add({
      targets: [this.sprite, this.hpBarBg, this.hpBarFg],
      x: screenPos.x + this.scene.gridOffsetX,
      y: (target) => {
        if (target === this.sprite) {
          return screenPos.y + this.scene.gridOffsetY;
        } else {
          return screenPos.y + this.scene.gridOffsetY - 60;
        }
      },
      duration: 200,
      ease: 'Power2'
    });
  }

  attackPlayer(player) {
    console.log(`Enemy attacks player for ${this.damage} damage!`);
    
    // Visual feedback (shake sprite)
    this.scene.tweens.add({
      targets: this.sprite,
      x: this.sprite.x + 5,
      duration: 50,
      yoyo: true,
      repeat: 3
    });
    
    // TODO: Apply damage to player (implement in Week 2)
  }

  takeDamage(amount) {
    this.hp -= amount;
    if (this.hp <= 0) {
      this.hp = 0;
      this.die();
    }
    
    this.updateHealthBar();
    
    // Visual feedback (flash red)
    this.scene.tweens.add({
      targets: this.sprite,
      tint: 0xFF0000,
      duration: 100,
      yoyo: true
    });
  }

  die() {
    this.alive = false;
    
    // Fade out and destroy
    this.scene.tweens.add({
      targets: [this.sprite, this.hpBarBg, this.hpBarFg],
      alpha: 0,
      duration: 300,
      onComplete: () => {
        this.sprite.destroy();
        this.hpBarBg.destroy();
        this.hpBarFg.destroy();
      }
    });
  }

  destroy() {
    if (this.sprite) this.sprite.destroy();
    if (this.hpBarBg) this.hpBarBg.destroy();
    if (this.hpBarFg) this.hpBarFg.destroy();
  }
}
✅ Success Check:

 Enemy.js created
 No syntax errors

Step 2: Update movePlayer to end turn

Modify movePlayer():

movePlayer(dx, dy) {
  if (!this.canMove || this.turnState !== 'player') return;
  
  // ... existing movement code ...

  this.time.delayedCall(this.moveCooldown + 100, () => {
    this.endPlayerTurn();
  });
}
Step 3: Add turn management

javascript
endPlayerTurn() {
  this.turnState = 'enemy';
  this.turnText.setText('Enemy Turn');
  
  // Execute enemy turns
  this.time.delayedCall(300, () => {
    this.executeEnemyTurns();
  });
}

executeEnemyTurns() {
  let delay = 0;
  
  this.enemies.forEach((enemy, index) => {
    if (enemy.alive) {
      this.time.delayedCall(delay, () => {
        enemy.takeTurn(this.player, this.grid);
      });
      delay += 400; // Stagger enemy turns
    }
  });
  
  // Return to player turn
  this.time.delayedCall(delay + 200, () => {
    this.startPlayerTurn();
  });
}

startPlayerTurn() {
  this.turnState = 'player';
  this.turnText.setText('Your Turn');
  this.canMove = true;
}

javascript
addCombatLogEntry(text) {
  this.combatLog.unshift(text); // Add to start
  if (this.combatLog.length > 10) {
    this.combatLog.pop(); // Remove oldest
  }
  this.updateCombatLog();
}

updateCombatLog() {
  const logText = 'COMBAT LOG:\n' + this.combatLog.join('\n');
  this.combatLogDisplay.setText(logText);
}

Step 2: Add grid fade on edges

javascript
// In renderGrid():
for (let y = 0; y < this.grid.gridHeight; y++) {
  for (let x = 0; x < this.grid.gridWidth; x++) {
    // Calculate distance from center
    const centerX = this.grid.gridWidth / 2;
    const centerY = this.grid.gridHeight / 2;
    const dist = Math.sqrt(
      Math.pow(x - centerX, 2) + Math.pow(y - centerY, 2)
    );
    const maxDist = Math.sqrt(
      Math.pow(centerX, 2) + Math.pow(centerY, 2)
    );
    const alpha = 1 - (dist / maxDist) * 0.5; // Fade toward edges
    
    graphics.lineStyle(1, COLORS.PRIMARY, alpha);
    this.drawIsometricTile(graphics, x, y);
  }
}

TASK 8.1: Create Combat Manager (2.5 hours)
Step 1: Create systems folder

mkdir src/systems
touch src/systems/CombatManager.js
Step 2: Write CombatManager.js

src/systems/CombatManager.js:

javascript
/**
 * Combat Manager
 * Handles turn-based combat, initiative, and combat state
 */
export default class CombatManager {
  /**
   * @param {Phaser.Scene} scene - Parent scene
   */
  constructor(scene) {
    this.scene = scene;
    
    // Combat state
    this.inCombat = false;
    this.combatants = []; // Array of {entity, initiative, hasActed}
    this.currentTurnIndex = 0;
    this.roundNumber = 1;
  }

  /**
   * Start combat with given entities
   * @param {Array} entities - Array of combatants (player + enemies)
   */
  startCombat(entities) {
    console.log('Combat starting...');
    this.inCombat = true;
    this.roundNumber = 1;
    this.combatants = [];
    
    // Roll initiative for all combatants
    entities.forEach(entity => {
      const initiative = this.rollInitiative(entity);
      this.combatants.push({
        entity: entity,
        initiative: initiative,
        hasActed: false
      });
    });
    
    // Sort by initiative (highest first)
    this.combatants.sort((a, b) => b.initiative - a.initiative);
    
    // Start first turn
    this.currentTurnIndex = 0;
    this.startTurn();
    
    console.log('Initiative order:', this.combatants.map(c => 
      `${c.entity.name || 'Enemy'}: ${c.initiative}`
    ));
  }

  /**
   * Roll initiative for an entity
   * @param {object} entity - Entity object
   * @returns {number} Initiative value
   */
  rollInitiative(entity) {
    // d20 + Agility modifier
    const d20 = Math.floor(Math.random() * 20) + 1;
    const agility = entity.agility || 0;
    return d20 + agility;
  }

  /**
   * Start the current combatant's turn
   */
  startTurn() {
    if (!this.inCombat) return;
    
    const current = this.combatants[this.currentTurnIndex];
    
    console.log(`Turn ${this.roundNumber}.${this.currentTurnIndex + 1}: ${current.entity.name || 'Enemy'}'s turn`);
    
    // Mark as not acted yet
    current.hasActed = false;
    
    // If player's turn, wait for input
    if (current.entity.isPlayer) {
      this.scene.startPlayerCombatTurn();
    } else {
      // AI turn
      this.scene.time.delayedCall(500, () => {
        this.executeAITurn(current.entity);
      });
    }
  }

  /**
   * Execute AI combatant's turn
   */
  executeAITurn(entity) {
    // AI logic (simple for now - attack player)
    const player = this.combatants.find(c => c.entity.isPlayer).entity;
    
    if (entity.alive) {
      entity.attackTarget(player);
    }
    
    // End turn after action
    this.scene.time.delayedCall(800, () => {
      this.endTurn();
    });
  }

  /**
   * End current turn, move to next
   */
  endTurn() {
    if (!this.inCombat) return;
    
    // Mark current as acted
    this.combatants[this.currentTurnIndex].hasActed = true;
    
    // Move to next combatant
    this.currentTurnIndex++;
    
    // Check if round is over
    if (this.currentTurnIndex >= this.combatants.length) {
      this.endRound();
      return;
    }
    
    // Start next turn
    this.startTurn();
  }

  /**
   * End current round, start new one
   */
  endRound() {
    console.log(`Round ${this.roundNumber} complete`);
    
    // Remove dead combatants
    this.combatants = this.combatants.filter(c => c.entity.alive);
    
    // Check for combat end
    const playerAlive = this.combatants.some(c => c.entity.isPlayer);
    const enemiesAlive = this.combatants.some(c => !c.entity.isPlayer);
    
    if (!playerAlive) {
      this.endCombat('defeat');
      return;
    }
    
    if (!enemiesAlive) {
      this.endCombat('victory');
      return;
    }
    
    // Start new round
    this.roundNumber++;
    this.currentTurnIndex = 0;
    
    // Reset hasActed flags
    this.combatants.forEach(c => c.hasActed = false);
    
    this.startTurn();
  }

  /**
   * End combat
   * @param {string} result - 'victory' or 'defeat'
   */
  endCombat(result) {
    console.log(`Combat ended: ${result}`);
    this.inCombat = false;
    this.combatants = [];
    
    this.scene.endCombat(result);
  }

  /**
   * Get current acting combatant
   */
  getCurrentCombatant() {
    if (!this.inCombat || this.currentTurnIndex >= this.combatants.length) {
      return null;
    }
    return this.combatants[this.currentTurnIndex];
  }

  /**
   * Get all combatants in initiative order
   */
  getInitiativeOrder() {
    return this.combatants.map((c, index) => ({
      name: c.entity.name || `Enemy ${index}`,
      initiative: c.initiative,
      hasActed: c.hasActed,
      isCurrent: index === this.currentTurnIndex,
      isPlayer: c.entity.isPlayer
    }));
  }
}

Step 2: Add combat start function

javascript
startCombat() {
  console.log('Initiating combat...');
  
  // Gather all combatants
  const combatants = [this.player, ...this.enemies.filter(e => e.alive)];
  
  // Start combat
  this.combatManager.startCombat(combatants);
  
  // Update UI
  this.updateTurnDisplay();
}

startPlayerCombatTurn() {
  console.log("Player's turn - waiting for action");
  this.canMove = true;
  
  // Update UI
  this.turnText.setText("Your Turn");
  this.updateTurnDisplay();
}

endCombat(result) {
  console.log(`Combat ended: ${result}`);
  
  if (result === 'victory') {
    this.addCombatLogEntry('Victory! All enemies defeated.');
    // TODO: Rewards, XP
  } else {
    this.addCombatLogEntry('Defeat! Game Over.');
    // TODO: Restart or load
  }
  
  this.turnText.setText(`Combat Over: ${result.toUpperCase()}`);
}

In create():

javascript
// Turn order UI
this.turnOrderPanel = this.add.container(20, 200).setDepth(1000);

// Background
const bgGraphics = this.add.graphics();
bgGraphics.fillStyle(0x1B5E20, 0.9);
bgGraphics.fillRoundedRect(0, 0, 200, 400, 10);
this.turnOrderPanel.add(bgGraphics);

// Title
const title = this.add.text(
  100, 20,
  'TURN ORDER',
  {
    fontSize: '18px',
    color: '#00E5FF',
    fontFamily: 'Arial',
    fontStyle: 'bold'
  }
).setOrigin(0.5);
this.turnOrderPanel.add(title);

// Turn entries (created dynamically)
this.turnOrderEntries = [];
Step 2: Add update function

javascript
updateTurnDisplay() {
  // Clear existing entries
  this.turnOrderEntries.forEach(entry => entry.destroy());
  this.turnOrderEntries = [];
  
  if (!this.combatManager.inCombat) {
    return;
  }
  
  // Get initiative order
  const order = this.combatManager.getInitiativeOrder();
  
  // Create entry for each combatant
  order.forEach((combatant, index) => {
    const y = 60 + (index * 60);
    
    // Background for current turn
    if (combatant.isCurrent) {
      const highlight = this.add.graphics();
      highlight.fillStyle(0x00E5FF, 0.3);
      highlight.fillRoundedRect(10, y - 5, 180, 50, 5);
      this.turnOrderPanel.add(highlight);
      this.turnOrderEntries.push(highlight);
    }
    
    // Combatant name
    const nameColor = combatant.isPlayer ? '#E0F7FA' : '#FF6B6B';
    const nameText = this.add.text(
      20, y,
      combatant.name,
      {
        fontSize: '16px',
        color: nameColor,
        fontFamily: 'Arial'
      }
    );
    this.turnOrderPanel.add(nameText);
    this.turnOrderEntries.push(nameText);
    
    // Initiative value
    const initText = this.add.text(
      180, y,
      `${combatant.initiative}`,
      {
        fontSize: '16px',
        color: '#00C853',
        fontFamily: 'monospace'
      }
    ).setOrigin(1, 0);
    this.turnOrderPanel.add(initText);
    this.turnOrderEntries.push(initText);
    
    // Status (acted or not)
    const statusText = this.add.text(
      20, y + 20,
      combatant.hasActed ? '✓ Acted' : (combatant.isCurrent ? '► Acting...' : '○ Waiting'),
      {
        fontSize: '12px',
        color: combatant.hasActed ? '#666666' : '#00E5FF',
        fontFamily: 'Arial'
      }
    );
    this.turnOrderPanel.add(statusText);
    this.turnOrderEntries.push(statusText);
  });
}

TASK 9.1: Create Dice Utility (1.5 hours)
Step 1: Create utils/Dice.js

bash
touch src/utils/Dice.js
src/utils/Dice.js:

javascript
/**
 * Dice Rolling Utility
 * Handles all dice rolls for combat and skill checks
 */
export default class Dice {
  /**
   * Roll a die with specified number of sides
   * @param {number} sides - Number of sides (e.g., 20 for d20)
   * @returns {number} Result (1 to sides)
   */
  static roll(sides) {
    return Math.floor(Math.random() * sides) + 1;
  }

  /**
   * Roll multiple dice and sum
   * @param {number} count - Number of dice
   * @param {number} sides - Sides per die
   * @returns {object} {total, rolls: []}
   */
  static rollMultiple(count, sides) {
    const rolls = [];
    let total = 0;
    
    for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
      const roll = this.roll(sides);
      rolls.push(roll);
      total += roll;
    }
    
    return { total, rolls };
  }

  /**
   * Roll with advantage (roll twice, take higher)
   * @param {number} sides - Die size
   * @returns {object} {result, rolls: [roll1, roll2]}
   */
  static rollAdvantage(sides) {
    const roll1 = this.roll(sides);
    const roll2 = this.roll(sides);
    return {
      result: Math.max(roll1, roll2),
      rolls: [roll1, roll2]
    };
  }

  /**
   * Roll with disadvantage (roll twice, take lower)
   */
  static rollDisadvantage(sides) {
    const roll1 = this.roll(sides);
    const roll2 = this.roll(sides);
    return {
      result: Math.min(roll1, roll2),
      rolls: [roll1, roll2]
    };
  }

  /**
   * Parse dice notation (e.g., "2d6+3")
   * @param {string} notation - Dice notation
   * @returns {object} {total, rolls: [], modifier}
   */
  static parseAndRoll(notation) {
    // Match pattern: XdY+Z or XdY-Z or XdY
    const match = notation.match(/(\d+)d(\d+)([+-]\d+)?/);
    
    if (!match) {
      console.error(`Invalid dice notation: ${notation}`);
      return { total: 0, rolls: [], modifier: 0 };
    }
    
    const count = parseInt(match[1]);
    const sides = parseInt(match[2]);
    const modifier = match[3] ? parseInt(match[3]) : 0;
    
    const result = this.rollMultiple(count, sides);
    
    return {
      total: result.total + modifier,
      rolls: result.rolls,
      modifier: modifier
    };
  }
}

Step 1: Add attack function to CombatManager

src/systems/CombatManager.js:

javascript
import Dice from '../utils/Dice.js';
import { COMBAT } from '../config/constants.js';

// Add to CombatManager class:

/**
 * Execute attack from attacker to target
 * @param {object} attacker - Attacking entity
 * @param {object} target - Target entity
 * @returns {object} Attack result
 */
performAttack(attacker, target) {
  console.log(`${attacker.name} attacks ${target.name || '
Continue

Feb 4
Enemy'}!`);

// 1. Roll to hit (d20 + attack bonus)
const d20Roll = Dice.roll(20);
const attackBonus = attacker.weapon.attackBonus;
const attackRoll = d20Roll + attackBonus;

console.log(  Attack roll: ${d20Roll} + ${attackBonus} = ${attackRoll} vs AC ${target.evasion});

// 2. Check if hit
const isHit = attackRoll >= target.evasion;
const isCrit = d20Roll === 20;
const isMiss = d20Roll === 1;

if (isMiss) { console.log(  Critical miss!); this.scene.addCombatLogEntry(${attacker.name} critically missed!); this.scene.showFloatingText(target, 'MISS', 0xFFFFFF); return { hit: false, crit: false, damage: 0 }; }

if (!isHit && !isCrit) { console.log(  Miss! (${attackRoll} < ${target.evasion})); this.scene.addCombatLogEntry(${attacker.name} missed!); this.scene.showFloatingText(target, 'MISS', 0xFFFFFF); return { hit: false, crit: false, damage: 0 }; }

// 3. Roll damage
let damageResult = Dice.parseAndRoll(attacker.weapon.damage);
let totalDamage = damageResult.total;

// Critical hit: double dice (not modifiers) if (isCrit) { const critRoll = Dice.parseAndRoll(attacker.weapon.damage); totalDamage = damageResult.total + critRoll.total; console.log(  CRITICAL HIT! Damage: ${totalDamage}); this.scene.addCombatLogEntry(${attacker.name} CRITICAL HIT for ${totalDamage} damage!); } else { console.log(  Hit! Damage: ${totalDamage}); this.scene.addCombatLogEntry(${attacker.name} hit for ${totalDamage} damage!); }

// 4. Apply damage
this.applyDamage(target, totalDamage, isCrit);

return { hit: true, crit: isCrit, damage: totalDamage };
}

/**

Apply damage to target (Guard first, then HP)
@param {object} target - Target entity
@param {number} damage - Damage amount
@param {boolean} isCrit - Was this a critical hit? */ applyDamage(target, damage, isCrit = false) { let remainingDamage = damage;
// Damage Guard first
if (target.guard > 0) {
const guardDamage = Math.min(target.guard, remainingDamage);
target.guard -= guardDamage;
remainingDamage -= guardDamage;

console.log(`  ${guardDamage} absorbed by Guard (${target.guard}/${target.maxGuard} remaining)`);
}

// Remaining damage goes to HP if (remainingDamage > 0) { target.hp -= remainingDamage; console.log(  ${remainingDamage} damage to HP (${target.hp}/${target.maxHp} remaining)); }

// Check if dead if (target.hp <= 0) { target.hp = 0; target.alive = false; console.log(  ${target.name || 'Enemy'} has been defeated!); this.scene.addCombatLogEntry(${target.name || 'Enemy'} was defeated!);

// Trigger death
if (target.die) {
  target.die();
}
}

// Update visuals
if (target.updateHealthBar) {
target.updateHealthBar();
}

if (target.updateGuardBar) {
target.updateGuardBar();
}

// Show floating damage text const color = isCrit ? 0xFF0000 : 0xFFFFFF; this.scene.showFloatingText(target, -${damage}, color); }

### TASK 9.4: Add Floating Damage Text (1.5 hours)

**Step 1: Add showFloatingText to BootScene**
```javascript
/**
 * Show floating damage/message text
 * @param {object} target - Entity to show text above
 * @param {string} text - Text to display
 * @param {number} color - Hex color
 */
showFloatingText(target, text, color = 0xFFFFFF) {
  // Get screen position
  const x = target.sprite ? target.sprite.x : target.x;
  const y = target.sprite ? target.sprite.y : target.y;
  
  // Create text
  const floatingText = this.add.text(
    x,
    y - 50,
    text,
    {
      fontSize: '24px',
      color: `#${color.toString(16).padStart(6, '0')}`,
      fontFamily: 'Arial',
      fontStyle: 'bold',
      stroke: '#000000',
      strokeThickness: 4
    }
  ).setOrigin(0.5).setDepth(2000);
  
  // Animate upward and fade
  this.tweens.add({
    targets: floatingText,
    y: y - 100,
    alpha: 0,
    duration: 1000,
    ease: 'Power2',
    onComplete: () => {
      floatingText.destroy();
    }
  });
}
```

```javascript
  50,
  4,
  0x004D40
).setOrigin(0, 0.5).setDepth(95);

).setOrigin(0, 0.5).setDepth(96);

  const hpPercent = this.player.hp / this.player.maxHp;
  this.player.hpBarFg.width = 50 * hpPercent;
};

this.player.updateGuardBar = () => {
  const guardPercent = this.player.guard / this.player.maxGuard;
  this.player.guardBarFg.width = 50 * guardPercent;
};
```

**Step 3: Update bars on movement**

In `movePlayer()`, add to tween targets:
```javascript
this.tweens.add({
  targets: [
    this.player.sprite, 
    this.player.shadow,
    this.player.hpBarBg,
    this.player.hpBarFg,
    this.player.guardBarBg,
    this.player.guardBarFg
  ],
  x: (target) => {
    if (target === this.player.sprite) {
      return screenPos.x + this.gridOffsetX;
    } else if (target === this.player.shadow) {
      return screenPos.x + this.gridOffsetX;
    } else {
      // Bars
      return screenPos.x + this.gridOffsetX - 20;
    }
  },
  y: (target) => {
    if (target === this.player.sprite) {
      return screenPos.y + this.gridOffsetY;
    } else if (target === this.player.shadow) {
      return screenPos.y + this.gridOffsetY + 5;
    } else if (target === this.player.hpBarBg || target === this.player.hpBarFg) {
      return screenPos.y + this.gridOffsetY - 70;
    } else {
      return screenPos.y + this.gridOffsetY - 80;
    }
  },
  duration: 150,
  ease: 'Power2'
});
```

### TASK 10.1: Create Action Menu UI (2.5 hours)

**Step 1: Create UI folder and ActionMenu class**

`src/ui/ActionMenu.js`:
```javascript
/**
 * Action Menu
 * Combat action selection UI
 */
export default class ActionMenu {
  constructor(scene, x, y) {
    this.scene = scene;
    this.x = x;
    this.y = y;
    
    this.container = null;
    this.buttons = [];
    this.visible = false;
    this.onActionSelected = null; // Callback
    
    this.create();
  }

  create() {
    this.container = this.scene.add.container(this.x, this.y).setDepth(5000);
    this.container.setVisible(false);
    
    // Background panel
    const bg = this.scene.add.graphics();
    bg.fillStyle(0x1B5E20, 0.95);
    bg.lineStyle(3, 0x00C853, 1);
    bg.fillRoundedRect(0, 0, 250, 300, 10);
    bg.strokeRoundedRect(0, 0, 250, 300, 10);
    this.container.add(bg);
    
    // Title
    const title = this.scene.add.text(
      125, 20,
      'CHOOSE ACTION',
      {
        fontSize: '20px',
        color: '#00E5FF',
        fontFamily: 'Arial',
        fontStyle: 'bold'
      }
    ).setOrigin(0.5);
    this.container.add(title);
    
    // Actions
    const actions = [
      { key: 'attack', label: 'Attack', icon: '⚔️', ap: 1 },
      { key: 'defend', label: 'Defend', icon: '🛡️', ap: 1 },
      { key: 'item', label: 'Use Item', icon: '💊', ap: 1 },
      { key: 'wait', label: 'Wait', icon: '⏸️', ap: 0 }
    ];
    
    actions.forEach((action, index) => {
      this.createButton(action, 125, 70 + (index * 55));
    });
  }

  createButton(action, x, y) {
    const button = this.scene.add.container(x, y);
    
    // Button background
    const bg = this.scene.add.graphics();
    bg.fillStyle(0x004D40, 1);
    bg.lineStyle(2, 0x00C853, 1);
    bg.fillRoundedRect(-110, -20, 220, 45, 8);
    bg.strokeRoundedRect(-110, -20, 220, 45, 8);
    button.add(bg);
    
    // Icon
    const icon = this.scene.add.text(
      -90, 0,
      action.icon,
      { fontSize: '24px' }
    ).setOrigin(0, 0.5);
    button.add(icon);
    
    // Label
    const label = this.scene.add.text(
      -50, 0,
      action.label,
      {
        fontSize: '18px',
        color: '#E0F7FA',
        fontFamily: 'Arial'
      }
    ).setOrigin(0, 0.5);
    button.add(label);
    
    // AP cost
    const apCost = this.scene.add.text(
      100, 0,
      `${action.ap} AP`,
      {
        fontSize: '14px',
        color: '#00E5FF',
        fontFamily: 'monospace'
      }
    ).setOrigin(1, 0.5);
    button.add(apCost);
    
    // Make interactive
    const hitArea = new Phaser.Geom.Rectangle(-110, -20, 220, 45);
    bg.setInteractive(hitArea, Phaser.Geom.Rectangle.Contains);
    
    // Hover effects
    bg.on('pointerover', () => {
      bg.clear();
      bg.fillStyle(0x00695C, 1);
      bg.lineStyle(2, 0x00E5FF, 1);
      bg.fillRoundedRect(-110, -20, 220, 45, 8);
      bg.strokeRoundedRect(-110, -20, 220, 45, 8);
      this.scene.sound.play('move', { volume: 0.2 });
    });
    
    bg.on('pointerout', () => {
      bg.clear();
      bg.fillStyle(0x004D40, 1);
      bg.lineStyle(2, 0x00C853, 1);
      bg.fillRoundedRect(-110, -20, 220, 45, 8);
      bg.strokeRoundedRect(-110, -20, 220, 45, 8);
    });
    
    // Click handler
    bg.on('pointerdown', () => {
      this.scene.sound.play('hit', { volume: 0.3 });
      this.selectAction(action.key);
    });
    
    this.container.add(button);
    this.buttons.push({ button, action });
  }

  show(callback) {
    this.onActionSelected = callback;
    this.container.setVisible(true);
    this.visible = true;
    
    // Animate in
    this.container.setAlpha(0);
    this.container.setScale(0.8);
    this.scene.tweens.add({
      targets: this.container,
      alpha: 1,
      scale: 1,
      duration: 200,
      ease: 'Back.easeOut'
    });
  }

  hide() {
    this.scene.tweens.add({
      targets: this.container,
      alpha: 0,
      scale: 0.8,
      duration: 150,
      ease: 'Power2',
      onComplete: () => {
        this.container.setVisible(false);
        this.visible = false;
      }
    });
  }

  selectAction(actionKey) {
    console.log(`Action selected: ${actionKey}`);
    
    // Call callback
    if (this.onActionSelected) {
      this.onActionSelected(actionKey);
    }
    
    this.hide();
  }

  destroy() {
    this.container.destroy();
  }
}
```

```javascript
startPlayerCombatTurn() {

    this.handlePlayerAction(actionKey);
  });

  this.updateTurnDisplay();
```

**Step 4: Handle action selection**
```javascript
handlePlayerAction(actionKey) {
  console.log(`Player chose: ${actionKey}`);
  
  switch(actionKey) {
    case 'attack':
      this.startTargetSelection('attack');
      break;
      
    case 'defend':
      this.playerDefend();
      break;
      
    case 'item':
      this.addCombatLogEntry('Items not yet implemented');
      this.combatManager.endTurn();
      break;
      
    case 'wait':
      this.addCombatLogEntry('Player waits...');
      this.combatManager.endTurn();
      break;
      
    default:
      console.warn(`Unknown action: ${actionKey}`);
  }
}

playerDefend() {
  this.addCombatLogEntry('Player takes defensive stance!');
  
  // Restore Guard
  this.player.guard = Math.min(
    this.player.guard + 4,
    this.player.maxGuard
  );
  this.player.updateGuardBar();
  
  // Visual feedback
  this.showFloatingText(this.player, '+4 Guard', 0x00C853);
  
  // TODO: Apply +3 Evasion buff until next turn
  
  // End turn
  this.combatManager.endTurn();
}
```

### TASK 10.2: Target Selection System (3 hours)

**Step 1: Add targeting state**

In BootScene:
```javascript
// Add to create():
this.targetingMode = false;
this.targetingAction = null; // 'attack', 'spell', etc.
this.targetableEnemies = [];
this.selectedTarget = null;

// Visual indicators
this.targetIndicators = [];
```

**Step 2: Create startTargetSelection**
```javascript
startTargetSelection(actionType) {
  console.log(`Starting target selection for: ${actionType}`);
  
  this.targetingMode = true;
  this.targetingAction = actionType;
  
  // Get valid targets (living enemies)
  this.targetableEnemies = this.enemies.filter(e => e.alive);
  
  if (this.targetableEnemies.length === 0) {
    console.log('No valid targets!');
    this.combatManager.endTurn();
    return;
  }
  
  // Show target indicators
  this.showTargetIndicators();
  
  // Add instruction
  this.targetInstructionText = this.add.text(
    640, 650,
    'Click enemy to target (ESC to cancel)',
    {
      fontSize: '18px',
      color: '#00E5FF',
      backgroundColor: '#1B5E20',
      padding: { x: 20, y: 10 }
    }
  ).setOrigin(0.5).setDepth(1000);
}

showTargetIndicators() {
  // Clear old indicators
  this.targetIndicators.forEach(indicator => indicator.destroy());
  this.targetIndicators = [];
  
  // Create indicator for each targetable enemy
  this.targetableEnemies.forEach(enemy => {
    // Pulsing circle
    const indicator = this.add.circle(
      enemy.sprite.x,
      enemy.sprite.y,
      40,
      0xFF0000,
      0.3
    ).setDepth(85);
    
    // Pulse animation
    this.tweens.add({
      targets: indicator,
      alpha: 0.6,
      scale: 1.2,
      duration: 500,
      yoyo: true,
      repeat: -1
    });
    
    // Make enemy sprite interactive
    enemy.sprite.setInteractive();
    
    enemy.sprite.on('pointerover', () => {
      indicator.setFillStyle(0xFFFF00, 0.5); // Yellow on hover
      enemy.sprite.setTint(0xFFFF00);
    });
    
    enemy.sprite.on('pointerout', () => {
      indicator.setFillStyle(0xFF0000, 0.3); // Red default
      enemy.sprite.clearTint();
    });
    
    enemy.sprite.on('pointerdown', () => {
      this.selectTarget(enemy);
    });
    
    this.targetIndicators.push(indicator);
  });
}

selectTarget(enemy) {
  console.log(`Target selected: ${enemy.name}`);
  
  // Clear targeting mode
  this.clearTargeting();
  
  // Execute action on target
  if (this.targetingAction === 'attack') {
    this.player.attackTarget(enemy);
  }
  
  // TODO: Handle other action types (spells, items)
}

clearTargeting() {
  this.targetingMode = false;
  this.targetingAction = null;
  
  // Clear indicators
  this.targetIndicators.forEach(indicator => indicator.destroy());
  this.targetIndicators = [];
  
  // Remove enemy interactivity
  this.targetableEnemies.forEach(enemy => {
    enemy.sprite.disableInteractive();
    enemy.sprite.clearTint();
  });
  
  this.targetableEnemies = [];
  
  // Clear instruction
  if (this.targetInstructionText) {
    this.targetInstructionText.destroy();
    this.targetInstructionText = null;
  }
}
```

**Step 3: Add ESC cancel**

In `create()`:
```javascript
// ESC key to cancel targeting
this.input.keyboard.on('keydown-ESC', () => {
  if (this.targetingMode) {
    this.addCombatLogEntry('Action cancelled');
    this.clearTargeting();
    this.actionMenu.show((actionKey) => {
      this.handlePlayerAction(actionKey);
    });
  }
});
```

Update action costs:
```javascript
handlePlayerAction(actionKey) {
  const apCosts = {
    attack: 1,
    defend: 1,
    item: 1,
    wait: 0
  };
  
  const cost = apCosts[actionKey] || 0;
  
  // Check if enough AP
  if (this.player.ap < cost) {
    this.addCombatLogEntry('Not enough AP!');
    this.actionMenu.show((actionKey) => {
      this.handlePlayerAction(actionKey);
    });
    return;
  }
  
  // Deduct AP
  this.player.ap -= cost;
  this.player.apText.setText(`AP: ${this.player.ap}/${this.player.maxAP}`);
  
  // ... rest of switch statement ...
  
  // If AP remaining, show menu again
  if (this.player.ap > 0 && actionKey !== 'wait') {
    this.time.delayedCall(800, () => {
      if (!this.targetingMode) {
        this.actionMenu.show((actionKey) => {
          this.handlePlayerAction(actionKey);
        });
      }
    });
  } else {
    // No AP left, end turn
    this.time.delayedCall(800, () => {
      this.combatManager.endTurn();
    });
  }
}
```

Restore AP at start of turn:
```javascript
startPlayerCombatTurn() {
  // Restore AP
  this.player.ap = this.player.maxAP;
  this.player.apText.setText(`AP: ${this.player.ap}/${this.player.maxAP}`);
  
  // ... rest of function ...
}
```

```javascript
    targets: continueText,
    alpha: 0.5,
    duration: 500,
    yoyo: true,
    repeat: -1
  });
  
  // Click to reset
  this.input.once('pointerdown', () => {
    this.scene.restart();
  });
```

### TASK 11.1: Create Save System (3 hours)

**Step 1: Create SaveManager**
```bash
touch src/systems/SaveManager.js
```

`src/systems/SaveManager.js`:
```javascript
/**
 * Save/Load Manager
 * Handles game state persistence
 */
export default class SaveManager {
  constructor(scene) {
    this.scene = scene;
    this.saveKey = 'verdance_save';
  }

  /**
   * Capture current game state
   */
  captureState() {
    const state = {
      version: '0.1.0',
      timestamp: Date.now(),
      
      // Player data
      player: {
        gridX: this.scene.player.gridX,
        gridY: this.scene.player.gridY,
        hp: this.scene.player.hp,
        maxHp: this.scene.player.maxHp,
        guard: this.scene.player.guard,
        maxGuard: this.scene.player.maxGuard,
        might: this.scene.player.might,
        agility: this.scene.player.agility,
        resilience: this.scene.player.resilience,
        insight: this.scene.player.insight,
        charisma: this.scene.player.charisma
      },
      
      // Combat state
      combat: {
        inCombat: this.scene.combatManager?.inCombat || false,
        roundNumber: this.scene.combatManager?.roundNumber || 0
      },
      
      // Enemies
      enemies: this.scene.enemies.map(enemy => ({
        gridX: enemy.gridX,
        gridY: enemy.gridY,
        type: enemy.type,
        hp: enemy.hp,
        maxHp: enemy.maxHp,
        guard: enemy.guard,
        alive: enemy.alive
      })),
      
      // World state
      world: {
        dsp: 100, // TODO: Implement DSP system
        sapPhase: 'blue', // TODO: Implement Sap Cycle
        gameDay: 1
      }
    };
    
    return state;
  }

  /**
   * Save game state to localStorage
   */
  save(slotNumber = 1) {
    try {
      const state = this.captureState();
      const key = `${this.saveKey}_slot${slotNumber}`;
      
      localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(state));
      
      console.log(`Game saved to slot ${slotNumber}`);
      this.scene.addCombatLogEntry(`Game saved!`);
      
      return true;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Save failed:', error);
      return false;
    }
  }

  /**
   * Load game state from localStorage
   */
  load(slotNumber = 1) {
    try {
      const key = `${this.saveKey}_slot${slotNumber}`;
      const savedData = localStorage.getItem(key);
      
      if (!savedData) {
        console.log(`No save found in slot ${slotNumber}`);
        return null;
      }
      
      const state = JSON.parse(savedData);
      console.log(`Game loaded from slot ${slotNumber}`);
      
      return state;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Load failed:', error);
      return null;
    }
  }

  /**
   * Restore game state
   */
  restoreState(state) {
    if (!state) return false;
    
    try {
      // Restore player
      this.scene.player.gridX = state.player.gridX;
      this.scene.player.gridY = state.player.gridY;
      this.scene.player.hp = state.player.hp;
      this.scene.player.maxHp = state.player.maxHp;
      this.scene.player.guard = state.player.guard;
      this.scene.player.maxGuard = state.player.maxGuard;
      
      // Update player visual position
      const playerPos = this.scene.grid.gridToScreen(
        state.player.gridX,
        state.player.gridY
      );
      this.scene.player.sprite.setPosition(
        playerPos.x + this.scene.gridOffsetX,
        playerPos.y + this.scene.gridOffsetY
      );
      
      // Update health bars
      this.scene.player.updateHealthBar();
      this.scene.player.updateGuardBar();
      
      // Restore enemies
      // Clear existing
      this.scene.enemies.forEach(e => e.destroy());
      this.scene.enemies = [];
      
      // Recreate from save
      state.enemies.forEach(enemyData => {
        const enemy = new this.scene.Enemy(
          this.scene,
          enemyData.gridX,
          enemyData.gridY,
          enemyData.type
        );
        enemy.hp = enemyData.hp;
        enemy.guard = enemyData.guard;
        enemy.alive = enemyData.alive;
        enemy.updateHealthBar();
        
        if (!enemy.alive) {
          enemy.die();
        }
        
        this.scene.enemies.push(enemy);
      });
      
      console.log('State restored successfully');
      this.scene.addCombatLogEntry('Game loaded!');
      
      return true;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Restore failed:', error);
      return false;
    }
  }

  /**
   * Check if save exists
   */
  hasSave(slotNumber = 1) {
    const key = `${this.saveKey}_slot${slotNumber}`;
    return localStorage.getItem(key) !== null;
  }

  /**
   * Delete save
   */
  deleteSave(slotNumber = 1) {
    const key = `${this.saveKey}_slot${slotNumber}`;
    localStorage.removeItem(key);
    console.log(`Save slot ${slotNumber} deleted`);
  }

  /**
   * Get save info (without loading)
   */
  getSaveInfo(slotNumber = 1) {
    const key = `${this.saveKey}_slot${slotNumber}`;
    const savedData = localStorage.getItem(key);
    
    if (!savedData) return null;
    
    try {
      const state = JSON.parse(savedData);
      return {
        timestamp: state.timestamp,
        playerLevel: 1, // TODO: Implement levels
        location: 'Canopy of Life',
        playtime: '0h 15m' // TODO: Track playtime
      };
    } catch (error) {
      return null;
    }
  }
}
```

**✅ Success Check:**
- [ ] SaveManager.js created
- [ ] No syntax errors
- [ ] Class exports correctly

```javascript
  this.saveManager.save(1);
  this.showNotification('Game Saved', 0x00C853);
});

// F9 = Quick Load
this.input.keyboard.on('keydown-F9', () => {
  const state = this.saveManager.load(1);
  if (state) {
    this.saveManager.restoreState(state);
    this.showNotification('Game Loaded', 0x00E5FF);
  } else {
    this.showNotification('No Save Found', 0xFF0000);
  }
});
```

**Step 3: Add notification system**
```javascript
showNotification(text, color = 0x00C853) {
  // Create notification
  const notification = this.add.text(
    640, 100,
    text,
    {
      fontSize: '24px',
      color: `#${color.toString(16).padStart(6, '0')}`,
      backgroundColor: '#1B5E20',
      padding: { x: 20, y: 10 },
      fontFamily: 'Arial'
    }
  ).setOrigin(0.5).setDepth(9999).setAlpha(0);
  
  // Animate in
  this.tweens.add({
    targets: notification,
    alpha: 1,
    y: 120,
    duration: 300,
    ease: 'Back.easeOut'
  });
  
  // Animate out and destroy
  this.time.delayedCall(2000, () => {
    this.tweens.add({
      targets: notification,
      alpha: 0,
      y: 100,
      duration: 300,
      ease: 'Power2',
      onComplete: () => {
        notification.destroy();
      }
    });
  });
}
```

```javascript
  // Auto-save after victory

    this.saveManager.save(1);
  });
}
```

### TASK 11.3: Create Save/Load Menu UI (2.5 hours)

**Step 1: Create SaveMenu class**
```bash
touch src/ui/SaveMenu.js
```

`src/ui/SaveMenu.js`:
```javascript
/**
 * Save/Load Menu UI
 */
export default class SaveMenu {
  constructor(scene) {
    this.scene = scene;
    this.container = null;
    this.mode = null; // 'save' or 'load'
    this.visible = false;
    
    this.create();
  }

  create() {
    this.container = this.scene.add.container(640, 360).setDepth(8000);
    this.container.setVisible(false);
    
    // Background overlay
    const overlay = this.scene.add.graphics();
    overlay.fillStyle(0x000000, 0.7);
    overlay.fillRect(-640, -360, 1280, 720);
    this.container.add(overlay);
    
    // Main panel
    const panel = this.scene.add.graphics();
    panel.fillStyle(0x1B5E20, 0.95);
    panel.lineStyle(4, 0x00C853, 1);
    panel.fillRoundedRect(-300, -250, 600, 500, 15);
    panel.strokeRoundedRect(-300, -250, 600, 500, 15);
    this.container.add(panel);
    
    // Title (will be set dynamically)
    this.title = this.scene.add.text(
      0, -220,
      '',
      {
        fontSize: '32px',
        color: '#00E5FF',
        fontFamily: 'Arial',
        fontStyle: 'bold'
      }
    ).setOrigin(0.5);
    this.container.add(this.title);
    
    // Save slots
    this.createSaveSlots();
    
    // Close button
    this.createCloseButton();
  }

  createSaveSlots() {
    this.slotContainers = [];
    
    for (let i = 1; i <= 3; i++) {
      const slotContainer = this.createSlot(i, 0, -140 + (i - 1) * 150);
      this.container.add(slotContainer);
      this.slotContainers.push(slotContainer);
    }
  }

  createSlot(slotNumber, x, y) {
    const slotContainer = this.scene.add.container(x, y);
    
    // Slot background
    const bg = this.scene.add.graphics();
    bg.fillStyle(0x004D40, 1);
    bg.lineStyle(2, 0x00C853, 1);
    bg.fillRoundedRect(-280, -60, 560, 120, 10);
    bg.strokeRoundedRect(-280, -60, 560, 120, 10);
    slotContainer.add(bg);
    
    // Slot label
    const label = this.scene.add.text(
      -260, -40,
      `Slot ${slotNumber}`,
      {
        fontSize: '20px',
        color: '#00E5FF',
        fontFamily: 'Arial',
        fontStyle: 'bold'
      }
    );
    slotContainer.add(label);
    
    // Save info (will update dynamically)
    const info = this.scene.add.text(
      -260, -10,
      'Empty',
      {
        fontSize: '16px',
        color: '#E0F7FA',
        fontFamily: 'Arial'
      }
    );
    slotContainer.add(info);
    slotContainer.infoText = info;
    
    // Make interactive
    const hitArea = new Phaser.Geom.Rectangle(-280, -60, 560, 120);
    bg.setInteractive(hitArea, Phaser.Geom.Rectangle.Contains);
    
    // Hover
    bg.on('pointerover', () => {
      bg.clear();
      bg.fillStyle(0x00695C, 1);
      bg.lineStyle(3, 0x00E5FF, 1);
      bg.fillRoundedRect(-280, -60, 560, 120, 10);
      bg.strokeRoundedRect(-280, -60, 560, 120, 10);
    });
    
    bg.on('pointerout', () => {
      bg.clear();
      bg.fillStyle(0x004D40, 1);
      bg.lineStyle(2, 0x00C853, 1);
      bg.fillRoundedRect(-280, -60, 560, 120, 10);
      bg.strokeRoundedRect(-280, -60, 560, 120, 10);
    });
    
    // Click
    bg.on('pointerdown', () => {
      this.selectSlot(slotNumber);
    });
    
    slotContainer.slotNumber = slotNumber;
    
    return slotContainer;
  }

  createCloseButton() {
    const closeButton = this.scene.add.text(
      0, 220,
      'Close (ESC)',
      {
        fontSize: '18px',
        color: '#E0F7FA',
        backgroundColor: '#004D40',
        padding: { x: 20, y: 10 },
        fontFamily: 'Arial'
      }
    ).setOrigin(0.5).setInteractive();
    
    closeButton.on('pointerover', () => {
      closeButton.setBackgroundColor('#00695C');
    });
    
    closeButton.on('pointerout', () => {
      closeButton.setBackgroundColor('#004D40');
    });
    
    closeButton.on('pointerdown', () => {
      this.hide();
    });
    
    this.container.add(closeButton);
  }

  show(mode) {
    this.mode = mode; // 'save' or 'load'
    this.title.setText(mode === 'save' ? 'SAVE GAME' : 'LOAD GAME');
    
    // Update slot info
    this.updateSlotInfo();
    
    this.container.setVisible(true);
    this.visible = true;
    
    // Animate in
    this.container.setAlpha(0);
    this.scene.tweens.add({
      targets: this.container,
      alpha: 1,
      duration: 200
    });
  }

  hide() {
    this.scene.tweens.add({
      targets: this.container,
      alpha: 0,
      duration: 150,
      onComplete: () => {
        this.container.setVisible(false);
        this.visible = false;
      }
    });
  }

  updateSlotInfo() {
    this.slotContainers.forEach(slotContainer => {
      const slotNumber = slotContainer.slotNumber;
      const saveInfo = this.scene.saveManager.getSaveInfo(slotNumber);
      
      if (saveInfo) {
        const date = new Date(saveInfo.timestamp);
        const dateStr = date.toLocaleString();
        slotContainer.infoText.setText(
          `${saveInfo.location}\n${dateStr}`
        );
      } else {
        slotContainer.infoText.setText('Empty');
      }
    });
  }

  selectSlot(slotNumber) {
    console.log(`Slot ${slotNumber} selected (${this.mode})`);
    
    if (this.mode === 'save') {
      // Confirm overwrite if save exists
      if (this.scene.saveManager.hasSave(slotNumber)) {
        // TODO: Add confirmation dialog
        console.log('Overwriting save...');
      }
      
      this.scene.saveManager.save(slotNumber);
      this.scene.showNotification(`Saved to Slot ${slotNumber}`, 0x00C853);
      this.updateSlotInfo();
    } else if (this.mode === 'load') {
      const state = this.scene.saveManager.load(slotNumber);
      if (state) {
        this.scene.saveManager.restoreState(state);
        this.scene.showNotification(`Loaded Slot ${slotNumber}`, 0x00E5FF);
        this.hide();
      } else {
        this.scene.showNotification('No Save Found', 0xFF0000);
      }
    }
  }

  destroy() {
    this.container.destroy();
  }
}
```

**Step 2: Add to BootScene**
```javascript
import SaveMenu from '../ui/SaveMenu.js';

// In create():
this.saveMenu = new SaveMenu(this);

// Add menu triggers (ESC key menu)
this.input.keyboard.on('keydown-ESC', () => {
  if (!this.saveMenu.visible && !this.targetingMode) {
    // Show quick menu
    this.showQuickMenu();
  } else if (this.saveMenu.visible) {
    this.saveMenu.hide();
  }
});

showQuickMenu() {
  // Pause game
  this.scene.pause();
  
  // Create simple menu
  const menuBg = this.add.graphics();
  menuBg.fillStyle(0x000000, 0.8);
  menuBg.fillRect(0, 0, 1280, 720);
  menuBg.setDepth(7000);
  
  const menuContainer = this.add.container(640, 360).setDepth(7001);
  
  const title = this.add.text(0, -150, 'PAUSED', {
    fontSize: '48px',
    color: '#00E5FF',
    fontFamily: 'Arial',
    fontStyle: 'bold'
  }).setOrigin(0.5);
  menuContainer.add(title);
  
  // Menu options
  const options = [
    { text: 'Resume', action: () => this.resumeGame(menuBg, menuContainer) },
    { text: 'Save Game', action: () => {
      this.saveMenu.show('save');
      menuBg.destroy();
      menuContainer.destroy();
    }},
    { text: 'Load Game', action: () => {
      this.saveMenu.show('load');
      menuBg.destroy();
      menuContainer.destroy();
    }},
    { text: 'Restart', action: () => this.scene.restart() }
  ];
  
  options.forEach((option, index) => {
    const button = this.add.text(
      0, -50 + (index * 60),
      option.text,
      {
        fontSize: '24px',
        color: '#E0F7FA',
        backgroundColor: '#004D40',
        padding: { x: 30, y: 12 },
        fontFamily: 'Arial'
      }
    ).setOrigin(0.5).setInteractive();
    
    button.on('pointerover', () => button.setBackgroundColor('#00695C'));
    button.on('pointerout', () => button.setBackgroundColor('#004D40'));
    button.on('pointerdown', option.action);
    
    menuContainer.add(button);
  });
}

resumeGame(menuBg, menuContainer) {
  menuBg.destroy();
  menuContainer.destroy();
  this.scene.resume();
}
```

**✅ Success Check:**
- [ ] ESC opens pause menu
- [ ] Pause menu has 4 options
- [ ] Save Game opens save menu
- [ ] Load Game opens load menu
- [ ] Slots show save info
- [ ] Clicking slot saves/loads
- [ ] Resume works
- [ ] Restart works

### TASK 12.1: Combat Animations (2.5 hours)

**Step 1: Add camera shake on hit**

```javascript
// Add to performAttack result handling (in CombatManager or after attack):
```

**Step 2: Improve attack animation**

Replace simple shake in `player.attackTarget`:
```javascript
this.player.attackTarget = (target) => {
  // Move toward target
  const targetPos = {
    x: target.sprite.x,
    y: target.sprite.y
  };
  
  const playerPos = {
    x: this.player.sprite.x,
    y: this.player.sprite.y
  };
  
  // Calculate direction
  const angle = Phaser.Math.Angle.Between(
    playerPos.x, playerPos.y,
    targetPos.x, targetPos.y
  );
  
  const lunge Distance = 30;
  const lungeX = playerPos.x + Math.cos(angle) * lungeDistance;
  const lungeY = playerPos.y + Math.sin(angle) * lungeDistance;
  
  // Lunge forward
  this.tweens.add({
    targets: [this.player.sprite, this.player.shadow, this.player.hpBarBg, this.player.hpBarFg, this.player.guardBarBg, this.player.guardBarFg],
    x: (sprite) => {
      if (sprite === this.player.sprite || sprite === this.player.shadow) {
        return lungeX;
      } else {
        return lungeX - 20;
      }
    },
    y: (sprite) => {
      if (sprite === this.player.sprite) return lungeY;
      if (sprite === this.player.shadow) return lungeY + 5;
      if (sprite === this.player.hpBarBg || sprite === this.player.hpBarFg) return lungeY - 70;
      return lungeY - 80;
    },
    duration: 150,
    ease: 'Power2',
    yoyo: true,
    onStart: () => {
      this.sound.play('hit', { volume: 0.6 });
    },
    onYoyo: () => {
      // Perform attack at apex of lunge
      const result = this.combatManager.performAttack(this.player, target);
      
      if (result.hit) {
        this.cameras.main.shake(200, result.crit ? 0.01 : 0.005);
      }
    },
    onComplete: () => {
      // End turn
      this.time.delayedCall(400, () => {
        this.combatManager.endTurn();
      });
    }
  });
};
```

**Step 3: Add hit particles**

In `applyDamage` (CombatManager):
```javascript
// After showing floating text:
this.scene.createHitEffect(target, isCrit);
```

Add to BootScene:
```javascript
createHitEffect(target, isCrit = false) {
  const x = target.sprite ? target.sprite.x : target.x;
  const y = target.sprite ? target.sprite.y - 20 : target.y - 20;
  
  // Blood/hit particles (red for crit, white for normal)
  const particles = this.add.particles(x, y, 'player_placeholder', {
    speed: { min: 50, max: 150 },
    angle: { min: 0, max: 360 },
    scale: { start: isCrit ? 1 : 0.5, end: 0 },
    alpha: { start: 1, end: 0 },
    tint: isCrit ? 0xFF0000 : 0xFFFFFF,
    lifespan: isCrit ? 600 : 400,
    quantity: isCrit ? 20 : 10,
    blendMode: 'ADD',
    gravityY: 200
  });
  
  // Auto-destroy after emission
  this.time.delayedCall(1000, () => {
    particles.destroy();
  });
}
```
