### TASK 12.2: UI Polish (2 hours)

**Step 1: Add health bar animations**

Update `updateHealthBar` and `updateGuardBar`:
```javascript
// In player and Enemy classes:
updateHealthBar() {
  const hpPercent = this.hp / this.maxHp;
  const targetWidth = (this.isPlayer ? 50 : 32) * hpPercent;
  
  // Animate instead of instant
  this.scene.tweens.add({
    targets: this.hpBarFg,
    width: targetWidth,
    duration: 300,
    ease: 'Power2'
  });
  
  // Flash if low HP (<30%)
  if (hpPercent < 0.3 && hpPercent > 0) {
    this.scene.tweens.add({
      targets: this.hpBarFg,
      alpha: 0.5,
      duration: 300,
      yoyo: true,
      repeat: 2
    });
  }
}

updateGuardBar() {
  const guardPercent = this.guard / this.maxGuard;
  const targetWidth = (this.isPlayer ? 50 : 32) * guardPercent;
  
  this.scene.tweens.add({
    targets: this.guardBarFg,
    width: targetWidth,
    duration: 300,
    ease: 'Power2'
  });
}
```

```javascript
showTurnIndicator(entity) {
  const name = entity.name || 'Enemy';
  const color = entity.isPlayer ? 0x00E5FF : 0xFF6B6B;
  
  // Large turn banner
  const banner = this.add.text(
    640, 360,
    `${name}'s Turn`,
    {
      fontSize: '48px',
      color: `#${color.toString(16).padStart(6, '0')}`,
      fontFamily: 'Arial',
      fontStyle: 'bold',
      stroke: '#000000',
      strokeThickness: 6
    }
  ).setOrigin(0.5).setDepth(9000).setAlpha(0).setScale(0.5);
  
  // Animate in and out
  this.tweens.add({
    targets: banner,
    alpha: 1,
    scale: 1,
    duration: 300,
    ease: 'Back.easeOut'
  });
  
  this.time.delayedCall(1000, () => {
    this.tweens.add({
      targets: banner,
      alpha: 0,
      scale: 1.5,
      duration: 300,
      ease: 'Power2',
      onComplete: () => banner.destroy()
    });
  });
}
```

### TASK 12.4: Performance Optimization (1.5 hours)

**Step 1: Object pooling for floating text**

Create text pool:
```javascript
// In create():
this.floatingTextPool = [];
this.maxPoolSize = 20;
```

Update `showFloatingText`:
```javascript
showFloatingText(target, text, color = 0xFFFFFF) {
  // Try to reuse from pool
  let floatingText = this.floatingTextPool.pop();
  
  if (!floatingText) {
    // Create new if pool empty
    floatingText = this.add.text(0, 0, '', {
      fontSize: '24px',
      fontFamily: 'Arial',
      fontStyle: 'bold',
      stroke: '#000000',
      strokeThickness: 4
    }).setOrigin(0.5).setDepth(2000);
  }
  
  // Set properties
  const x = target.sprite ? target.sprite.x : target.x;
  const y = target.sprite ? target.sprite.y : target.y;
  
  floatingText.setPosition(x, y - 50);
  floatingText.setText(text);
  floatingText.setColor(`#${color.toString(16).padStart(6, '0')}`);
  floatingText.setAlpha(1);
  floatingText.setVisible(true);
  
  // Animate
  this.tweens.add({
    targets: floatingText,
    y: y - 100,
    alpha: 0,
    duration: 1000,
    ease: 'Power2',
    onComplete: () => {
      floatingText.setVisible(false);
      // Return to pool
      if (this.floatingTextPool.length < this.maxPoolSize) {
        this.floatingTextPool.push(floatingText);
      } else {
        floatingText.destroy();
      }
    }
  });
}
```

**Step 2: Reduce particle count on lower-end devices**
```javascript
// In create(), detect performance tier:
this.performanceTier = this.detectPerformance();

detectPerformance() {
  // Simple heuristic: check FPS after 1 second
  this.time.delayedCall(1000, () => {
    const fps = this.game.loop.actualFps;
    if (fps > 55) {
      this.performanceTier = 'high';
    } else if (fps > 45) {
      this.performanceTier = 'medium';
    } else {
      this.performanceTier = 'low';
    }
    console.log(`Performance tier: ${this.performanceTier}`);
  });
  
  return 'high'; // Default assumption
}

// In createHitEffect():
const quantity = isCrit ? 
  (this.performanceTier === 'low' ? 10 : 20) :
  (this.performanceTier === 'low' ? 5 : 10);
```

```javascript
      this.endTurn();
    });
    return;
  }
  
  // ... existing AI logic ...
}
```
